# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Interpretable Computer Vision for Defect Detection in X-ray Tomography of Aerospace SiC/SiC Composites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20159)
*Antonio Peña Corredor,Julien Lesseur,Romain Nunez,Paul Rivalland,Thomas Philippe*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出p-ResNet-50，一种在卷积网络中集成原型层（prototype layer）的框架，用于SiC/SiC复合材料的X射线计算机断层扫描（XCT）无损检测。该方法在保持与黑盒ResNet-50相当的高检测性能（ROC-AUC约0.99）的同时，提供基于案例的可解释决策，并显式标记不确定性区域。六个原型对应于专家定义的语义缺陷类别，两项新颖的正则化项（anchor-based与medoid-based）防止原型坍塌。该框架建立了将领域专家知识嵌入原型网络的可复用方法论，适用于需要可追溯、可审计决策的XCT检测场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 航空航天SiC/SiC复合材料的XCT无损检测当前依赖专家视觉评估，工作流程中可追溯性有限（limited traceability）。深度卷积网络可以自动化缺陷检测，但其黑箱属性（black-box nature）与工业检测实践所需透明性（transparency）之间存在冲突。

Method: 提出p-ResNet-50框架，在ResNet-50基础上扩展一个原型层（prototype layer）。六个学习到的原型明确对齐专家定义的语义类别（healthy matrix, matrix–air interfaces, pores, line-like defects, mixed morphologies）。引入两种新颖正则化项——锚点正则化（anchor-based）和类中心正则化（medoid-based），将原型锚定到专家选择的图像块（patches）并防止原型坍塌（prototype collapse）。使用UMAP进行潜在空间分析（latent-space analysis）来描绘语义相干子域与不确定性区域。

Result: 在约12,000个图像块的XCT数据集上验证。以黑盒ResNet-50为基线（ROC-AUC=0.991），原型扩展方法达到可比性能（准确率0.957 vs. 0.959；ROC-AUC 0.994 vs. 0.993），以轻微的灵敏度（sensitivity）降低换取了更高的精确率（precision）和特异性（specificity）。每个决策均由代表性证据图像块支持，模型显式标记其不确定性区域。

Conclusion: p-ResNet-50弥合了高精度缺陷检测与可解释性（interpretability）之间的差距，为工业XCT检测提供了可追溯、可审计的决策支持。该框架建立了一种可复用的方法论，用于将领域专家知识嵌入原型网络，并可推广至其他需要透明决策的XCT检测场景。

Abstract: Non-destructive testing of aerospace SiC/SiC composites via X-ray computed tomography (XCT) relies on expert visual assessment, with current workflows offering limited traceability for accept/reject decisions. Deep convolutional networks can automate defect detection, yet their black-box nature conflicts with the transparency that industrial inspection practice demands. To close this gap, we introduce p-ResNet-50, a convolutional framework extended with a prototype layer that couples high detection accuracy with case-based explanations. Six learned prototypes are explicitly aligned with expert-defined semantic categories-healthy matrix, matrix--air interfaces, pores, line-like defects, and mixed morphologies-so that every classification is traceable to a physically meaningful reference. Two novel regularisation terms, anchor-based and medoid-based, tether prototypes to expert-selected patches and prevent prototype collapse, addressing a known limitation of prototype networks. Latent-space analysis via UMAP delineates semantically coherent sub-domains and maps zones of uncertainty where misclassifications concentrate, giving inspectors an explicit picture of where the model is-and is not-reliable. The framework is validated on an XCT patch dataset of approximately 12,000 patches extracted from four defect-rich SiC/SiC laboratory specimens. Taking a black-box ResNet-50 as a baseline (ROC-AUC = 0.991), the prototype extension achieves comparable performance (accuracy 0.957 vs. 0.959; ROC-AUC 0.994 vs. 0.993) while trading a slight reduction in sensitivity for higher precision and specificity. Each decision is backed by representative evidence patches, and the model explicitly flags its uncertainty regions. Beyond defect mapping, the framework establishes a reusable methodology for embedding domain-expert knowledge into prototype networks, applicable to other XCT inspection scenarios requiring traceable, auditable decisions.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.dis-nn'></div>

# cond-mat.dis-nn [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Banded non-Hermitian random matrices, neural networks, and eigenvalue degeneracies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19072)
*Richard Huang,David R. Nelson*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究受稀疏神经网络启发的双能带非厄米随机矩阵，重点分析SSH链和梯子模型中随机符号无序与方向性偏置的竞争，揭示了复平面上扩展态环与局域态区域的丰富能谱结构，以及两种模型不同的退局域化现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多聚焦于单能带系统，而双能带非厄米随机矩阵中无序与方向性偏置的相互作用及其导致的退局域化行为尚未被充分理解。本文旨在通过SSH链和梯子模型这两种范式的对比，揭示不同能带结构带来的退局域化现象差异。

Method: 采用两种非厄米随机矩阵模型——SSH链（Su-Schrieffer-Heeger chain）和梯子模型（ladder model），两者均包含非厄米方向性偏置（directional bias）和服从戴尔法则（Dale's Law）的随机符号无序（random sign disorder）。通过数值对角化（numerical diagonalization）计算本征态和本征能谱，并利用随机转移矩阵（random transfer matrices）的乘积的Lyapunov指数（Lyapunov exponents）预测扩展态所在等值线。

Result: 随机符号无序导致本征态局域化，而方向性偏置驱动退局域化转变。两模型能谱均被限制在环形区域内，复平面上呈现被局域态区域包围的扩展态环。在无无序时，方向性偏置可导致本征值简并：SSH链为例外点（exceptional point），梯子模型为魔鬼点（diabolic point）。在无序存在下，这些简并点仍被保留并标示退局域化的关键阶段。增加方向性偏置时，SSH链中扩展态在复平面能谱上打开一个空洞；梯子模型则分两阶段退局域化，形成两个分离的扩展态环，中间夹有局域态区域。Lyapunov指数的理论预测与数值对角化结果一致。

Conclusion: 无序与方向性偏置的竞争在双能带非厄米系统中产生丰富的相图，能带结构差异（SSH链与梯子模型）决定了不同的退局域化路径和能谱拓扑特征。周期性边界条件的结果为主，同时讨论了开放边界条件的情形。

Abstract: We study two-banded, non-Hermitian random matrices inspired by sparse neural networks with a circular, 1d topology. We focus on two paradigmatic models, an SSH chain and a ladder model, which have both non-Hermitian directional bias and random sign disorder in the hoppings. The random sign disorder, which follows Dale's Law, leads to localization of the eigenstates, while the directional bias drives a delocalization transition in these states. The competition between disorder and directional bias results in rich eigenspectra with loops of extended states in the complex plane surrounded by regions of localized ones, and the eigenvalues are all confined to an annular region. Furthermore, the distinct band structures of the SSH chain and ladder model lead to different delocalization phenomena. Even in the absence of disorder, tuning the directional bias can lead to an eigenvalue degeneracy, which is an exceptional point for the SSH chain but a diabolic point for the ladder. In the presence of the disorder, these special eigenvalue degeneracies are preserved and also highlight key stages in the delocalization process. For both models, increasing the directional bias initially delocalizes states starting from within the bands. For the SSH chain, for large enough directional bias, the delocalized states open up a hole in the spectrum in the complex plane, similar to prior results for single band systems. But for the ladder model, as the directional bias is increased, the states delocalize in two stages, leading to two separate loops of extended states with localized states in between. The precise contours on which the extended states reside can be predicted from the Lyapunov exponents associated with products of random transfer matrices, in agreement with direct numerical diagonalization. Although we focus on periodic boundaries, results are discussed for open boundaries as well.

</details>


### [3] [Activation Functions, Statistics and Learning of Higher-Order Interactions in Restricted Boltzmann Machines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19178)
*Giovanni di Sarra,Yasser Roudi*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文利用受限玻尔兹曼机（RBM）与相互作用二元变量模型之间的对偶性，系统研究了四种不同激活函数（Linear、Step、ReLU、Exponential）下RBM所诱导的相互作用统计特性，揭示了高非线性激活函数（如Exponential）在特定参数范围内有助于表示和学习含高阶相互作用的复杂数据结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经网络的成功源于大量参数与非线性单单元激活函数的联合运用。受限玻尔兹曼机（Restricted Boltzmann Machine, RBM）为研究激活非线性对性能与表示的影响提供了简洁而强大的框架，但不同激活函数如何影响RBM的表示能力与学习效果尚需深入理解。

Method: 利用RBM与相互作用二元变量模型之间的对偶性（duality），从诱导相互作用（induced interactions）分布矩的角度，解析地表征四种常用激活函数（Linear、Step、ReLU、Exponential）所对应的可表示模型空间。通过理论计算与训练模拟结果进行定量对比验证。

Result: 解析计算对学习过程的定量预测与训练模拟结果高度吻合。研究发现，存在某些数据结构（尤其是由含大项高阶相互作用的模型生成的数据）对所有RBM而言都难以表示和学习。然而，快速增强的非线性激活函数（如Exponential）在通过解析确定的特定参数范围内，能够促进此类数据结构的表示与学习。

Conclusion: 不同激活函数显著影响RBM的表示能力，高阶相互作用数据结构是RBM表示学习的固有难点，但选择适当的高非线性激活函数可在特定条件下缓解这一限制。

Abstract: The great success of neural networks in recognizing hidden patterns and correlations in complex data lies in the way they take advantage of the large number of parameters and nonlinear single-unit activation, jointly. Restricted Boltzmann Machines (RBMs) provide a simple yet powerful framework for studying the impact of activation nonlinearities on performance and representation. In this work, we exploit the duality between RBMs and models of interacting binary variables to study the statistics of the interactions induced by RBM ensembles with different hidden unit activation functions. We characterize the space of representable models analytically in terms of moments of the distribution of induced interactions for four commonly used activation functions: Linear, Step, ReLU, and Exponential. Quantitative predictions of the analytical calculations on learning show a very good agreement with results of the simulations of the training process. In particular, our analysis shows that there are certain data structures, namely those generated by models of interacting variables with large interaction terms beyond pairwise, that are difficult to represent, and thus to learn, for any RBM. Yet, we find that rapidly increasing nonlinearities, such as the Exponential function, can facilitate the representation and learning of such data structures for a specific range of parameters that is determined analytically.

</details>


### [4] [Diffusing diffusivity selects Pareto tail exponent in random growth with redistribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19464)
*Maxence Arutkin,Alexandre Vallée*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究波动扩散率（diffusing diffusivity）如何影响Bouchaud-Mézard模型中帕累托（Pareto）财富尾部的选择，发现扩散率的随机波动会导致帕累托指数偏离平均扩散率情形，在高扩散慢刷新与平均扩散快刷新极限之间插值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Bouchaud-Mézard模型假设固定乘性噪声强度（multiplicative noise intensity），这限制了其在物理和金融增长过程中的适用性，因为实际过程中波动率（volatility/diffusivity）常呈现随机波动特征。

Method: 采用具有扩散扩散率（diffusing diffusivity）的几何布朗运动（geometric Brownian motion）替代常数噪声强度，并引入再分配（redistribution）机制；对两态扩散率（two-state diffusivity）情形进行精确尾部分析。

Result: 对于无再分配的几何布朗运动，扩散率波动效应是瞬态的（transient）：对数收益率在短时间尺度呈现非高斯统计，但在长时间尺度自平均为高斯形式。引入再分配后，相同的持久性（persistence）变为稳态。处于高扩散率状态的个体主导了稀有的大财富事件，因此帕累托指数不能通过将扩散率替换为其平均值来获得。两态扩散率下的精确尾部分析给出帕累托指数在高扩散率慢刷新（slow-refresh）极限与平均扩散率快刷新（fast-refresh）Bouchaud-Mézard极限之间插值。

Conclusion: 扩散率的随机波动对帕累托财富尾部的选择具有重要影响，标准模型中采用平均扩散率的做法在波动扩散率情形下不成立，需要新的理论框架来描述这类系统的尾部行为。

Abstract: Random multiplicative growth with redistribution generates stationary Pareto wealth tails in the Bouchaud-Mézard model, but assumes a fixed multiplicative noise intensity. This is restrictive for physical and financial growth processes, where volatility (diffusivity) is often fluctuating. We replace the constant noise intensity by a diffusing diffusivity and ask how these fluctuations select the Pareto stationary tail. For a geometric Brownian motion with diffusing diffusivity, the effect is transient: log-returns show non-Gaussian short-time statistics but self-average to a Gaussian form at long times. With redistribution, the same persistence becomes stationary. Agents remaining in high-diffusivity states dominate rare large-wealth events, so the Pareto exponent is not obtained by replacing the diffusivity by its mean. For a two-state diffusivity, an exact tail analysis gives a Pareto exponent interpolating between the high-diffusivity slow-refresh limit and the mean-diffusivity fast-refresh Bouchaud-Mézard limit.

</details>


### [5] [Optimal Persistence Reveals Hidden Topology in Complex Energy Landscapes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19785)
*LI Zhenpeng*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究了有限持久时间（finite persistence）下p=2球面自旋玻璃（spherical spin glass）中峡谷发现率（canyon-finding rate）Gamma(tau_p)的行为，发现其呈现倒U形分布，并在最优持久时间tau_p^*处达到峰值。tau_p^*随系统尺寸N和温度T的变化揭示了离散到准连续GOE交叉（crossover）以及景观拓扑的隐藏结构，表明最优持久性是无序景观中拓扑变化的一个普适原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索有限持久时间下无序景观（disordered landscape）中的拓扑转变（topological transition）机制，特别是通过峡谷发现率Gamma(tau_p)的峰值行为来揭示隐藏的景观拓扑结构。

Method: 在p=2球面自旋玻璃模型上，通过改变系统尺寸N（64–1024）和温度T（0.05–0.15以上），扫描持久时间tau_p并测量峡谷发现率Gamma(tau_p)，分析其峰值tau_p^*随N和T的变化规律。

Result: 低T=0.05时，tau_p^*随N增大从10降至5，标志着离散到准连续高斯正交系综（GOE, Gaussian Orthogonal Ensemble）交叉。N=1024时峰值在tau_p=5–6间平坦。N≥128时峡谷宽度饱和于xi_eff=1，对应tau_p^*=5（beta=0.4）。T≥0.15时tau_p^*=10，beta(T)∝1/T，温度仅通过v_th=√(2T)进入。T=0.10时，N≥128给出tau_p^*=8.0，N≤64时在8–10之间。

Conclusion: 最优持久时间（optimal persistence）揭示了无序景观中隐藏的拓扑结构，这一原理被认为在具有熵瓶颈（entropic bottlenecks）的无序景观中具有普适性。

Abstract: Infinite persistence marks the topological transition. For finite persistence, the canyon-finding rate Gamma(tau_p) on the p=2 spherical spin glass forms an inverted-U profile, peaking at an optimal tau_p^*. At low temperature (T=0.05), tau_p^* drops from 10 to 5 as N increases through 128, marking the discrete-to-quasi-continuous GOE crossover. For N=1024, the peak is flat between tau_p=5 and 6 within statistical uncertainties, preventing a more precise determination. For N>=128, the canyon width saturates at xi_eff=1, consistent with the measured tau_p^*=5 when beta=0.4. At higher temperatures (T>=0.15), tau_p^*=10 and beta(T) scales as 1/T, with temperature dependence entering only through v_th = sqrt(2T). For T=0.10 and N>=128, high-resolution scans give tau_p^*=8.0; for N<=64 at the same temperature, coarse scans place tau_p^* in the range 8-10. Thus, optimal persistence reveals the hidden topology of the landscape-a principle expected to be generic in disordered landscapes with entropic bottlenecks.

</details>


### [6] [Relativistic Saturation of Coulomb-Limited Electron Coherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20141)
*Yury A. Budkov*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文从狄拉克方程出发，将库仑无序介质中互相干（mutual coherence）和局域化（localization）的非相对论理论推广至透射电子显微镜（TEM）的相对论电子束情形，推导出包络旋量的近轴薛定谔类方程并得到有效耦合常数 \(A_{\rm rel}\)，发现横向相干长度 \(\rho_c\) 与单粒子局域化长度 \(\ell\) 的普适关系保持不变，且TEM标准能量范围已接近抑制库仑退相干的最优区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将非相对论框架下库仑无序介质的互相干与局域化理论拓展到相对论电子束（如TEM中的高能电子），以更准确地描述实际高能实验条件下的退相干现象。

Method: 从狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）出发，推导出描述包络旋量（envelope spinor）的近轴薛定谔类方程（paraxial Schrödinger-like equation），并提取无量纲化后的有效耦合常数 \(A_{\rm rel}=(\gamma+1)/(2\gamma\hbar v)\)；通过解析比较非相对论与极端相对论极限下的渐近行为，分析相位结构函数（phase structure function）与局域化长度。

Result: 有效耦合常数在非相对论极限下退化为 \(1/(\hbar v)\)，在极端相对论极限下饱和为 \(1/(2\hbar c)\)；横向相干长度 \(\rho_c\) 与单粒子局域化长度 \(\ell\) 之间的普适关系 \(\rho_c\sim\lambda_D\sqrt{\ell/L}\) 保持不变；互相干在大分离下的代数衰减（algebraic decay）类似于湍流介质中的波结构函数渐近行为，在两种情形中均存在；标准TEM能量（100–300 keV）已接近最优区间，进一步提高束能量带来的收益递减。

Conclusion: 相对论效应对库仑退相干的影响可通过修正后的有效耦合常数体现，但相干性与局域化之间的普适几何关系并未改变。实际TEM实验参数下退相干效应主要为概念和渐近意义上的，指数虽非指数型衰减但指数仍可较大。

Abstract: We show that the non-relativistic theory of mutual coherence and localization in Coulomb-disordered media can be extended to relativistic electron beams used in transmission electron microscopy (TEM). Starting from the Dirac equation, we derive a paraxial Schrödinger-like equation for the envelope spinor and obtain an effective coupling constant $A_{\rm rel}=(γ+1)/(2γ\hbar v)$ that governs the disorder-induced phase fluctuations. In the non-relativistic limit $γ\to1$ this reduces to $1/(\hbar v)$, while for ultra-relativistic electrons it saturates at $1/(2\hbar c)$. The universal relation between the transverse coherence length $ρ_c$ and the single-particle localization length $\ell$, namely $ρ_c\simλ_D\sqrt{\ell/L}$, remains unchanged. We compare the asymptotic behaviour of the phase structure function $D_φ(ρ)$ and the localization length in the non-relativistic and relativistic regimes, and show that the emergent algebraic decay of mutual coherence at large separations, analogous to the wave-structure-function asymptotics in turbulent media, persists in both cases. The results imply that standard TEM energies (100--300~keV) are already close to the optimal regime for minimizing Coulomb decoherence, and that further increasing the beam energy yields diminishing returns. While the asymptotic coherence decay is algebraic rather than exponential, the corresponding exponent can still be large for realistic experimental parameters, so the effect is primarily of conceptual and asymptotic significance.

</details>

# math.QA [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [The Hitchin and Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov connections are projectively equivalent in the genus zero case](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20097)
*Jørgen Ellegaard Andersen,Tim Henke*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文证明了在至少有三个标记点的亏格0曲面上，Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov联络与Hitchin联络之间的射影等价性。Pauly同构建立了两个向量丛的等价关系，主要定理表明该同构在上可以交织这两个联络（相差一个标量值1-形式），并据此构造了具有辅助度量校正的Hitchin联络，该构造是射影唯一且射影平坦的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立共形场论（conformal field theory）中Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov联络与几何量子化（geometric quantisation）中Hitchin联络之间的射影等价关系，从而沟通两种不同的数学物理框架。

Method: 利用Pauly同构建立Tsuchiya-Ueno-Yamada模型中的共形块层（sheaf of conformal blocks）上与平坦联络模空间（moduli space of flat connections）上的Verlinde丛之间的向量丛等价，并证明该同构以标量值1-形式为差交织两个联络。进一步通过辅助度量校正（auxiliary metaplectic correction）构造Hitchin联络。

Result: 主要定理证明Pauly同构在相差一个标量值1-形式的意义下交织Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov联络与Hitchin联络。由此构造的Hitchin联络具有射影唯一性（projectively unique）和射影平坦性（projectively flat）。

Conclusion: 本文在亏格0且至少有三个标记点的情形下建立了KZ联络与Hitchin联络的射影等价性，为共形场论与几何量子化之间的深层联系提供了严格证明，并为后续射影平坦联络的构造提供了新方法。

Abstract: This paper establishes the projective equivalence between the Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov connection and the Hitchin connection in genus 0 with at least 3 marked points. The Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov connection is defined on the sheaf of conformal blocks in the Tsuchiya-Ueno-Yamada model of conformal field theory. The Hitchin connection is defined on the Verlinde bundle via geometric quantisation of the moduli space of flat connections. Pauly's isomorphism establishes the equivalence of these two vector bundles. The main theorem of this paper is that the isomorphism intertwines these two connections up to a scalar-valued one-form. In addition, this theorem is used to construct a Hitchin connection through an auxiliary metaplectic correction. As a corollary of the main theorem, this construction of the Hitchin connection is projectively unique and projectively flat.

### [8] [Introduction to Higher Order Classical Dynamics: Pais-Uhlenbeck Model and Coupled Oscillators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20094)
*Cássius Anderson Miquele de Melo,Ivan Francisco de Souza*

Main category: physics.ed-ph

TL;DR: 本文展示了Hamilton-Ostrogradski形式论在Pais-Uhlenbeck振子上的应用，旨在为高等经典力学课程提供教学素材。该形式论扩展了经典哈密顿方程，用于处理包含高阶导数（higher-order derivatives）的拉格朗日量（Lagrangian），并基于Ostrogradski对高阶导数运动方程的开创性工作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然界中的大多数定律仅涉及二阶导数，而高阶导数系统（如Pais-Uhlenbeck振子）在理论上具有重要意义。尽管Hamilton-Ostrogradski形式论是处理此类系统的理论基础，但在教材和教学文献中鲜有讨论，因此作者希望填补这一教学空白。

Method: 作者基于Ostrogradski的工作，将Hamilton-Ostrogradski形式论（Hamilton-Ostrogradski formalism）应用于Pais-Uhlenbeck振子（Pais-Uhlenbeck oscillator），展示如何从包含高阶导数的拉格朗日量出发，构造相应的哈密顿方程（Hamilton's equations）。

Result: 本文给出了Hamilton-Ostrogradski形式论在Pais-Uhlenbeck振子上的具体应用示例，提供了可操作的计算框架。

Conclusion: 作者希望该工作能为高等经典力学课程中的高阶导数系统讨论提供一个教学基础，促进这一在标准教材中较少涉及的形式论得到更广泛的关注。

Abstract: Most of the laws of Nature involve derivatives up to the second order. Ostrogradski was the first to seek a formulation of the equations of higher-order derivatives. He extended Hamilton's equations by considering Lagrangians that depend on higher-order derivatives of generalized coordinates. The Hamilton-Ostrogradski formulation served as the basis for later studies with higher-order derivatives. However, the Hamilton-Ostrogradski formalism is rarely discussed in textbooks or the pedagogical literature. This motivated us to show how the Hamilton-Ostrogradski formalism can be applied it to the Pais-Uhlenbeck oscillator. We hope that the approach presented in this work can serve as a basis for discussion in advanced classical mechanics courses.

### [9] [First-passage processes in a deterministic one-dimensional cellular automaton model of traffic flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19023)
*Ofer Biham,Gilad Hertzberg Rabinovich,Eytan Katzav*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文推导了确定性一维交通流元胞自动机（CA规则184）中首次停车时间（first-stopping time）、末次停车时间（last-stopping time）以及停车事件次数的闭式表达式，揭示了个体车辆视角下的拥塞与弛豫时间尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解确定性交通流中个体车辆层面的首次通过过程（first-passage processes），特别是从自由流相到拥塞相的动力学相变（dynamical phase transition）及其弛豫（relaxation）行为。

Method: 采用首次通过过程（first-passage processes）框架，对CA规则184（CA rule 184）模型从随机初始状态出发进行解析推导，得到首次停车时间、末次停车时间及联合分布的闭式表达式。

Result: 得到了首次停车时间分布$P(T_{FS}=t)$和停车概率$P_S(t)$的闭式表达式；在低密度相（$0<p<1/2$）中给出了末次停车时间分布$P(T_{LS}=t)$及其与停车事件次数$N_S$的联合分布$P(T_{LS}=t,N_S=n)$和边际分布$P(N_S=n)$的闭式表达式。

Conclusion: 这些结果从个体车辆角度揭示了确定性交通流中拥塞与弛豫的时间尺度，并可为涉及多粒子相互作用的复杂弛豫过程（如确定性表面生长）提供见解。

Abstract: We present analytical results for first-passage processes in a deterministic one-dimensional cellular automaton (CA) model of traffic flow. Starting at time $t=0$ from a random initial state with car density p, at every time step $t\ge 1$ each car moves one step to the right if the cell on its right is empty, and is stopped if it is occupied by another car. The model, which coincides with CA rule 184 in Wolfram's numbering scheme, exhibits a continuous dynamical phase transition at $p=1/2$, between a low-density free-flowing phase and a high-density congested phase. Using the framework of first-passage processes, we derive a closed-form expression for the distribution $P(T_{FS}=t)$ of first-stopping (FS) times, which is the probability that a randomly selected car will be stopped for the first time at time $t$. We also obtain a closed-form expression for the stopping probability $P_S(t)$, which is the probability that a randomly selected car will be stopped at time $t$. In the low-density phase of $0<p<1/2$, the probability $P_S(t)$ yields a closed-form expression for the distribution $P(T_{LS}=t)$ of last-stopping (LS) times, which is the probability that a randomly selected car will be stopped for the last time at time $t$, beyond which it will move freely indefinitely. In this regime, we analyze the relation between the LS time and the number of stopping events $N_S$ which take place up to that time. We present closed-form expressions for the joint distribution $P(T_{LS}=t,N_S=n)$, for the two conditional distributions that emanate from it and for the marginal distribution $P(N_S=n)$. These results provide insight on the time scales of congestion and relaxation in deterministic traffic flow from the point of view of individual cars. In a broader context, they provide insight on complex relaxation processes that involve many interacting particles, such as deterministic surface growth.

</details>


### [10] [Proof of the absence of local conserved quantities in the Holstein model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19606)
*Fuga Ishii,Mizuki Yamaguchi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文证明了一维Holstein模型及更一般的Holstein-Hubbard模型不存在除哈密顿量和总费米子数算符之外的非平凡局域守恒量，从而将不可积性（nonintegrability）证明的范围扩展到包含不同统计性质粒子混合的系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子多体系统中，热化与输运等现象的讨论常假设系统不存在局域守恒量（即不可积性），但在电子-声子耦合系统（electron-phonon coupled system）——凝聚态物理中的典型场景——中，这一性质尚无具体证明。

Method: 论文通过分析一维Holstein模型及其推广的Holstein-Hubbard模型，证明其中除哈密顿量和总费米子数算符外，不存在其他非平凡局域守恒量（local conserved quantities）。

Result: 一维Holstein模型无除哈密顿量和总费米子数算符外的非平凡局域守恒量；该结论同样适用于更一般的Holstein-Hubbard模型。

Conclusion: 该结果将不可积性证明的范围拓展到包含不同统计性质粒子（如费米子与玻色子）混合的系统，具有重要理论推进意义。

Abstract: Absence of local conserved quantities, or \textit{nonintegrability}, is often assumed when discussing various phenomena in quantum many-body systems, such as thermalization and transport. However, no concrete proof of this property is known in electron--phonon coupled systems, a typical setting for condensed matter physics. In this paper, we show that the one-dimensional Holstein model has no nontrivial local conserved quantities other than the Hamiltonian itself and the total fermion number operator. We further show that the absence of nontrivial local conserved quantities also holds for the more general Holstein--Hubbard model. Our result has accomplished an advance in nonintegrability proofs by expanding their scope to systems in which particles with different statistical properties are mixed.

### [11] [Planckian dissipation from classical hydrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19450)
*Laura Foini,Jorge Kurchan,Silvia Pappalardi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过考察经典流体力学描述的自洽性对量子系统施加的约束，发现光锥内部分裂为经典区域和量子区域；维持经典区域存在迫使有效弛豫率至少达到普朗克量级，从而恢复扩散率、平衡时间和剪切粘度的下界，表明普朗克标度扩散常数是系统在低温下仍可被经典流体力学描述的代价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究经典流体力学描述的自洽性（self-consistency）对量子系统施加了哪些约束，尤其是理解普朗克标度（Planckian scaling）扩散常数的起源——它是否源于微观动力学的量子约束，还是源于经典描述本身的要求。

Method: 从量子涨落-耗散定理（quantum fluctuation-dissipation theorem）在时域的解读出发，将其视为在普朗克时间尺度（Plankian time-scale）上对关联函数精细细节的模糊化（blurring）。沿着光锥（light cone）内部的射线追踪这种模糊化，针对三种唯象流体力学方程——扩散方程（diffusion）、电报方程（telegraph）和扩散-电报方程（diffusive-telegraph）——进行分析。

Result: 光锥内部分裂为经典区域（classical region）和量子区域（quantum region）：经典区域中关联与响应满足经典涨落-耗散关系（classical fluctuation-dissipation relation），量子区域中则与之截然偏离。降低温度时，若要保持有限大小的经典区域，有效弛豫率（effective relaxation rate）必须至少达到普朗克量级（Planckian），从而导出扩散率（diffusivity）、平衡时间（equilibration time）和剪切粘度（shear viscosity）的下界。

Conclusion: 普朗克标度扩散常数并非微观动力学的量子约束，而是系统在低温下仍可被经典流体力学描述所必须付出的代价。

Abstract: In this work we ask what the self-consistency of a classical hydrodynamic description imposes on a quantum system. The quantum fluctuation-dissipation theorem, when read in the time domain, acts as a blurring of the fine details of the correlation functions on a Plankian time-scale. We track this blurring along rays inside the light cone for three phenomenological hydrodynamic equations -- diffusion, telegraph and diffusive-telegraph -- and find that the interior of the cone splits into a classical region, where correlation and response satisfy the classical fluctuation-dissipation relation, and a quantum region, where they deviate sharply from it. Preserving a finite classical region as the temperature is lowered forces the effective relaxation rate to be at least Planckian, recovering bounds on diffusivity, equilibration time and shear viscosity. In this way, Planckian scaling of the diffusion constant emerges not as a quantum constraint on microscopic dynamics, but as the price a system pays to remain describable by classical hydrodynamics down to low temperatures.

</details>


### [12] [Orthogonal Decomposition of Discretization-Induced Transport-Information Cost under Rank-Deficient Parametrizations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19505)
*Koretaka Yuge*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Frobenius投影的正交分解方法，将离散化引发的传输-信息代价分解为相对所选参数化的可观测与不可观测分量，从而在参数化秩亏情况下建立离散化代价与信息几何（information geometry）之间的桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续概率分布（continuous probability distributions）的离散化不可避免地导致支撑集（support）上局部测度的不可逆几何畸变，而此类畸变在信息几何（information geometry）框架下是外在的。现有工作虽建立了最优输运（optimal transport, OT）与信息几何的对应关系，但要求参数与支撑坐标直接对应。本文旨在将该框架推广至更一般的参数化情形，特别是当参数与支撑坐标之间的雅可比矩阵（Jacobian）秩亏时，离散化代价无法直接解释为信息几何量的问题。

Method: 引入基于Frobenius投影（Frobenius projection）的第二矩张量（second-moment tensor）正交分解方法，将参数涨落生成的协方差矩阵（covariance matrices）投影到线性子空间上，从而将离散化代价自然分解为相对于所选参数化的可观测分量（observable component）与不可观测分量（unobservable component）。

Result: 该正交分解方法成功将离散化诱导的传输-信息代价分离为可观测与不可观测两部分，揭示了参数化依赖性信息损失（parametrization-dependent information loss）的几何机制。

Conclusion: 所提出的形式化框架为分析离散化诱导传输-信息代价的部分可观测性（partial observability）提供了几何视角，系统阐明了参数化选择在信息损失中所扮演的角色。

Abstract: When we consider discretization of continuous probability distributions, it inevitably induces irreversible geometric distortion of local measure on the discretized support. While such discretziation-induced distortion is extrinsic to information geometry (IG) alone, we recently demonstrate that the discretization cost can be naturally characterized by the standard Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence between continuous distributions as expectation of their infinitesimal parameter variations. The framework is based on the correspondence between optimal transport (OT) and IG, primarily requring the selected parameters directly identifiable with support coordinates. The present work extends the framework to more generalized parametrization theta, particularly the Jacobian between theta and support coordinates is rank-deficient, which generally results in breaking down the interpretation of the discretization-induced costs as information-geometric quantities. To address the problem, we here introduce an orthogonal decomposition of the second-moment tensor onto linear subspace for the covariance matrices generated by parameter fluctuations, based on Frobenius projection. The decomposition naturally separates the discretization cost into observable and unobservable components relative to the chosen parametrization. The present formulation provides a geometric framework for analyzing partial observability of discretization-induced transport-information costs and clarifies the role of parametrization-dependent information loss.

</details>


### [13] [Ground-state Entropy of the Ising model on a Frustrated lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19831)

Method: 基于沙斯特里-萨瑟兰晶格上的二维伊辛模型，通过精确或数值方法计算基态熵；进一步引入一个推广模型，通过连续改变参数逐步解除零温下允许构型的约束，以分析熵的演化。

Result: 报告了该晶格上伊辛模型的基态熵具体数值，并给出了推广模型中约束连续移除后的熵变结果。

Abstract: We report the ground-state entropy of a 2-d Ising model on the Shastry-Sutherland lattice. We also study a generalization of this model, where a constraint on the zero temperature allowed configurations is removed continuously.

### [14] [Non-equilibrium quantum dynamics of interacting integrable models by Monte Carlo sampling Lehmann representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20065)
*Riccardo Senese,Fabian H. L. Essler*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）采样的数值方案，用于评估可积多体量子系统在均匀量子淬火（quantum quench）后有限时间内的局域算符期望值，该方法能够显著超越现有方法可处理的系统尺寸和时间尺度，并在Lieb-Liniger模型等系统中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定可积相互作用多粒子量子系统在均匀量子淬火（homogeneous quantum quench）后有限时间内的动力学是一个长期存在的挑战，现有方法在处理较大系统尺寸和较长演化时间时存在局限。

Method: 提出一种蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）采样方案，数值评估时间依赖局域算符期望值的Lehmann表示（Lehmann representation）；该方法同时兼容完整的Lehmann求和（full Lehmann sum）与淬灭作用形式（Quench Action formalism）。

Result: 在无相互作用的晶格和连续模型以及弱相互作用短时间结果中与精确解达到良好吻合；成功应用于排斥型Lieb-Liniger模型（Lieb-Liniger model）中从玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensate）开始的量子淬火，得到了宽相互作用强度范围内序参量的时间演化。

Conclusion: 所提方法能够有效扩展可积量子系统淬火动力学的数值可研究范围，但讨论指出在更一般的动力学关联函数和设置中可能出现“符号问题（sign problem）”。

Abstract: Determining the dynamics of interacting integrable many-particle quantum systems at finite times after homogeneous quantum quenches is a long-standing challenge. We present a Monte Carlo sampling scheme that numerically evaluates the Lehmann representation for time-dependent expectation values of local operators, allowing us to access system sizes and times significantly beyond the reach of existing methods. The approach accommodates both the full Lehmann sum and the Quench Action formalism. We benchmark against exact results for non-interacting lattice and continuum models and short-time results at weak interactions, finding excellent agreement. We apply the method to quantum quenches from a Bose-Einstein condensate in the repulsive Lieb-Liniger model and determine the time evolution of the order parameter for a wide range of interaction strengths. We discuss the emergence of a "sign problem" for more general dynamical correlators and setups.

### [15] [Diffusive-to-Ballistic transition in a Persistent Random Walk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20116)
*Amit Pradhan,Reshmi Roy,Purusattam Ray*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有时间依赖速度反转概率的持久随机游走（persistent random walk），发现当幂律反转概率 $p(t) \sim t^{-α}$ 在 $α=1$ 处出现非平衡动力学相变，区分超扩散（$α<1$）与弹道（$α\geq 1$）两个相，并通过速度关联、持续统计量、Binder累积量（Binder cumulant）和位移涨落的有限时间标度（finite time scaling）对转变进行了详细表征。该转变在更一般的时间依赖反转概率下也成立，并在任意维数下保持各向同性时依然存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 持久随机游走是许多物理与生物系统的基本模型，但时间依赖速度反转概率对系统动力学行为的影响尚不明确。本文旨在识别此类系统中是否存在非平衡动力学相变（non-equilibrium dynamical transition），并揭示其普适性。

Method: 以幂律反转概率 $p(t)\sim t^{-α}$ 作为代表性模型，利用速度关联（velocity correlations）和持续统计量（persistence statistics）分析动力学行为，并结合Binder累积量（Binder cumulant）与位移涨落的有限时间标度（finite time scaling）表征相变特征。

Result: 系统在 $α=1$ 处发生动力学相变：$α<1$ 为超扩散（super-diffusive）区域，$α\geq 1$ 为弹道（ballistic）区域。该转变不仅限于幂律形式，在满足相同判据的多种时间依赖反转概率下均能出现，且在任意空间维度中当速度空间保持各向同性时依然成立。

Conclusion: 时间依赖速度反转概率可诱导持久随机游走中的非平衡动力学相变，该相变具有普适性，不受具体概率形式或空间维度的限制（在保持速度各向同性的前提下）。

Abstract: We study persistent random walk with time dependent velocity reversal probabilities and identify a criterion for a non-equilibrium dynamical transition. As a representative example, we consider a power law reversal probability $p(t)\sim t^{-α}$ and show that the system undergoes a transition at $α=1$, separating a super-diffusive regime for $α<1$ from ballistic regime for $α\geq 1$. Using the results for velocity correlations and persistence statistics, together with finite time scaling of the Binder cumulant and displacement fluctuations, we characterize the transition and its properties in detail. We further argue that the transition is not limited to the power law form, but can also arise for several other time dependent reversal probabilities satisfying the same criterion. The transition persists in arbitrary spatial dimensions provided isotropy of the velocity space is preserved.

</details>


### [16] [Towards a Matrix Product Ansatz in Two Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20160)
*Chandraniva Guha Ray,Aikya Banerjee,P. K. Mohanty*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文将矩阵乘积拟设（matrix product ansatz, MPA）形式推广到二维，并引入并精确求解了一个非守恒辅助排斥模型（NAEM）。该模型在守恒极限下发生吸收相变，临界密度ρ_c=1/2，阶参量指数β=3；其稳态映射到硬方块晶格气体，为非平衡系统实现约束晶格气体的平衡态提供了动力学途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 矩阵乘积拟设（MPA）是一维非平衡随机过程精确稳态构造的强大框架，但向高维的推广受到限制。本文旨在将MPA形式推广到二维，以建立二维相互作用随机系统精确求解的系统性方法。

Method: 本文引入了二维MPA形式，并基于此提出并精确求解了非保守辅助排斥模型（non-conserved assisted exclusion model, NAEM）。该模型具有受约束的跳跃和局域的出生-死亡动力学：一个粒子仅当恰好有一个邻居位点空置时才能跳向该邻居，而粒子的产生和湮灭只发生在所有邻居均被占据的位点上。

Result: MPA给出了精确的稳态权重，并提供了计算密度矩、粒子流等可观测量的系统方法。在粒子守恒极限下，系统在临界密度ρ_c=1/2处发生吸收相变，阶参量指数β=3。此外，NAEM稳态精确映射到具有最近邻排斥的硬方块晶格气体（hard-square lattice gas）。

Conclusion: 本工作将矩阵乘积方法推广到一维之外，建立了二维相互作用随机系统精确求解的系统性途径，同时为非平衡动力学实现约束晶格气体的平衡态提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Matrix product ansatz (MPA) is a powerful framework for constructing exact steady state weights of one dimensional non-equilibrium stochastic processes; but its generalization to higher dimensions is limited. Here, we introduce the MPA formalism for two dimensions (2D). As a concrete application, we introduce and exactly solve a non-conserved assisted exclusion model (NAEM) in one and two dimensions with constrained hopping and local birth-death dynamics: a particle can hop to a neighbouring site only when exactly one of its neighbouring sites is vacant, while creation and annihilation occur exclusively at sites whose neighbours are all occupied. The MPA yields exact steady-state weights and provides a systematic method to compute observables such as density moments and particle currents. In the particle-conserving limit, the system undergoes an absorbing phase transition at the critical density $ρ_c=\frac12$ with order-parameter exponent $β=3$. We further show that the steady state of the NAEM maps exactly onto the well-studied hard-square lattice gas with nearest-neighbour exclusion, thereby providing a nonequilibrium dynamical route to realizing equilibrium states of constrained lattice gases. Our work generalizes matrix-product methods beyond one dimension, establishing a systematic approach to exact solutions of interacting stochastic systems in 2D.

</details>

### [17] [Floquet-Engineered Odd-Parity Altermagnetic Higher-Order Topology in a Two-Dimensional Antiferromagnet Cr$_2$CH$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19184)
*Xiaorong Zou,Hyeon Suk Shin,Baibiao Huang,Yanmei Zang,Ying Dai,Chengwang Niu,Chang-Jong Kang,Chang Woo Myung*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过周期性驱动（periodic driving）在Cr₂CH₂单层中实现了奇宇称交变磁性（odd-parity altermagnetic）高阶拓扑绝缘体（HOTI）相，验证了周期驱动下对称性保护的角态能够在Floquet能带重整化中保持稳定，并揭示了驱动强度增大下向交变磁性半金属态的演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 周期性驱动为动态调控量子物质态提供了平台，但其对对称性保护拓扑相（symmetry-protected topological phases）的影响尚未被完全理解；本文旨在探索周期性驱动如何实现磁性高阶拓扑相，并建立磁性与拓扑之间的直接联系。

Method: 以Cr₂CH₂单层为研究对象，在平衡态下其为受C₃旋转对称性保护的二维反铁磁（antiferromagnetic, AFM）高阶拓扑绝缘体；通过施加圆极化光（circularly polarized light, CPL）驱动，利用Floquet理论分析其能带重整化（band renormalization）及对称性变化，研究其向交变磁性高阶拓扑绝缘体相的演化。

Result: 在圆极化光驱动下，系统形成具有奇宇称自旋劈裂（odd-parity spin splitting）的f波交变磁性态，对称性为[C₂||\overline{3}_{001}]；尽管存在显著的Floquet诱导能带重整化，C₃保护的角态（corner states）在广泛的驱动强度范围内保持稳定；随光强增大，系统逐渐演化为交变磁性半金属态（altermagnetic semimetallic state）。

Conclusion: 周期性驱动可在反铁磁系统中实现交变磁性高阶拓扑绝缘体相，建立了磁性与高阶拓扑之间的直接联系，为耦合自旋与拓扑输运的调控提供了新途径。

Abstract: Periodic driving provides a platform to dynamically tailor quantum states of matter, yet its impact on symmetry-protected topological phases remains incompletely understood. Here, we demonstrate that periodic driving enables the realization of an odd-parity altermagnetic (AM) higher-order topological insulator (HOTI) phase in the Cr$_2$CH$_2$ monolayer. In equilibrium, Cr$_2$CH$_2$ is a 2D antiferromagnetic (AFM) HOTI protected by $\mathcal C_3$ rotational symmetry, characterized by a symmetry indicator $χ^{(3)}$ = $\{-2,1\}$ and robust corner states. Under circularly polarized light (CPL), the system develops a f-wave altermagnetic state governed by the symmetry $[C_{2}||\overline{3}_{001}]$ with odd-parity spin splitting. Despite substantial Floquet-induced band renormalization, the $\mathcal C_3$-protected corner states remain intact over a broad range of driving strengths, highlighting the altermagnetic higher-order topology under Floquet driving. As the light intensity increases, the system gradually evolves into an altermagnetic semimetallic state. These results establish a direct connection between magnetism and topology in a periodically driven AFM system, offering a route toward the control of coupled spin and topological transport.

### [18] [Informational blueprints reveal condition-dependent gene regulatory architectures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19071)
*Doruk Efe Gökmen,Rosalind Wenshan Pan,Tom Röschinger,Stephen Quake,Hernan Garcia,Rob Phillips,Vincenzo Vitelli*

Main category: q-bio.GN

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为信息蓝图（information blueprint）的算法，受重整化群（renormalization group）技术启发，通过将核苷酸序列压缩为集体坐标（hyperletters），从非编码区中提取转录因子（transcription factor, TF）结合位点，并验证于大肠杆菌（E. coli）实验数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基因组中大量非编码区域控制关键生物学功能，但缺乏类似遗传密码的“查找表”来直接识别转录因子（TF）的结合位点，现有局部信息足迹方法无法充分捕获全局信息。

Method: 提出信息蓝图（information blueprint）算法，通过优化可同时扫描整个启动子序列的滤波器（filters），将核苷酸序列压缩为集体坐标（hyperletters），从而压缩全局信息。该方法受重整化群（renormalization group）技术启发，将TF结合位点识别为粗粒化变量（coarse-grained variables），这些变量组合了具有最高集体表达影响的关联突变组。

Result: 在大肠杆菌（E. coli）实验数据上验证了该方法，并发现了新的调控元件（regulatory elements），展示了该方法在不同生长条件下大规模部署的能力。

Conclusion: 该算法超越了基于单个碱基与表达水平之间局部信息足迹的方法，能够有效从非编码序列中提取TF结合位点，并为大规模调控元件发现提供了通用框架。

Abstract: While coding regions in the genome have a direct interpretation in terms of protein products, significant fractions are non-coding and yet control essential biological functions. Unlike the genetic code, there is no "lookup table" that identifies where regulatory proteins, known as transcription factors (TFs), bind. Here, we extract these binding sites by distilling sequences of nucleotide letters into collective coordinates (hyperletters) representing the binding sites that are active under specific environmental conditions. Going beyond local information footprints between individual bases and expression levels, our $\textit{information blueprint}$ algorithm compresses the global information by optimising filters that simultaneously scan an entire promoter sequence. Inspired by renormalisation-group techniques, we identify TF binding sites as coarse-grained variables combining groups of correlated mutations with the highest collective impact on gene expression. We validate our approach on experimental data for $\textit{E. coli}$ and discover novel regulatory elements illustrating its deployment at scale across growth conditions.

### [19] [Tracking Coupled Granular Temperature and Entropy Dynamics in Granular Materials via Dielectric Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19560)
*Sophia G. Krastana,Anthony N. Papathanassiou*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过阻抗谱测量石墨粉末的体积变化，证明介电弛豫时间与颗粒温度（granular temperature）和构型熵（configurational entropy）之间的关系符合修正的Adam-Gibbs（AG）定律，从而建立了介电谱（dielectric spectroscopy）作为探测颗粒物质（granular matter）构型动力学的非破坏性手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究是否可以通过热激活过程（thermally activated processes），特别是电荷跳跃与俘获（charge hopping and trapping），来探测颗粒体系中结构弛豫（structural relaxation）的变化，从而将介电谱方法从热体系推广至颗粒物质。

Method: 通过逐步减少石墨粉末体积以改变其堆积分数（packing fraction），从体积数据估计相对构型熵与颗粒温度，并利用阻抗谱（impedance spectroscopy）评估电导率与电容。

Result: 由复阻抗导出的介电弛豫时间（dielectric relaxation time）的对数在松散态与密实态下均与颗粒温度和熵成线性标度关系；堆积分数变化引起的复阻抗改变受颗粒构型调控，严格遵循类似热体系的AG关系。

Conclusion: 介电谱可作为一种有效且非破坏性的工具，用于追踪颗粒物质中的构型动力学，类似于其在聚合物和玻璃形成体（glass formers）中的既有应用。

Abstract: In glass-forming liquids, structural dynamics are governed by configurational entropy and temperature, with dielectric relaxation time scaling alongside structural relaxation time as described by the Adam-Gibbs (AG) model. Under Edwards's athermal statistical thermodynamics, a modified AG law similarly governs granular matter, provided that granular temperature and configurational entropy are appropriately defined. This study investigates whether variations in the structural relaxation of granular systems can be probed via thermally activated processes, specifically electric charge hopping and trapping. By progressively reducing the volume of graphite powder to vary its packing fraction, we estimated relative configurational entropy and granular temperature from volumetric data, while evaluating electrical conductivity and capacity via impedance spectroscopy. We demonstrate that the logarithm of the dielectric relaxation time, derived from complex impedance, scales with granular temperature and entropy across both loose and compact states. Consequently, changes in the complex impedance resulting from packing fraction variations are tuned by granule configuration, strictly adhering to an AG-like relationship for thermal systems. These findings establish dielectric spectroscopy as a viable, non-destructive tool for tracing configurational dynamics in granular matter, analogous to its established use in polymers and glass formers.

### [20] [The fracture resistance of elastic networks increases with the density of defects like a random walk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19684)
*Antoine Sanner,Luca Michel,David S. Kammer*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过分析二维三角弹簧网络中缺失键的浓度变化，建立了微观无序性（missing bonds）与宏观断裂能（fracture energy G^c）之间的定量联系，发现G^c随裂纹扩展a增加而增加，其均值与无序度参数ν的平方根呈正比，且G^c(a)随a呈对数增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已知无序性（disorder）可通过局部不均匀性引起的裂纹止裂（crack arrest）提高表观断裂能G^c，但G^c对无序程度的依赖关系仍不明确，缺乏定量理解。

Method: 采用二维三角弹簧网络（two-dimensional triangular network of springs）作为模型系统，通过改变缺失键（missing bonds）的浓度ν引入无序性，模拟裂纹扩展并测量表观断裂能G^c(a)；将缺失键效应映射为等效局部断裂能景观Γ^{loc}(a)，并应用裂纹止裂理论进行分析。

Result: Γ^{loc}涨落的标准差随√ν增加，可归因于单个缺失键扰动的随机游走式叠加；平均G^c(a)同样遵循√ν标度；Γ^{loc}的概率密度函数具有指数尾部，导致G^c(a)随裂纹扩展a呈对数增长。

Conclusion: 结果定量地将微观结构无序性与宏观断裂能联系起来，为广泛材料中断裂能的定量预测奠定了基础。

Abstract: Disordered spring networks are a well-established model system to study fracture in a wide range of materials, from ceramics to polymer networks and mechanical metamaterials, across length scales from the atomistic to the macroscopic. A central quantity characterizing fracture is the apparent fracture energy $G^c$, which measures the resistance to the propagation of a preexisting dominant crack. While it is well established that disorder can increase $G^c$ through crack arrest by local inhomogeneities, its dependence on the degree of disorder remains poorly understood. Here, we study the effect of varying concentrations of missing bonds on crack propagation of an otherwise perfect two-dimensional triangular network of springs. For a given network with a fixed concentration of missing bonds, the apparent fracture energy $G^c(a)$ increases with crack advance $a$. This behavior can be explained by mapping the effect of the missing bonds onto an equivalent local fracture energy landscape $Γ^{loc}(a)$ and applying established theories linking planar crack arrest with fluctuations in $Γ^{loc}(a)$. For increasing fraction of missing bonds $ν$, the standard deviation of the fluctuations of $Γ^{loc}$ increases with $\sqrtν$, which we explain by considering a random-walk-like superposition of perturbations caused by individual missing bonds. We demonstrate that as a consequence of crack arrest by fluctuations in $Γ^{loc}$, the average $G^c(a)$ follows the same $\sqrtν$ scaling. Furthermore, we observe that the probability density of $Γ^{loc}$ has an exponential tail leading to a logarithmic increase of $G^c(a)$ with crack advance $a$. Our results quantitatively link microstructural disorder to macroscopic fracture energy and paves the way for quantitative predictions of the fracture energy in a wide variety of materials.

</details>


### [21] [Function, Complexity and Thermodynamics in Adaptive and Intelligent Soft Matter Systems: An Information-Theoretical Formulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19795)
*George S. Attard*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文针对软物质（soft matter）中“响应性、适应性和智能性”三个术语定义模糊的问题，将其形式化为信息通道模型，并提出了三种信息论指标（I1、I2、I3）用于跨类比较。通过将材料视为信息通道，揭示了复杂度-功能之间的权衡关系，并推导出热力学上限（Carnot模拟极限）和最优内部复杂度N*。基准框架将十种典型系统映射到体积速率-功率密度平面，发现了软物质与生物学之间的差距源于每个元素的基底能量尺度（1–10 kBT 对比 10^4–10^5 kBT），并提出了三种填补该差距的架构路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软物质领域中“响应性（responsive）、适应性（adaptive）和智能性（intelligent）”三个术语被广泛使用但定义不一致，缺乏统一的量化框架来区分和比较不同复杂程度的材料。

Method: 将三种行为形式化为信息通道模型：响应性为无记忆映射 p(y|x)，适应性为状态条件化映射 p(y|x,s)，智能性为反馈修正通道 p(y_t|x_t, X_past, Y_past)。提出三种信息论指标——构型多样性I1、Hazen功能选择性I2和刺激-响应信息传递I3——并构建基准框架（benchmarking framework）在共同信息坐标下比较不同系统。

Result: 十种代表系统被映射到体积速率（I3/单位体积）对功率密度（power density）的平面上，形成四条位于Landauer下限（Landauer floor）之上的谱带：软物质和形状记忆合金为10^18至10^20；硅数字和机电系统为10^10至10^16；忆阻神经形态系统为10^9至10^10；演化生物系统为10^5至10^8（均至少具有一个数量级的不确定性）。

Conclusion: 软物质与生物学之间的机理差距源自每个元素的基底能量尺度不同（1–10 kBT 对比 10^4–10^5 kBT）。提出三种架构路径——反馈（feedback）、多通道正交性（multi-channel orthogonality）和分子记忆（molecular memory）——可使软物质填充这一差距。

Abstract: The terms responsive, adaptive and intelligent are widely used in soft matter but inconsistently defined. This paper formulates them as information channels of increasing architectural complexity: a memoryless map p(y|x) (responsive), a state-conditioned map p(y|x,s) (adaptive), and a feedback-modified channel p(y_t|x_t, X_past, Y_past) (intelligent). Existing complexity metrics for cross-class comparison fail at least one of: dimensional consistency, common reference, thermodynamic coupling, scale-bridging. Three information-theoretic metrics are proposed: configurational diversity I1, Hazen functional selectivity I2, and stimulus-response information transfer I3. Treating the material as the channel yields a complexity-function relationship: internal complexity raises potential information capacity but also raises attenuation and dissipation. This implies a thermodynamic scaling ceiling and an optimal internal complexity N* set by transmission efficiency, stimulus energy and thermal noise (a Carnot-analogue limit). A benchmarking framework compares synthetic soft matter, biological systems and hard-matter architectures in common information coordinates. Ten representative systems are mapped on the volumetric rate (I3 per unit volume) versus power density plane. They form four bands above the Landauer floor: 10^18 to 10^20 for soft matter and shape-memory alloys; 10^10 to 10^16 for silicon digital and electromechanical; 10^9 to 10^10 for memristor neuromorphic; 10^5 to 10^8 for evolved biology (all uncertain to at least one order of magnitude). The mechanistic origin of the gap between synthetic soft matter and biology is the per-element substrate energy scale (1 to 10 kBT versus 10^4 to 10^5 kBT). Three architectural routes - feedback, multi-channel orthogonality, and molecular memory - are proposed to let soft matter populate this gap.

</details>


### [22] [Percolation of a cohesive fine particle in a static bed](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19845)
*Jizhi Zhang,Qiong Zhang,Julio M. Ottino,Paul B. Umbanhowar,Richard M. Lueptow*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过离散元法（discrete element method）模拟了黏性细颗粒在静态大颗粒床中的渗流行为，发现当黏聚力（cohesion）和摩擦力足够大时，即使几何上允许通过，细颗粒也会因碰撞后无法回弹而被捕获，从而建立了基于碰撞捕获概率和力平衡的预测模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细颗粒在静态大颗粒床中的渗流对工业和自然过程至关重要，已有研究关注了粒径、摩擦系数、恢复系数及多分散性等因素，但黏聚力（cohesion）作为额外因素的影响尚不明确，需要系统研究。

Method: 采用离散元法（discrete element method, DEM）模拟重力驱动的黏性细颗粒通过随机堆积的大颗粒静态床的渗流过程；细颗粒仅与床颗粒相互作用，不相互接触；设定大颗粒与细颗粒的直径比为7，以确保非黏性细颗粒在几何上能够通过最窄的孔隙喉道。

Result: 足够大的黏聚力和摩擦力会导致非几何捕获（non-geometric trapping）：细颗粒因黏聚力大、恢复系数低、碰撞速度低而在碰撞后无法回弹，后续的滚动或滑动也不足以使其脱离；建立了基于每次碰撞捕获概率和碰撞频率的碰撞模型来预测捕获距离；提出了基于力平衡的静态平衡条件来判定接触后细颗粒是否保持静止。

Conclusion: 黏性细颗粒的渗流不仅由几何可达性（geometric accessibility）决定，还受颗粒尺度的相互作用动力学（particle-scale interaction dynamics）控制，后者可以超越几何预期的结果。

Abstract: Percolation of fine particles (fines) in a static bed of larger particles is central to many industrial and natural processes. Non-cohesive fines either pass through the bed or become trapped depending on multiple factors including particle sizes, friction and restitution coefficients, and size-polydispersity. Here we consider the additional factor of cohesion. We use the discrete element method to simulate gravity-driven percolation of cohesive fine particles through a static bed of randomly packed large particles; fines interact with bed particles but not with each other. A large-to-fine particle diameter ratio of 7 geometrically permits non-cohesive fines to pass the narrowest pore throats formed by the large particles so they can freely percolate. However, sufficiently large cohesion and friction lead to non-geometric trapping. Fines are trapped when they fail to rebound after a collision, due to large cohesion, low restitution, and low collision velocity, and any subsequent rolling or sliding is insufficient to cause detachment. This establishes a sequence of local interactions -- collision, adhesion, and post-contact motion -- that governs the ultimate fate of a fine particle. A collisional model that incorporates a trapping probability per collision and a collision frequency predicts the trapping distance in the regime dominated by collision-induced trapping. For non-rebounding collisions, frictional effects are enhanced by cohesion and, when large enough, prevent the fine particle from subsequently detaching. A static equilibrium condition based on force balance predicts whether a fine particle remains stationary after contact. These results show that percolation of cohesive fine particles is not determined by geometric accessibility alone, but also by particle-scale interaction dynamics that can override geometric expectations.

</details>

# econ.GN [[Back]](#toc)

### [23] [Geometric Brownian motion with intermittent entries and exits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17299)
*Suvam Pal,Viktor Stojkoski,Arnab Pal,Trifce Sandev*

Main category: econ.GN

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个广义几何布朗运动（generalized geometric Brownian motion）框架，通过引入非对称的进入（entry）与退出（exit）机制，扩展了早期随机重置（stochastic resetting）模型。研究发现，尽管系统非保守且进入与退出率不对称，系统仍能收敛到平稳分布（stationary distribution），并呈现出三种不同的动力学区间。此外，论文推导了生存概率（survival probability）和平均首达时间（mean first-passage time, MFPT），并发现存在最优退出率使平均首达时间最小化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期随机重置模型假设进入率与退出率相同，无法刻画经济系统中常见的非对称进入/退出过程（如企业进入与退出、劳动者流入与流出、收入增长与损失等现实特征）。本文旨在建立一个更一般化的框架，以捕捉这些实际经济现象。

Method: 采用广义几何布朗运动框架，引入独立的进入率与退出率参数，构建非保守（non-conservative）随机过程模型，并通过解析方法分析系统的平稳分布、矩的动态行为、生存概率与平均首达时间。

Result: 系统在非对称进入与退出条件下仍能松弛到平稳分布；矩的动态行为表现出三种不同区间，源于波动率（volatility）、漂移（drift）、进入率与退出率的相互作用；推导了生存概率与平均首达时间；发现存在一个最优退出率使平均首达时间最小化。

Conclusion: 该模型有助于理解由增长、波动、进入与退出共同塑造的异质性经济系统的长期演化行为，并为进入与退出政策如何影响系统结果提供了理论启示。

Abstract: We study a generalized geometric Brownian motion framework that incorporates both entries of new units and exit mechanisms for the current population, extending earlier stochastic resetting models where these rates are treated as identical. The model captures realistic features observed in many economic observables, which can be explained as market-driven firm entries/exits, worker inflow/outflow, and income growth/loss. This model is not conservative and, despite the asymmetry in the entry and exit rates, we find that the system eventually relaxes to a stationary distribution. Moreover, our analysis reveals three distinct dynamical regimes in the moments of the distribution, arising from the interplay between volatility, drift, entry, and exit rates. We further derive the survival probability and the mean first-passage time associated with the observed variable reaching certain threshold under the competing entry-exit processes. Interestingly, we identify an optimal exit rate that minimizes the mean first-passage time, providing insights into how entry and exit policies can influence the outcome of the system. These results should be useful for understanding the long-run behavior of economic systems in which growth, volatility, entry, and exit jointly shape the evolution of heterogeneous units.

</details>

### [24] [Evidence for Intermediate-Mass Black Holes From Microlensing Signatures in CHIME/FRB catalog 2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19653)
*Huan Zhou,Zhengxiang Li,Cheng-Gang Shao,Xi-Jing Wang,Kai Liao,He Gao,Zong-Hong Zhu*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文基于快速射电暴（FRB）的微引力透镜效应，开发了一套动态谱搜索管线，并在CHIME/FRB目录2中识别出两个候选中间质量黑洞（IMBH），其质量分别约为539–609 M☉和1544–2571 M☉；若这些透镜信号真实，对应的原初黑洞（PBH）可能占暗物质约4%；若为假阳性，则质量>300 M☉的PBH丰度上限约为13%（95%置信水平）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中间质量黑洞（intermediate-mass black holes, IMBHs）是黑洞质量谱系中的缺失环节，兼具强场引力检验与多信使观测前景，但极难直接探测。本文旨在利用快速射电暴（fast radio bursts, FRBs）的微引力透镜（microlensing）效应，提供一种清洁而有力的IMBH搜寻方法。

Method: 开发了一套基于FRB动态谱（dynamic spectra）的微透镜搜索管线，并将其应用于CHIME/FRB Catalog 2的数据。

Result: 在两个独立源FRB 20190131D和FRB 20211115A中各识别出一个微透镜信号，对应的透镜质量分别约为539–609 M☉和1544–2571 M☉。若视线上无星系或星系团等中间结构，这两个候选IMBH可能为孤立的原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs），其在相应质量范围内占暗物质约4%。若两个候选信号并非真实透镜信号，则质量>300 M☉的原初黑洞丰度上限为约13%（95%置信水平）。

Conclusion: FRB微透镜效应有望成为探测（原初）IMBH的有力工具；未来需要更全面的FRB观测信息，并深入理解FRB本征辐射机制是否可能产生类透镜信号，以确证这一方法的可靠性。

Abstract: Intermediate-mass black holes (IMBHs) are the missing link in the cosmic hierarchy of black holes, bridging the gap between stellar-mass black holes and supermassive ones. They also serve as unique laboratories for testing strong-field gravity and are prime targets for future multi-messenger observations. However, IMBHs are a population that has remained notoriously difficult to detect. The microlensing effect of fast radio bursts (FRBs) can serve as a clean and powerful method to probe IMBHs. In this work, we develop a pipeline to search for microlensed FRBs based on their dynamic spectra and apply it to the CHIME/FRB Catalog 2. Two microlensing signatures have been identified in two separate sources, i.e. FRB~20190131D and FRB~20211115A. The inferred lens masses for these two signatures are $\sim[539-609]~M_{\odot}$ and $\sim[1544-2571]~M_{\odot}$, respectively. Here we interpret them as evidence for IMBHs. If there are no intervening structures-such as galaxies or clusters-along the line of sights for these two sources, the two identified IMBHs might be isolated and of primordial origins. In that case, we obtain primordial black holes (PBHs) within these two mass ranges would constitute $\sim4\%$ of dark matter. Moreover, if these two candidates are not genuine lensing signatures, the abundance of intermediate-mass PBHs with masses $>300,M_{\odot}$ is constrained to be $\sim13\%$ at $95\%$ confidence level. Therefore, more comprehensive observational information for FRBs, together with a deeper understanding of whether the intrinsic emission mechanisms of FRBs can produce lensing-like signals, will be crucial for establishing this effect as a powerful tool for probing (primordial) IMBHs.

</details>


### [25] [Magnetized neutron stars: perturbative versus fully-numerical approaches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19761)
*Debarati Chatterjee,Daw Guttmann,Jérôme Novak,Micaela Oertel,Martin Jakob Steil*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文在广义相对论（General Relativity）框架下，系统比较了两种研究强磁化中子星（即磁星，magnetar）在纯环极磁场（poloidal magnetic field）下结构变形的方法：微扰法（Konno-99）与全数值方法（基于LORENE库）。结果表明：微扰法在极高磁场（>10^16 G）下失效，但在实际观测值范围内表现良好；而全数值法在低磁场（~10^10 G）下存在分辨率问题，导致形变与质量四极矩（mass quadrupole moment）计算不精确。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高磁化中子星（磁星，magnetar）的强磁场对其结构与形状的影响，这一效应对于理解连续引力波（continuous gravitational waves）的发射具有重要意义。为此，需要系统比较已有的数值方法与微扰方法在广义相对论（General Relativity）框架下的适用性与局限性。

Method: 在广义相对论框架下，将磁场限制为纯环极（poloidal）结构，分别采用两种方法：(1) 微扰法（Konno-99），假设磁场引起的变形很小且磁场仅来自偶极电流（dipole currents）；(2) 全数值法，基于LORENE库。通过改变极区磁场强度、恒星致密度及物态方程（equation of state）来计算磁场分布与恒星形变。

Result: 微扰法在极高极区磁场值（通常高于数倍10^16 G）下失效，但在实际观测值（包括磁星在内）范围内结果良好。全数值法则在较低磁场值（约10^10 G）时出现分辨率问题，导致恒星形变与质量四极矩（mass quadrupole moment）的计算不够精确。

Conclusion: 两种方法各有优劣：微扰法适用于实际观测的磁场范围，但在极端高场下不可靠；全数值法能处理高场情形，却在低场下因分辨率不足而精度受限。研究建议根据具体磁场强度选择合适的方法，或结合两者优势以更全面地表征磁化中子星的结构。

Abstract: (1) Background: for the study of highly magnetized neutron
  stars observed as magnetars, and to quantify the effect of this
  intense magnetic field onto the star's structure and shape which
  can be particularly relevant for the study of emission of continuous
  gravitational waves, both numerical and perturbative approaches have been developed. (2) Methods: we compare these two approaches in General
  Relativity with the limitation to the case where the magnetic field has a
  purely poloidal structure. The perturbative one (Konno-99)
  assumes that the deformation induced by the magnetic field is small
  and that this field arises only from dipole currents. The full
  numerical one is based on the library LORENE. (3) Results: we have used both
  approaches to compute the magnetic field distribution and the
  deformation of the star, varying the value of the magnetic field at
  the pole, the compactness of the star and its equation of state. (4)
  Conclusions: whereas the perturbative approach breaks down for very
  high polar magnetic field values (typically above a few times
  $10^{16}$ G), it gives very good results for observed values, even
  in magnetars. On the contrary, the numerical code exhibits
  resolution problems for relatively low magnetic field values
  (typically $10^{10}$ G), which translates into imprecise computation of the star's
  deformation and mass quadrupole moment.

</details>

### [26] [Quantum effective action for dissipative semiclassical dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19643)
*Cesare Vianello,Andrea Bardin,Luca Salasnich*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文利用 Schwinger-Keldysh 形式论中的量子有效作用量，推导了耗散系统中由宏观自由度控制的半经典朗之万动力学的量子修正，并应用于超导约瑟夫森结与玻色子结两种系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在半经典描述中，耗散系统的量子涨落修正尚未被系统性地推导，特别是与埃伦费斯特定理（Ehrenfest theorem）之间的关联尚不明确。

Method: 采用 Schwinger-Keldysh 形式论（Schwinger-Keldysh formalism）中的量子有效作用量（quantum effective action）来推导耗散系统半经典朗之万动力学（semiclassical Langevin dynamics）的量子修正。

Result: 在低温弱阻尼（low-temperature and weak-damping regime）条件下，量子修正由在经典欠阻尼频率（classical underdamped frequency）下计算的涨落零点能（zero-point energy of fluctuations）决定，与保守情形类似；在电阻电容并联分路超导约瑟夫森结（resistively and capacitively shunted superconducting Josephson junction）及细长玻色子结（elongated bosonic junction）中，实际条件下量子修正可达百分之一量级。

Conclusion: 该工作为耗散系统的量子涨落效应提供了统一的解析框架，并指出在实际超导与玻色子结器件中量子修正不可忽略。

Abstract: Using the quantum effective action in the Schwinger-Keldysh formalism, we derive quantum corrections to the semiclassical Langevin dynamics of a dissipative system governed by a macroscopic degree of freedom. We discuss the connection with the Ehrenfest theorem and show that, in the low-temperature and weak-damping regime, quantum corrections are determined by the zero-point energy of fluctuations evaluated at the classical underdamped frequency, closely paralleling the conservative case. We apply these general results to the resistively and capacitively shunted superconducting Josephson junction and to an elongated bosonic junction, where quantum corrections can reach the percent level under realistic conditions.

</details>


### [27] [Finite-temperature spin diffusion in the two-dimensional XY model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20124)
*Erik Fitzner,Byungjin Lee,Junhyeok Hur,Minseok Kim,Benedikt Schneider,Jae-yoon Choi,Björn Sbierski*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过理论与实验相结合的方式，量化了有限温度下平方晶格量子自旋-1/2 XY模型中的自旋扩散（spin diffusion）过程。理论方面采用了一种新发展的动力学高温展开方法（dynamical high-temperature expansion method），实验则基于光晶格硬核玻色子量子模拟器（optical lattice hard-core boson quantum simulator）。自旋扩散常数的理论与实验高度吻合，标志着自旋输运（spin-transport）研究突破一维限制，并定量验证了当前最先进的量子模拟平台。此外，论文还为动态自旋电导率（dynamic spin conductivity）及各向异性诱导的可积性破缺（anisotropy-induced integrability breaking）的未来实验提供了理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解有限温度下量子自旋系统中的自旋扩散行为是凝聚态物理和量子模拟领域的重要课题。此前自旋输运研究主要局限于一维系统，二维及以上维度的定量理论与实验验证尚未实现。本文旨在通过结合先进的解析方法和量子模拟实验，首次实现二维平方晶格量子自旋-1/2 XY模型中自旋扩散常数的精确量化与交叉验证。

Method: 理论方面采用动力学高温展开方法，该方法能有效捕捉流体力学区域（hydrodynamic regime）的长时空尺度行为。实验方面利用光晶格硬核玻色子量子模拟器实现平方晶格量子自旋-1/2 XY模型，通过测量得到自旋扩散常数。理论与实验结果进行定量比较。

Result: 理论与实验得到的自旋扩散常数之间实现了极好的一致性（excellent agreement）。这一结果标志着自旋输运研究突破了一维限制，并对当前最先进的量子模拟平台进行了定量验证。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了动力学高温展开方法在二维自旋扩散问题中的有效性，同时验证了光晶格量子模拟器作为定量研究工具的可靠性。论文还提供了关于动态自旋电导率和各向异性诱导可积性破缺的未来实验预测，为后续研究指明了方向。

Abstract: We present a combined theory-experiment study to quantify spin diffusion in the square lattice quantum spin-1/2 XY model at finite temperature. On the theory side, we leverage a recently developed dynamical high-temperature expansion method to faithfully capture the long spatiotemporal scales of the hydrodynamic regime. Experimental results are obtained from an optical lattice hard-core boson quantum simulator. The excellent agreement of spin diffusion constants marks a breakthrough in spin-transport beyond one dimension and for the quantitative validation of state-of-the-art quantum simulation platforms. We also provide theory predictions for future experiments on dynamic spin conductivity or anisotropy-induced integrability breaking.

</details>

### [28] [Positive Criticality and Optimal Hardy Inequality for Fractional Laplacians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19423)
*Philipp Hake,Matthias Keller,Felix Pogorzelski*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文刻画了加权图上一般拉普拉斯算子的正临界哈代权（positive critical Hardy weights），并将该结果应用于一般图上的分数阶拉普拉斯算子（fractional Laplacians），在适当假设下识别出最优哈代权（optimal Hardy weight），最后以凯莱图（Cayley graphs）、满足曲率假设的图及分形图（fractal graphs）为例进行了说明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在加权图（weighted graphs）上建立一般拉普拉斯算子（general Laplacians）的正临界哈代权的系统性刻画，并进一步将这一刻画推广到分数阶拉普拉斯算子，以在更广泛的图类中识别最优哈代权。

Method: 首先对加权图上的正临界哈代权进行特征化（characterization）；然后将该特征化结果应用于一般图上的分数阶拉普拉斯算子；最后通过凯莱图、满足曲率假设的图以及分形图三类示例验证理论结果。

Result: 给出了加权图上正临界哈代权的完整刻画，并基于该刻画在适当假设下识别出了分数阶拉普拉斯算子的最优哈代权。

Conclusion: 所建立的刻画框架适用于多种图结构（包括群凯莱图、曲率约束图及分形图），表明该方法的通用性和有效性。

Abstract: We characterize positive critical Hardy weights for general Laplacians on weighted graphs. We then apply this result to fractional Laplacians on general graphs and use the characterization to identify an optimal Hardy weight under suitable assumptions. We finally illustrate our results with examples of graphs which arise as Cayley graphs of groups, satisfy curvature assumptions or are fractal graphs.

</details>


### [29] [Algebraic Leonard trio approach to rational functions: the Hahn case](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19475)
*Nicolas Crampé,Quentin Labriet,Lucia Morey,Luc Vinet*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在 Leonard 三元组（Leonard trios）的代数框架下，对 Hahn 多项式（Hahn polynomials）的有限族及其相关的双正交有理函数（biorthogonal rational functions）进行了代数解释。通过引入三元组 Hahn 代数（trio Hahn algebra）并证明其与元 Hahn 代数（meta Hahn algebra）同构，澄清了 Leonard 三元组与元代数（meta algebras）之间的结构联系。基于差分算子（difference operators）构造了有限维实现，相关函数作为普通特征值问题本征解的重叠出现，其双谱性（bispectrality）与双正交性（biorthogonality）自然源于此代数框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为 Hahn 多项式有限族及相关双正交有理函数提供统一的代数解释，并阐明 Leonard 三元组与元代数之间的结构关联。

Method: 引入三元组 Hahn 代数，证明其与元 Hahn 代数的同构关系；通过差分算子构造有限维实现，将目标函数作为普通特征值问题本征解的重叠（overlaps）导出。

Result: 建立了 Leonard 三元组与元代数之间的同构对应；在代数框架下自然导出了相关函数的双谱性与双正交性。

Conclusion: 该代数框架有效统一了对 Hahn 多项式族及相关双正交有理函数的理解，其双谱与双正交性质可从代数结构直接推得。

Abstract: The finite families of Hahn polynomials and associated biorthogonal rational functions are interpreted algebraically in the framework of Leonard trios. We introduce the trio Hahn algebra and prove that it is isomorphic to the meta Hahn algebra, thereby clarifying the structural connection between Leonard trios and meta algebras. Finite dimensional realizations in terms of difference operators are constructed, and the functions of interest arise as overlaps between eigensolutions of ordinary eigenvalue problems. Their bispectral and biorthogonality properties follow naturally from the algebraic framework.

</details>


### [30] [Numerical approach to the modular operator for fermionic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20001)
*Henning Bostelmann,Daniela Cadamuro,Christoph Minz*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过数值方法近似计算1+1维有质量Majorana场局部子代数的Tomita-Takesaki模算子，发现模算子对质量具有非平凡依赖性，且在双锥区域中模生成元包含双局域项，其强度随质量增大而减弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子场论（quantum field theory）中，Tomita-Takesaki模算子（modular operator）是描述局部代数的关键数学对象，但其在有质量场中的行为缺乏数值研究。作者旨在通过数值方法填补这一空白，并探讨质量参数对模算子结构的影响。

Method: 采用数值方法在单粒子（one-particle）层次上近似计算模算子，通过对位置空间中t=0时刻数据进行离散化（discretisation）实现。局部子空间（local subspaces）选取为单个双锥（double cone）和两个双锥的不交并（disjoint union）。整体时空主要选择为圆柱体（cylinder）以避免边界效应，并比较了反周期（antiperiodic）和周期（periodic）两种边界条件。数值结果与无质量情形下的已知解析表达式进行了对比。

Result: 模算子对质量（mass）具有非平凡的依赖性。在两个双锥的情形下，模生成元（modular generator）不仅包含局域（local）贡献（支持在构型空间的对角线上），还包含双局域（bilocal）项（连接两个双锥区域）。双局域项在高质量时变得不显著，与理论预期一致。

Conclusion: 数值方法成功揭示了有质量Majorana场中模算子的质量依赖性，验证了双局域项随质量增大而减弱的预期。该工作为理解量子场论中局部代数的模结构提供了数值工具和定量结果。

Abstract: We numerically approximate the Tomita-Takesaki modular operator for local subalgebras of the 1+1-dimensional massive Majorana field. Our method works at the one-particle level with a discretisation of time-0 data in position space. The local subspaces we consider are associated with one double cone and with the disjoint union of two double cones. In order to avoid boundary effects, we primarily choose the overall spacetime to be a cylinder; different choices of boundary conditions (antiperiodic and periodic) are considered. We compare our numerical results to known analytic expressions in the massless case. It turns out that the modular operator has a non-trivial dependence on the mass. In the case of two double cones, the modular generator does not only have ''local'' contributions (supported on the diagonal in configuration space) but also ''bilocal'' terms (connecting the two double cone regions); we find the latter to be less prominent at higher masses, in line with expectations.

</details>


### [31] [Concurrent enforcement of polyconvexity and true-stress-true-strain monotonicity in incompressible isotropic hyperelasticity: application to neural network constitutive models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20031)
*Maximilian P. Wollner,Dominik K. Klein,Herbert Baaser,Gerhard A. Holzapfel,Patrizio Neff*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了各向同性不可压缩超弹性（isotropic incompressible hyperelasticity）的经典框架，证明了多凸性（polyconvexity）可导出真实应力-真实应变单调性，并基于此设计了四种物理增强神经网络（PANNs）。实验表明，满足相同本构约束的不同PANN参数化在校准范围内表现相近但在外推时差异显著，引发了对PANNs预测能力的批判性讨论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，物理增强神经网络（physics-augmented neural networks, PANNs）在本构建模（constitutive modeling）领域受到广泛关注。本研究旨在将本构不等式（constitutive inequalities）的最新进展与经典不可压缩超弹性理论相结合，为PANNs的架构设计提供理论指导，并评估其预测能力。

Method: 首先从理论上证明了不可压缩应变能函数（strain-energy function）的多凸性（polyconvexity）蕴含真实应力-真实应变单调性（true-stress-true-strain monotonicity），确保满足勒让德-阿达马条件（Legendre-Hadamard condition）即椭圆性（ellipticity）以及应力随应变增加而增加的原则。基于此理论结果，设计了四种不同的PANN架构，这些架构先验地（a priori）满足相同的本构约束，随后使用三组不同的实验数据对其进行校准。

Result: 不同的PANN参数化在校准范围内表现相近，但在外推（extrapolation）时表现出显著差异。这表明即便在满足相同本构约束的前提下，不同的参数化对材料行为的逼近能力（approximation power）各不相同。

Conclusion: 本文对PANNs的预测能力（predictive power）进行了批判性讨论，指出仅满足本构约束并不足以保证可靠的外推性能。这一发现对于通过神经网络建模更复杂材料行为具有重要启示意义。

Abstract: The design of physics-augmented neural networks (PANNs) for the purposes of constitutive modeling has received considerable attention as of late for a variety of material behaviors. Here, we revisit the classical framework of isotropic incompressible hyperelasticity in light of recent advances in the study of constitutive inequalities. We show that polyconvexity implies true-stress-true-strain monotonicity for a large class of incompressible strain-energy functions. The resulting elastic law obeys the physically reasonable Legendre-Hadamard (or ellipticity) condition as well as the notion of increasing stress with increasing strain. These results then inform the architecture of four distinct PANNs which are subsequently calibrated to three different sets of experimental data each. We show that different PANN parametrizations - satisfying the same constitutive constraints a priori - have varying approximation power for the description of material behavior. Moreover, even when distinct parametrizations perform comparatively well within the calibration regime, they show pronounced differences in extrapolation. This observation motivates a critical discussion about the predictive power of PANNs which also has implications for the modeling of more complex material behavior by virtue of neural networks.

</details>


### [32] [Complex deformations of the circle: Group cohomology and Virasoro uniformization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20175)
*Sid Maibach,Eveliina Peltola*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了圆微分同胚群（diffeomorphism group of the circle）的复化问题，通过考虑从圆到带孔复平面的实解析映射（winding number +1）来构造复变形，建立了其Frölicher光滑流形结构及Witt代数（Witt algebra）的李代数关系，计算了第二群上同调（second group cohomology），并证明了一个Virasoro一致化定理（Virasoro uniformization theorem），最后将复变形的作用与Fenchel-Nielsen坐标和Schiffer变分联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回答圆微分同胚群复化这一理论问题，并为了共形场论（conformal field theory）的应用而计算相关的上同调结构。

Method: 考虑从圆到带孔复平面（punctured complex plane）的实解析（real-analytic）映射，且具有winding number +1。利用Frölicher结构（Frölicher structures）定义光滑性，从李代数层面建立Witt代数关系，并通过第二群上同调计算寻找Bott-Thurston上循环（Bott-Thurston cocycle）和Gelf'and-Fuks上循环（Gelf'and-Fuks cocycle）的推广。

Result: 构建了无限维流形及其Frölicher光滑结构，并在第二群上同调中找到了推广Bott-Thurston上循环的余循环（cocycle），以及一个结合旋转数（rotation number）和共形半径（conformal radius）的自然相对余循环（relative cocycle）。证明了Virasoro一致化定理：Segal模空间（Segal moduli spaces）的切空间由Witt代数诱导的向量场张成。复变形的作用还与Fenchel-Nielsen坐标（Fenchel-Nielsen coordinates）和Schiffer变分（Schiffer variation）建立了联系。

Conclusion: 复变形为圆微分同胚群的复化提供了一种光滑无限维流形框架，并为共形场论中的模空间结构和一致化问题提供了新的技术工具。

Abstract: We approach the question of complexification of the diffeomorphism group of the circle by considering real-analytic maps from the circle into the punctured complex plane with winding number +1. Such complex deformations form an infinite-dimensional manifold with partially defined inversion and composition operations, smooth in the sense of Frölicher structures, and with Lie algebra relations at the identity given by the Witt algebra. With applications to conformal field theory in mind, we compute the second group cohomology group with real coefficients, finding cocycles extending the Bott-Thurston cocycle related to the Gelf'and-Fuks cocycle of the Virasoro algebra, and a natural relative cocycle combining the rotation number and conformal radius of a complex deformation.
  Complex deformations act naturally on the (infinite-dimensional) Segal moduli spaces of Riemann surfaces with analytically parametrized boundary components. These actions equip said moduli spaces with smooth Frölicher structures. We prove a Virasoro uniformization theorem: the tangent spaces of the Segal moduli spaces are spanned by vector fields induced by the Witt algebra. Finally, we relate the actions of complex deformations to Fenchel-Nielsen coordinates and Schiffer variation on finite-dimensional moduli spaces of hyperbolic surfaces with one marked point on each boundary component.

</details>


### [33] [On the single field formulation in magnetostatics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19126)
*Stefan Krömer,Giuseppe Tomassetti*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统讨论了静磁学（magnetostatics）的两种变分公式（variational formulations）之间的等价性：一种基于磁化强度（magnetization）和磁场（magnetic field），另一种仅使用磁感应强度（magnetic induction）。当磁学定律与弹性（elasticity）耦合形成磁弹性（magnetoelastic）模型时，该等价性仍然成立。两种公式无法通过标准凸对偶（standard convex duality）在泛函层面建立联系，且变换不要求目标泛函满足凸性和强制性（coercivity），这些性质也不一定被变换所保持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清静磁学两种变分表述之间的等价关系，并检验该关系在耦合弹性模型时是否依然稳健。此外，探究这两种表述在泛函层面能否通过标准凸对偶建立联系，以及凸性和强制性条件在变换中的作用与地位。

Method: 采用系统分析的方法，对比两种变分公式（分别以磁化强度/磁场和磁感应强度为状态变量），并通过Legendre-Fenchel变换（Legendre-Fenchel transform）在磁性状态变量层面计算材料中的磁弹性能量密度。

Result: 两种变分公式在静磁学中等价，且该等价关系在耦合弹性模型后依然成立。然而，这两种公式在泛函层面无法通过标准凸对偶相联系，并且变换既不要求泛函具有凸性和强制性，这些性质也不一定在变换后得到保持。

Conclusion: 静磁学的两种变分表述之间存在稳定的等价关系，即使与弹性耦合仍然成立；但该等价性无法归结为标准凸对偶，且凸性和强制性不是实现该变换的必要条件。

Abstract: We systematically discuss the equivalence of two variational formulations of magnetostatics, in terms of magnetization and magnetic field on the one hand and the single field formulation using only magnetic induction. To demonstrate that this link is stable also when the magnetic laws are coupled with other variational static models, elasticity is included in the models as well. Interestingly, despite the fact that the corresponding magnetoelastic energy densities in the material can be computed via Legendre-Fenchel transform in the magnetic state variables, the two formulations are not linked by standard convex duality on the level of the functionals. In addition, convexity and coercivity of the given functional are neither required for the transformation nor always preserved by it.

</details>

### [34] [Primordial Black Hole from Tensor-induced Density Fluctuation: First-order Phase Transitions and Domain Walls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15197)
*Utkarsh Kumar,Anish Ghoshal*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文分别提出了第一类相变（FOPT）和畴壁（DW）中原始黑洞（PBH）的一种新颖的、规范不变且极小的形成机制，并给出了基于现有PBH约束对相变与畴壁参数的模型无关限制，发现小行星质量PBH可构成全部暗物质，且对应的引力波信号处于LISA、SKA和ET探测器的可及范围内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有原始黑洞（PBH）形成机制通常依赖于特定模型或引入额外自由度；本文旨在提出一种更普适、规范不变且极小的PBH形成途径，并建立PBH与第一类相变（FOPT）及畴壁（DW）参数之间的直接联系。

Method: 利用微扰论中二阶张量扰动，分别从第一类相变（FOPT）中的气泡碰撞与声波、以及畴壁（DW）湮灭产生的一阶张量扰动出发，推导该扰动对曲率扰动的二阶贡献，从而形成原始黑洞（PBH）；并给出张量诱导密度谱、PBH质量与丰度的半解析公式。

Result: 小行星质量PBH可构成全部暗物质（DM），对应FOPT参数范围：$T_{\star} \in (4 \times 10^{2}, 10^{4})$ GeV、$\beta/H \simeq 6$、$\alpha > \mathcal{O}(1)$，引力波峰值振幅$\Omega_{\rm GW}^{\rm p} h^2 \sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-8})$，频率$f_{\rm p} \in (10^{-5}, 10^{-2})$ Hz（LISA/SKA可及）；DW情形：$\sigma^{1/3} \in [10^{6}, 10^{8}]$ TeV、$V_{\rm bias}^{1/4} \in [10^{7}, 10^{10}]$ MeV，引力波峰值振幅$\Omega_{\rm GW}^{\rm p} h^2 \sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-9})$，频率$f_{\rm p} \in (4 \times 10^{-4}, 10^{-1})$ Hz（LISA/ET可及）。

Conclusion: 该机制建立了PBH形成与FOPT及DW参数之间的模型无关约束，从而可将可见扇区或暗扇区中的粒子物理微观模型与PBH及引力波观测联系起来，实现多信使检验。

Abstract: We present a novel \textit{gauge-invariant and minimal} formation mechanism of primordial black holes (PBHs) in first-order phase transition (FOPT) and domain walls (DW) separately. This is based on the first-order tensor perturbations, generated during FOPT from bubble collisions \& sound waves, and from DW annihilation, sourcing curvature, at second-order in perturbation theory. We show that the PBH formation implies \textit{model-independent constraints} on FOPT parameters ($β/H, α, T_{\star}$ ) and on DW parameters, ($α_{\rm ann}, V_{\rm bias}, σ$), from existing PBH constraints. We find that asteroid mass PBHs can become the entire dark matter (DM) of the Universe, for $T_{\star} \in (4 \times 10^{2}, 10^{4})$ GeV, for $β/H \simeq 6$, involving $α>\mathcal{O}(1)$ values. The corresponding FOPT Gravitational Waves (GW) amplitude will have its characteristic peak at $Ω_{\rm GW}^{\rm p} h^2$ $\sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-8})$ between frequencies $f_{\rm p} \in ({10^{-5},10^{-2}})$ Hz which is within the reach in LISA and SKA detectors. PBH as entire DM is possible for $σ^{1/3} \in [10^{6}, 10^{8}]$ TeV, for $V_{\rm bias}^{1/4} \in [10^7, 10^{10}]$ MeV with the corresponding GW amplitude peak from DW annihilation $Ω_{\rm GW}^{\rm p} h^2$ $\sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-9})$ (for $α_{\rm ann} \sim 10^{-2}$) and peak frequencies between $f_{\rm p} \in (4 \times {10^{-4},10^{-1}})$ Hz with ($T_{\rm ann} \in 4.5 \times [10^3, 10^6] $) GeV within the reach in LISA and ET detectors. We also provide semi-analytical formulae for the tensor-induced density spectrum, $P_{δ^{(2)}}$, $M_{\rm PBH}$ and $f_{\rm PBH}$, relating them in terms of FOPT and DW parameters which in turn, are related to viable particle physics origin of such FOPT and DW, and therefore, constrain such microphysics, either in the visible, or in dark sector models.

### [35] [Expected redshift drift for tilted observers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16426)
*Franco R. de Pedro,Gabriel R. Bengochea*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文在协变1+3形式体系下，计算了具有非零本动（peculiar motion）的倾斜观测者（tilted observers）所预期的红移漂移（redshift drift），推导出该漂移由FLRW背景项和观测者本动运动学引起的方向修正项组成，并在EdS和ΛCDM两种背景下进行了定量分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 红移漂移通常仅针对随宇宙学背景共动（comoving）的观测者讨论，但实际观测中的观测者普遍具有非零本动速度，因此需要研究本动运动对红移漂移信号的影响。

Method: 采用协变1+3形式体系（covariant \(1+3\) formalism），从倾斜参考系（tilted frame）中测量的精确红移出发，推导出相应的红移漂移表达式，将其分解为FLRW背景项和由观测者本动运动学（peculiar kinematics）引起的方向修正项，后者通过本动膨胀（peculiar expansion）、投影剪切（projected shear）和投影加速度（projected acceleration）沿视线方向编码。

Result: 在爱因斯坦-德西特（Einstein–de Sitter, EdS）背景下，该分析隔离了无背景加速时倾斜的纯运动学效应；在ΛCDM背景下，定量展示了相同的各向异性修正（anisotropic corrections）如何改变标准红移漂移信号。

Conclusion: 观测者的本动运动会在标准红移漂移信号上叠加方向依赖的修正项，该效应在未来的红移漂移实测中不可忽略。

Abstract: Redshift drift is usually discussed for observers comoving with the cosmological background, but realistic observations are made by observers with nonzero peculiar motion. In this work, we calculate the expected redshift drift for tilted observers within the covariant \(1+3\) formalism. Starting from the exact redshift measured in the tilted frame, we derive the corresponding drift as an FLRW background term plus a directional correction driven by the observer's peculiar kinematics, encoded through peculiar expansion, projected shear, and projected acceleration along the line of sight. We analyse first an Einstein--de Sitter (EdS) background, which isolates the purely kinematic effect of tilt in the absence of background acceleration, and then extend the calculation to \(Λ\)CDM in order to quantify how the same anisotropic corrections deform the standard drift signal in the concordance model.
