### [36] [Recombination Thickness as an Uncertainty in Inflationary Observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19336)
*V. K. Oikonomou*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本论文指出，由于再复合时期（recombination era）具有有限持续时间（finite duration），CMB多极矩ℓ与原初波数k之间的映射本质上是概率性的，而非标准假设的确定性映射。作者将原初扰动功率谱提升为由再复合宽度导致的概率分布，引入ln k空间的高斯平滑尺度，该效应对标准幂律暴胀场景为零，但对具有奇特振荡特征的场景可能显著，且平滑效应会在谱指数及其运行、尤其是TT与EE推得的谱指数差异中产生可观测信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准CMB分析假设CMB多极矩ℓ与原初波数k之间存在直接的确定性映射（deterministic mapping）。然而，再复合时期具有有限持续时间，这一映射本质上是概率性的。论文旨在揭示这一被忽略的效应，并探讨其对原初功率谱重建的物理与观测影响。

Method: 将原初扰动功率谱提升为一种概率分布（probability distribution），归因于再复合时期的有限宽度。推导出再复合有限宽度在ln k空间中引入高斯平滑尺度（Gaussian smoothing scale），平滑幅度由σ_ln k ∼ σ_η / D_*给出。将观测到的有效功率谱视为真实原初谱经尺度重建不确定性模糊后的结果，并指出其数学上等价于对潜变量（latent variable）进行贝叶斯边际化（Bayesian marginalization），即自变量测量误差的传播。最后通过最小Fisher矩阵分析（minimal Fisher matrix analysis）考察平滑效应的可观测性前景。

Result: 平滑效应对谱指数（spectral index）及其运行（running）有可量化的影响；更重要的是，TT和EE推得的谱指数差异n_s^{TT} - n_s^{EE}在平滑效应下非零，与标准无平滑暴胀场景形成对比。该差异可能被未来CMB实验观测到，n_s^{TT} - n_s^{EE}中的任何张力（tension）都可能指示原初谱存在振荡和平滑效应。

Conclusion: 再复合有限持续时间导致的功率谱平滑效应在标准幂律暴胀场景中为零，但在具有奇特振荡特征的原初功率谱场景中可能变得重要，未来CMB实验有望对其进行探测。该效应不仅在谱指数及其运行中留下可量化印记，还通过TT与EE谱指数差异提供了一个新的观测窗口。

Abstract: Standard CMB analysis assumes a direct deterministic mapping between the multipole probed by the CMB $\ell$ and the primordial wavenumber $k$. Since the recombination era has a finite duration, this mapping is probabilistic by construction. We elevate the power spectrum of the primordial perturbations to a probability distribution caused by the finite duration of the recombination era. We show that a finite recombination width introduces a Gaussian smoothing scale in $\ln k$ with $σ_{\ln k} \sim σ_η/ D_*$, leading to a probabilistic mapping from multipoles to inflationary e-folds. This effect is zero in standard power-law inflationary scenarios, but it may become relevant for scenarios with exotic oscillating features of the primordial power spectrum, which will be probed by the future CMB experiments. The observed effective power spectrum is the true primordial spectrum blurred by the uncertainty in scale reconstruction, which is mathematically identical to a Bayesian marginalization over a latent variable, and thus there is a propagation of the measurement error in the independent variable, which is another more formal way to view the smoothing effect. Our results indicate that the smoothing has quantifiable effects on the spectral index and its running, but more importantly the difference between the TT and EE inferred spectral indices, $n_s^{TT}-n_s^{EE}$, is non-trivial, in contrast to standard inflation without smoothing, and might become observable by future cosmic microwave background experiments. Any tension in $n_s^{TT}-n_s^{EE}$ could indicate oscillations in the primordial spectrum and the effects of the power spectrum smoothing. Finally, a minimal Fisher matrix analysis is performed to investigate the observability prospects of the smoothing effect.

</details>


### [37] [Prospect of Measuring the Cosmic Dipole by Strongly Lensed Gravitational Waves Associated with Galaxy Surveys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19476)
*Anson Chen,Jun Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了利用强引力透镜化引力波事件（strongly lensed GW events）测量宇宙偶极子（cosmic dipole）的可行性。基于奇异等温球透镜模型（singular isothermal sphere lens model）对双像透镜事件的统计样本进行重建，并结合爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）和宇宙探测器（Cosmic Explorer）的模拟，预测在10年观测期内可检测到与宇宙微波背景（CMB）及计数测量一致的偶极子幅度g。通过结合双像与三像/四像透镜事件，约束精度显著提升，最乐观情形下获得g = (2.45^{+1.53}_{-1.28}) × 10^{-3}。强透镜引力波事件为宇宙偶极子测量提供了一种独立于电磁探针的新方法，兼具不同系统误差的一致性检验价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，宇宙微波背景（CMB）中观测到的宇宙偶极子（cosmic dipole）被解释为观测者相对于背景运动所致，但射电星系计数测量结果与之存在张力，亟需独立探针进行交叉验证。

Method: 利用强引力透镜化引力波（GW）事件的多重时延像推断透镜和源的距离，结合星系红移（redshift）信息编码宇宙偶极效应；基于奇异等温球（SIS）透镜模型重建统计样本，并联合估计宇宙偶极子与背景宇宙学参数。

Result: 在爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）和宇宙探测器（Cosmic Explorer）的模拟中，10年观测可探测与CMB及计数测量一致的偶极子幅度g；结合双像与三像/四像事件可大幅提升约束精度，最乐观情形下得到g = (2.45^{+1.53}_{-1.28}) × 10^{-3}。

Conclusion: 强引力透镜化引力波事件为宇宙偶极子测量提供了一种新颖方法，可作为独立于电磁探针的一致性检验工具，虽然实验挑战较大但具有独特的系统误差优势。

Abstract: The cosmic dipole observed in the cosmic microwave background (CMB) is traditionally interpreted as being caused by the observer's motion relative to the background. However, tensions with dipole measurements from radio galaxy counts motivate the need for independent probes. This work investigates the feasibility of using strongly lensed gravitational wave (GW) events to measure the cosmic dipole. Strongly lensed GWs produce multiple time-delayed images, which can be used to infer the distances to both the lens and the source. These distances, associated with the observed redshifts of the lens and the source from galaxy catalogues, encode information about the background cosmology and cosmic dipole effects. By reconstructing a statistical sample of doubly lensed GW events based on the singular isothermal sphere lens model, the cosmic dipole can be estimated jointly with background cosmological parameters. Using realistic simulations for Einstein Telescope and Cosmic Explorer, we forecast that a dipole magnitude $g$ consistent with both the CMB and number count measurement could be detected with 10 years of observation. Furthermore, constraints on $g$ are greatly improved by combining constraints from doubly lensed events with those from triply or quadruply lensed events. In the most optimistic scenario, where we measure the number count dipole magnitude with 10 years of observation, we obtain $g = (2.45^{+1.53}_{-1.28}) \times 10^{-3}$ from the combined constraint, provided that systematic uncertainties are mitigated. Although challenging, strongly lensed GWs offer a novel approach to measuring the cosmic dipole, providing an independent consistency test with different systematics from electromagnetic probes.

</details>


### [38] [Probing String-Theory-Inspired Topologies of the Early Universe through CMB Temperature and Polarization Anisotropies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19953)
*Nick E. Mavromatos,Miguel-Angel Sanchis-Lozano*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出，尽管TeV尺度弦理论已被实验排除、普朗克尺度弦理论难以直接探测，但早期宇宙的宇宙微波背景（CMB）辐射可间接检验高弦标度弦理论。通过重新分析CMB温度与偏振的角关联，特别是大角度两点关联函数，作者发现与空间宇称破缺（spatial-parity breaking）相关的可能迹象，与暴胀前GUT能标下六维额外空间紧致化（toroidal compactification）一致，并指出B模偏振（B-mode polarization）是未来实验的灵敏探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高弦标度（high-string scale）弦理论因所需能量远超当前对撞机能力而被认为难以直接检验，但早期宇宙可能通过CMB遗留印记提供间接观测窗口。本研究旨在重新审视CMB温度与偏振角关联，探测量子暴胀（inflation）前宇宙的几何与拓扑性质，以寻找弦理论预言的空间拓扑信号。

Method: 基于先前研究，重新分析CMB温度与偏振的角关联（angular correlations），特别聚焦于大角尺度上的两点关联函数（two-point correlation functions），以此探测非平凡空间拓扑（nontrivial spatial topology）的遗迹。具体考察了环面紧致化（toroidal compactification）的观测后果，并分析其对普朗克卫星（Planck satellite）提供的CMB原初功率谱（primordial power spectrum）的影响。

Result: 在现有实验与理论不确定性范围内，识别出一个与空间宇称破缺（spatial-parity breaking）相关的可能迹象，该迹象与早期宇宙在暴胀开始前GUT能标下存在六个空间额外维度（spatial extra dimensions）并发生紧致化的图景一致。

Conclusion: 研究框架可扩展至B模偏振（B-mode polarization），强调其作为灵敏探针在未来地基与空间实验中具有极高潜力，可对高弦标度弦理论进行前所未有的精确检验。

Abstract: TeV string-mass-scale strings have been excluded experimentally at colliders, as their effects have not been observed at the Large Hadron Collider (CERN). On the other hand, higher-scale string theory, with mass scales typically close to the Planck scale, is often regarded as experimentally inaccessible due to the enormous energies required for direct tests, and far beyond the reach of present or foreseeable particle accelerators. Nevertheless, the early Universe may provide an indirect observational window for high-string scale through imprints left on the Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB). In this work, building on previous studies, we reexamine temperature and polarization angular correlations as probes of the geometry and topology of the pre-inflationary Universe. We focus in particular on two-point correlation functions at large angular scales, where signatures of nontrivial spatial topology may survive as relics of primordial physics. We investigate the observational consequences of toroidal compactification and analyze their impact on the primordial power spectrum of the CMB provided by the Planck satellite. Within the current experimental and theoretical uncertainties, we identify a possible indication closely related to spatial-parity breaking, consistent with the presence of six spatial extra dimensions in the early Universe, compactified at the GUT epoch before the start of inflation. Finally, we extend our framework to B-mode polarization, highlighting its potential as a sensitive probe in forthcoming ground-based and space-borne experiments with unprecedented precision.

</details>


### [39] [Inflaton Accretion onto Primordial Black Holes During Reheating](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19825)
*Jitumani Kalita,Debaprasad Maity*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了在大爆炸核合成（Big Bang Nucleosynthesis, BBN）之前形成的原初黑洞（Primordial Black Holes, PBHs）在再加热（reheating）时期的完整生命周期，发现黑洞吸积与辐射浴的耦合会导致其质量非线性增长、寿命显著延长，并最终大幅放大其发射的随机引力波背景（Stochastic Gravitational Wave Background, SGWB）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究较少追踪原初黑洞（PBHs）在再加热时期（reheating epoch）这一由振荡暴胀子（inflaton）场衰变为主导环境的完整演化过程，尤其是黑洞吸积与辐射浴之间的耦合效应尚未被系统建模。

Method: 利用α-吸引子E模型（α-attractor E-models）将再加热初始条件解析锚定于宇宙微波背景（Cosmic Microwave Background, CMB）观测；通过将史瓦西时空（Schwarzschild spacetime）中的精确标量场解与宇宙学远区（cosmological far-zone）相匹配，导出周期平均质量吸积率，并将其耦合至增长的辐射浴。

Result: 发现吸积与辐射的联合效应导致原初黑洞（PBH）最终质量呈现高度非线性的增强；由于霍金蒸发（Hawking evaporation）时标与质量呈立方关系，接近临界失控极限（critical runaway limits）形成的黑洞寿命大幅延长；存活至辐射主导时期的黑洞在其随机引力波背景（SGWB）信号上产生多个数量级的放大。

Conclusion: 再加热时期吸积-蒸发耦合动力学显著改变了原初黑洞（PBH）的演化轨迹，存活黑洞发射的随机引力波背景（SGWB）可能成为探测早期宇宙中这类极端天体过程的独特观测窗口。

Abstract: Primordial Black Holes (PBHs) forming prior to Big Bang Nucleosynthesis evolve during the reheating epoch, an environment dominated by an oscillating inflaton field decaying into a relativistic thermal bath. In this work, we track the complete lifecycle of PBHs within this coupled inflaton-radiation background. Utilizing $α$-attractor E-models, we analytically anchor the reheating initial conditions directly to Cosmic Microwave Background observations. By matching exact scalar field solutions in a Schwarzschild spacetime to the cosmological far-zone, we derive the cycle-averaged mass accretion rate and couple it to the growing radiation bath. We find that this combined accretion induces a highly non-linear enhancement of the final PBH mass. Because the Hawking evaporation timescale scales cubically with mass, PBHs forming near their critical runaway limits experience a massive extension of their lifespans. Surviving deeper into the radiation-dominated era triggers a multi-order-of-magnitude amplification in their emitted Stochastic Gravitational Wave Background (SGWB).

</details>


### [40] [Domain-wall Quintessence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19841)
*Nobufusa Kobayashi,Yuichiro Tada,Fuminobu Takahashi,Takahiro Terada*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究一种由厚度接近或大于当前哈勃半径的平面畴壁（domain wall）结构驱动的暗能量模型，计算其对宇宙微波背景（CMB）各向异性和超新星观测的影响。通过Planck 2018数据和MCMC分析（含Pantheon+ SH0ES和DESY5样本），发现此类哈勃尺度畴壁受到观测的严格约束，其能量密度必须低于当前临界密度的10⁻⁵量级，在晚期宇宙加速中只能扮演次主导角色，观测数据更支持标准ΛCDM模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一种由哈勃尺度畴壁（domain wall）驱动的暗能量模型，该模型具有本征各向异性（intrinsic anisotropy），旨在研究其对宇宙膨胀各向异性的可能贡献及其观测可行性。

Method: 首先计算畴壁产生的各向异性CMB温度多极矩（multipoles），利用Planck 2018测量数据施加约束；随后使用MCMC方法，结合Pantheon+ SH0ES和DESY5两个Ia型超新星（Type Ia supernova）样本进行参数估计，并与标准ΛCDM模型进行对比。

Result: CMB数据将畴壁能量密度严格限制在当前临界密度的10⁻⁵量级以下，以压制四极矩（quadrupole）贡献；联合CMB和超新星数据均支持ΛCDM极限，即畴壁贡献可忽略、宇宙有效各向同性（isotropic）。

Conclusion: 哈勃尺度畴壁受到当前观测数据的严格约束，在晚期宇宙加速膨胀中只能起次主导作用，无法替代标准ΛCDM模型。

Abstract: We investigate a dark energy model driven by a planar domain-wall-like structure with a thickness comparable to, or larger than, the current Hubble radius, focusing on its intrinsic anisotropy and observational viability. Near the centre of the domain wall (DW), the spacetime is anisotropic, with distinct expansion rates parallel and perpendicular to the wall. This anisotropic structure induces direction-dependent cosmic expansion and modifies photon geodesics from cosmological sources, leaving characteristic signatures in cosmological observables. We confront the model with recent observational data. We first compute the anisotropic Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) temperature multipoles generated by the DW and impose constraints from the Planck 2018 measurements. These constraints severely limit the allowed DW abundance, requiring the DW energy density to be less than $\mathcal{O}(10^{-5})$ of the current critical density in order to suppress the quadrupole contributions. We then perform a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) analysis using Type Ia supernova (SNe Ia) data, including the Pantheon+ SH0ES and DESY5 samples, to compare the DW scenario with the standard $Λ$CDM model. We find that although the DW naturally realises anisotropic accelerated expansion, the combined constraints from the CMB and SNe Ia favour the $Λ$CDM limit, in which the DW contribution is negligible, and the universe is effectively isotropic. Our results demonstrate that a Hubble-scale domain wall is tightly constrained by current observations and can only play a subdominant role in the late-time cosmic acceleration.

</details>


### [41] [Gravitational-wave constraints on $H_0$ are robust to (putative) redshift evolution in the binary black hole mass spectrum at current sensitivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20112)
*Alessandro Agapito,Viola De Renzis,Michele Mancarella*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文利用GWTC-4.0双黑洞目录重新审视了谱线警笛（spectral-siren）宇宙学对哈勃常数$H_0$的约束，明确允许质量谱的主质量标度随红移演化。研究发现当前灵敏度下无显著演化证据，演化引起的系统不确定性小于质量谱替代描述方式（如谱特征数量与函数形式）带来的影响，表明$H_0$约束对红移演化具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 谱线警笛宇宙学通过引力波观测约束哈勃常数$H_0$时，红移演化（redshift evolution）被认为是潜在的系統誤差源。该研究旨在系统评估质量谱红移演化对$H_0$测量的影响程度。

Method: 利用GWTC-4.0双黑洞（binary black hole）目录，在标准参数化质量模型中明确允许主质量标度随红移演化，进行谱线警笛约束分析，并结合注入研究（injection studies）验证结果。

Result: 当前灵敏度下未发现质量谱演化的显著证据；允许演化使$H_0$后验向低值产生非统计显著的微小偏移；演化引起的系统误差小于质量谱替代描述方式（如谱特征数量、函数形式）带来的不确定性；注入研究表明该偏移在非演化总体用演化模型分析时即可重现。

Conclusion: 在当前灵敏度下，谱线警笛对$H_0$的约束在研究所考虑的灵活性范围内对质量谱红移演化具有鲁棒性；偏移的方向和幅度可能随探测器灵敏度与红移覆盖范围变化。

Abstract: Spectral-siren cosmology constrains the Hubble constant $H_0$ using gravitational-wave observations of compact-binary coalescences. The method combines luminosity distances inferred from the waveform with redshift information statistically encoded in population features of the source-frame mass spectrum. Because the detector measures redshifted masses, structure in the intrinsic mass distribution acts as an internal ``ruler'', making the inference sensitive to assumptions about the population model. In particular, redshift evolution of the mass spectrum is widely discussed as a potential systematic for $H_0$ measurements. We revisit spectral-siren constraints with the GWTC-4.0 binary black hole catalog, explicitly allowing the main mass scales of a standard parametric mass model to evolve with redshift. We find no compelling evidence for evolution at current sensitivity. Allowing evolution produces a modest, non--statistically--significant shift of the $H_0$ posterior toward lower values, which we interpret with targeted posterior and event-level diagnostics. Importantly, the associated systematic uncertainty is subdominant to that induced by alternative redshift-independent descriptions of the mass spectrum, such as the number of spectral features and the functional form used to model them. Our results indicate that, at current sensitivity, spectral-siren constraints on $H_0$ are robust to redshift evolution of the mass spectrum within the flexibility explored here. Using injection studies, we show that this mild $H_0$ shift is reproduced when a non-evolving underlying population is analyzed with an evolving model, consistent with an over-flexible population description at the present signal-to-noise. The sign and magnitude of the shift can, however, depend on detector sensitivity and redshift reach as the population features become increasingly constrained directly by the data.

</details>

### [42] [Imaging stripe dynamics in trilayer nickelate La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18954)
*Uladzislau Mikhailau,Luke Rhodes,Siri A. Berge,Matthias Hepting,Masahiko Isobe,Carolina A. Marques,Pascal Puphal,Peter Wahl*

TL;DR: 本文利用自旋极化扫描隧道显微镜（spin-polarised scanning tunnelling microscopy）对三层镍基超导体 La₄Ni₃O₁₀ 中的条纹有序（stripe order）进行了实空间成像，发现其具有与铜氧化物超导体（cuprate superconductors）相似的周期结构（四个晶胞周期）和能隙（~66 meV），并首次在原子尺度上观测到了条纹动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自镍基超导体（nickelate superconductors）中的高温超导现象被发现以来，其超导态与铜氧化物超导体（cuprate superconductors）的相似程度一直是一个悬而未决的问题。铜氧化物高温超导相图中的一个显著特征是条纹有序（stripe order），但此前实空间成像仅限于电荷（charge）领域，缺乏对磁有序结构的直接观测。

Method: 采用自旋极化扫描隧道显微镜（spin-polarised scanning tunnelling microscopy）对三层镍基超导体 La₄Ni₃O₁₀ 中由条纹有序（stripe order）引发的局域磁和电荷分布（local magnetic and charge distribution）进行可视化成像。

Result: 条纹有序呈现出四个晶胞（four unit cell）的周期结构，与铜氧化物中的条纹高度相似；该有序在费米能级（Fermi level）处打开了一个接近完整的约 66 meV 的能隙（gap）；当隧穿电子（tunneling electrons）能量超过约 20 meV 阈值时，可触发离散的相位滑移（discrete phase slips），从而在原子尺度实现条纹动力学（stripe dynamics）的成像。

Conclusion: 这些结果突显了关联物理（correlation physics）在镧基镍氧化物（lanthanum nickelates）中驱动类条纹有序的重要性，并与铜氧化物超导体展现出引人注目的相似性。

Abstract: Since the discovery of high-temperature superconductivity in nickelate superconductors, it is an open question how closely the superconducting state resembles that of cuprate superconductors. One salient feature of the phase diagram of the high-temperature cuprate superconductors is stripe order. Despite their prevalence, real-space imaging has been limited to the charge sector. Here we use spin-polarised scanning tunnelling microscopy to visualize the local magnetic and charge distribution emerging due to a stripe order in the trilayer nickelate La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$. The stripe order exhibits a four unit cell periodicity, closely resembling that seen in cuprates, and opens a near-complete $\sim66\mathrm{meV}$ gap at the Fermi level. Crucially, discrete phase slips can be triggered by tunneling electrons above a $\sim 20\mathrm{meV}$ threshold, allowing imaging of stripe dynamics at the atomic scale. These results highlight the importance of correlation physics driving stripe-like orders in lanthanum nickelates with striking similarities to the cuprates.

*I. V. Lukin,M. O. Luhanko,Yu. V. Slyusarenko,A. G. Sotnikov*

TL;DR: 本文通过角转移矩阵重整化群（CTMRG）和无限螺旋投影纠缠对态（iPEPS）方法，系统研究了蜂巢晶格上 J₁-J₂ 反铁磁 XY 模型的基态性质与相图，识别出 Néel、Ising、共线（collinear）及非公度螺旋（incommensurate spiral）等主要相，并揭示了各相之间的转变行为，特别是共线相到非公度螺旋相的二阶相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在蜂巢晶格上，J₁-J₂ 反铁磁 XY 模型由于竞争相互作用（competing interactions）而呈现丰富的磁性序和相变行为，现有数值方法对该模型的全面刻画尚不充分。本文旨在通过高精度张量网络方法填补这一空白。

Method: 采用两种互补的张量网络方法：基于双位点单胞的角转移矩阵重整化群（CTMRG）算法和无限螺旋投影纠缠对态（iPEPS）变分波函数，用于计算基态能量和刻画相图。

Conclusion: 本文建立了蜂巢晶格 J₁-J₂ 反铁磁 XY 模型的完整基态相图，排除了二聚化序在该竞争区域占优的可能性，并明确了共线相到非公度螺旋相的连续相变性质。

Abstract: We study ground-state properties and phase diagram of the $J_{1}$-$J_{2}$ antiferromagnetic XY model on the honeycomb lattice by means of the developed corner transfer matrix renormalization group algorithm with the two-site unit cell and the infinite spiral projected entangled pair states ansatz. We identify the main phases: Néel, Ising, collinear, and incommensurate spiral phases, as well as the transitions between them, as functions of the ratio $J_{2}/J_{1}$. In the regime of competing types of ordering, we show that the energies of the dimerized states are systematically higher than the energies in the collinear phase. This collinear phase transforms to the incommensurate spiral phase through the second-order phase transition upon a further increase of $J_2/J_1$.

*Chengxiang Ding,Long Zhang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 临界点位于Q_c=0.310(11)；临界指数包括y_s=0.81(4)，反铁磁序参量的标度维数Δ_s=0.660(15)，价键固体序参量的标度维数Δ_v=0.204(14)。

Abstract: We investigate the boundary phases of a (2+1)-dimensional quantum critical Heisenberg model with a dangling spin chain. By introducing a multispin $Q$-term along the boundary, we drive a continuous boundary transition from an antiferromagnetic (AF) order to a valence-bond solid (VBS) order. Using large-scale quantum Monte Carlo simulations, we locate the critical point at $Q_{c}=0.310(11)$, and obtain the critical exponents at $Q_{c}$, including $y_{s}=0.81(4)$ and the scaling dimensions of AF and VBS order parameters $Δ_{s}=0.660(15)$ and $Δ_{v}=0.204(14)$. The weak long-range AF order for $Q<Q_{c}$ is stabilized by quasi-long-range effective interactions mediated by the critical bulk state, while the VBS phase restores the ordinary critical behavior. Our findings highlight the synergy between topological terms and quasi-long-range interactions in low-dimensional quantum many-body systems.

### [45] [Higher-order Weyl nodes driven by helical magnetic order in EuAgAs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19347)
*Jian-Rui Soh,Ziming Zhu,Louis Withers,J. Alberto Rodríguez-Velamazán,Timur K. Kim,Oscar Fabelo,Anne Stunault,Daniil Yevtushynsky,Dharmalingam Prabhakaran,Shengyuan A. Yang,Andrew T. Boothroyd*

TL;DR: 本研究通过中子衍射、共振弹性X射线散射、球形中子极化测量和第一性原理计算，系统表征了六方磷族化合物EuAgAs中耦合的磁有序与电子结构。实验发现该材料存在两次连续磁相变（TN1 = 12 K, TN2 = 8 K），其磁结构为沿c轴的横向螺旋（transverse helix），周期约为c晶格常数的两倍。计算预测该螺旋相会诱导能带折叠效应并产生有效高阶外尔节点（higher-order Weyl nodes），但由于计算费米能级（Fermi energy, EF）高于角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）测得的EF位置，这些拓扑特征未能被实验探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁性拓扑半金属（magnetic topological semimetals）为研究长程磁序如何改变电子能带结构并产生新型准粒子（如外尔费米子）提供了重要平台。六方磷族化合物EuAgAs的磁基态此前一直不明确，亟需对其耦合的磁有序与电子结构进行深入表征。

Method: 采用中子衍射（neutron diffraction）和共振弹性X射线散射（resonant elastic X-ray scattering）确定磁有序序列与传播矢量；利用球形中子极化测量（spherical neutron polarimetry）解析磁结构的具体构型；结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）预测螺旋相中能带折叠效应和拓扑节点特征。

Result: 在EuAgAs中观察到两次连续磁相变：TN1 = 12 K和TN2 = 8 K，对应两个略微不同的磁传播矢量（magnetic propagation vectors）。磁结构确定为沿c轴的横向螺旋，周期约为c晶格常数的两倍。第一性原理计算预测该螺旋相存在微弱的能带折叠效应和有效高阶外尔节点，但这些拓扑特征出现在计算费米能级附近，而该能量高于角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）测得的实际EF位置，因此在本研究中无法被实验探测。

Conclusion: EuAgAs展现出罕见的横向螺旋磁有序及两次连续相变，是研究磁序与拓扑电子结构耦合的新体系。虽然计算预测存在高阶外尔节点，但理论EF与实验EF的不一致使得实验验证仍需进一步研究，可能需要通过元素掺杂等手段调节电子填充以探测其拓扑特性。

Abstract: Magnetic topological semimetals provide a fertile ground for exploring how long-range magnetic order can alter electronic band structures and generate novel quasiparticles such as Weyl fermions. Here, we investigate the coupled magnetic and electronic structure of single-crystalline EuAgAs, a hexagonal pnictide whose magnetic ground state has remained elusive. Using neutron diffraction and resonant elastic X-ray scattering, we identify an unusual magnetic ordering sequence with two successive phase transitions at $T_\mathrm{N1} = 12$ K and $T_\mathrm{N2} = 8$ K. We observe two slightly different magnetic propagation vectors, one associated with $T_\mathrm{N1}$ and the other with $T_\mathrm{N2}$. Spherical neutron polarimetry reveals that the magnetic structure is a transverse helix aligned along the $c$ axis with a period that is approximately twice the $c$ lattice parameter. First-principles calculations for the helical phase predict subtle band folding effects and the emergence of effective higher-order Weyl nodes. These topological features appear near the calculated Fermi energy $E_{\mathrm{F}}$ which, however, lies above the position of $E_{\mathrm{F}}$ obtained from angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy so could not be probed in this study.

### [46] [Green's Function-Free Formalism of Projective Truncation Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19404)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前期工作中，投影截断近似（projected truncation approximation, PTA）已被发展为一种系统且可控的方法，用于截断量子或经典多体哈密顿量下格林函数（Green's functions, GFs）的运动方程。本文旨在将PTA重新表述为一种不依赖于GF的、针对约化密度矩阵（reduced density matrices, RDMs）的自洽理论。

Method: 本文分别讨论了如何确定动力学矩阵${\bf M}$以及从中求解物理量的问题。通过阐明${\bf M}$的性质，将PTA方程的解构造成一个过约束优化（over-constrained optimization）问题。在此框架下，进一步讨论了替代内积方案（alternative inner product）、广义位力定理（generalized virial theorem）、广义维克定理（generalized Wick's theorem）以及PTA静态分量问题等议题。

Result: 成功将PTA重新表述为一种不依赖格林函数的约化密度矩阵自洽理论，并揭示了PTA与变分RDM理论（variational RDM theory）之间的内在联系。

Conclusion: 该新形式架起了PTA与变分RDM理论之间的桥梁，为多体问题的数值求解提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: In previous works, the projected truncation approximation (PTA) was developed as a systematic and controlled method to truncate the equation of motion of Green's functions (GFs) for a given quantum or classical many-body Hamiltonian. The static averages are obtained self-consistently with the GF through the spectral theorem. In this work, PTA is reformulated as a self-consistent theory for the reduced density matrices (RDMs) without reference to GF. We separately discuss the issues of determining the dynamical matrix ${\bf M}$ and solving the physical quantities from it. The properties of ${\bf M}$ is clarified and the solution of PTA equations is cast into an over-constrained optimization problem. This makes connection of the present theory to the variational RDM theory. We discuss various issues of PTA under this formalism, including the scheme of alternative inner product, the generalized virial theorem, the generalized Wick's theorem, and the static component problem of PTA.

### [47] [Fractonic Constraints and Magnetic Order in a Dipole-Conserving Spin Chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19421)

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）模拟结合大规模对角化（large-scale diagonalization）方法，分析序参量（order parameters）、纠缠谱（entanglement spectrum）和动力学谱函数（dynamical spectral functions）等特征量。

Result: 系统稳定存在反铁磁偶极有序基态（在自旋对层面而非单个自旋层面有序化）；大伊辛相互作用强度下发生从偶极有序相到自旋反铁磁相的相变；铁磁伊辛相互作用下同时存在反铁磁和铁磁偶极有序相；足够负的相互作用下偶极有序相转变为具有常规自旋铁磁序的铁磁相。

Abstract: This work investigates the competition between dipole conservation, which imposes strong dynamical constraints and prevents the propagation of isolated spin excitations, and Ising-type interactions that favor ordering. Specifically, we explore the ground state phase diagram of a one-dimensional spin chain in the presence of both fractonic constraints and interactions. Despite the kinetic constraints, the system stabilizes an antiferromagnetic dipole-ordered ground state, where the ordering occurs at the level of spin pairs rather than individual spins. At a large Ising interaction strength, the model undergoes a phase transition from a dipole-ordered phase to a spin antiferromagnetic phase. In contrast, for ferromagnetic Ising interactions, the model exhibits both antiferromagnetic and ferromagnetic dipole ordered phases. At sufficiently large negative interaction strength, the dipole ordered phase transitions to a ferromagnetic phase with conventional spin ferromagnetic order. To characterize these distinct phases, we employ density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) simulations alongside large-scale diagonalization. We analyze appropriate order parameters, along with features of the entanglement spectrum and dynamical spectral functions. In limiting cases, the observed transitions can be understood by mapping the dipole conserving model onto effective XXZ models in a restricted Hilbert space of composite spins.

### [48] [Filling-Sensitive Spectral Complexity from Hilbert-Space Holonomy in Fragmented Non-Hermitian Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19740)
*Jiong-Hao Wang,Maria Zelenayova,Christopher Ekman,Emil J. Bergholtz*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出希尔伯特空间和乐（Hilbert-space holonomy）为破碎非厄米多体系统中的谱实性提供了几何组织原则，补充了传统的对称性保护机制。在两种最小破碎模型中，复谱仅出现在最高对称性扇区；通过将非互易跳跃振幅视为 Krylov 图上的离散规范场，解释了对角相似变换能否将系统化为厄米极限的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示非厄米多体系统中谱实性（spectral reality）的深层几何机制，超越传统的对称性保护（symmetry protection）解释，理解为何在某些扇区谱为实而在其他扇区为复。

Method: 分析两种最小破碎非厄米多体模型（费米子模型和自旋链），考察不同对称性扇区下的谱实性；将非互易跳跃振幅（nonreciprocal hopping amplitudes）重新解释为 Krylov 图（Krylov graph）上的离散规范场（discrete gauge field），基于和乐（holonomy）是否平凡判断是否存在对角相似变换（diagonal similarity transformation）至厄米极限。

Result: 复谱仅出现在最高对称性扇区：费米子模型的半填充（half filling）扇区和自旋链的零磁化（zero magnetization）扇区；增减一个粒子或翻转一个自旋即可使谱完全变为实数；平凡和乐（trivial holonomy）允许对角相似变换将系统映射至厄米极限，非平凡和乐（nontrivial holonomy）阻碍该变换从而允许复谱存在。

Conclusion: 希尔伯特空间和乐构成了破碎非厄米系统中谱实性的几何组织原则，在特定条件下平凡和乐可对应 emergent-boundary 解释，更长程模型中的实谱与复谱区域也受同一判据支配。

Abstract: We show that Hilbert-space holonomy provides a geometric organizing principle for spectral reality in fragmented non-Hermitian many-body systems, complementary to conventional symmetry protection. In two minimal fragmented models, complex spectra can arise only within the most symmetric sectors: half filling in the fermion model and zero magnetization in the spin chain. Adding or removing a single particle, or flipping a single spin, renders the spectra entirely real despite unchanged periodic boundary conditions, reminiscent of boundary-condition sensitivity in systems with a non-Hermitian skin effect. We explain this by viewing nonreciprocal hopping amplitudes as a discrete gauge field on the Krylov graph: trivial holonomy permits a diagonal similarity transformation to the Hermitian limit, whereas nontrivial holonomy obstructs it and allows complex spectra. In certain regimes, trivial holonomy admits an emergent-boundary interpretation, and longer-range models exhibit finite real and complex regions governed by the same criterion.

*Alejandro S. Miñarro,Gervasi Herranz*

Method: 将传播子和响应顶点通过与集体模式的相互作用进行动力学 dressing，从而将多体集体涨落的贡献纳入量子几何的量子偶极涨落框架。以贝里曲率（Berry curvature）为焦点，通过非弹性散射谱中的反对称通道来区分集体涨落与裸能带几何贡献。

Conclusion: 量子几何的图像可从裸带间混合扩展至包含多体集体涨落的动力学框架，后者在响应函数中产生可实验区分的贡献，并揭示了非对易性与非局域时间相互作用作为曲率生成元的新机制。

Abstract: Quantum geometry characterizes the variation of wavefunctions in momentum space through their overlaps and relative phases, providing a general framework for understanding many transport and optical properties. It is generally formulated in terms of interband matrix elements, which, entering the response functions, allow obtaining experimental access to the quantum geometric tensor. Recently, it has been emphasized that quantum geometry can also be interpreted in terms of quantum dipole fluctuations in the ground state driven by interband mixing. Here, we extend this picture to include contributions from many-body collective fluctuations, in which propagators and response vertices are dressed dynamically by the interaction with collective modes. Focusing on the Berry curvature, we show that contributions from collective fluctuations can be experimentally distinguished from bare band-geometric contributions, via specific antisymmetric channels in inelastic scattering spectra. We further identify the non-commutative properties of transverse quantum fluctuations as well as non-local-time interactions as the generators of this dynamical curvature in the susceptibility response.

### [53] [Itinerant Nature of Spin-Density-Wave Order in Ruddlesden-Popper Nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20148)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究的关键在于NiO₂块的多层镜面结构（multilayer mirror structure），它将低能电子态组织为镜面偶（mirror-even）和镜面孔（mirror-odd）两个区。研究表明，镜面相反的能带之间的主导能带间嵌套（interband nesting）驱动了一种镜面选择性的巡游SDW不稳定性。

Result: 该SDW的集体模式自然地复现了实验观测到的类似自旋波的谱。在La₄Ni₃O₁₀中，SDW进一步诱导出次生的镜面偶电荷密度波（CDW），产生了交织的自旋和电荷纹理（intertwined spin and charge textures）。

Conclusion: 多层镍氧化物中的磁性本质上是巡游而非局域磁矩起源，镜面选择性的能带间SDW序可作为这些体系中磁关联的统一组织原则。

Abstract: The nature of magnetism in layered Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates remains a central open question, particularly in light of recent observations of spin-wave-like magnetic excitations in metallic multilayer compounds. Here, we develop a unified itinerant description of spin-density-wave (SDW) order and magnetic excitations in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ and La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$. The essential ingredient is the multilayer mirror structure of the NiO$_2$ blocks, which organizes the low-energy electronic states into mirror-even and mirror-odd sectors. We show that dominant interband nesting between mirror-opposite bands drives a mirror-selective itinerant SDW instability, whose collective modes naturally reproduce the experimentally observed spin-wave-like spectra. In La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$, the SDW further induces a secondary mirror-even charge density wave, yielding intertwined spin and charge textures. Our results demonstrate that magnetism in multilayer nickelates is fundamentally itinerant rather than local-moment in origin, and establish mirror-selective interband SDW order as a unifying organizing principle for magnetic correlations in these systems.

</details>


### [54] [Controlled expansion for correlated electrons with concentrated kinematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20171)
*Pavel A Nosov,Eslam Khalaf,Patrick Ledwith*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种适用于强局域相互作用系统的系统性展开方法，通过小参数s²控制动量空间区域大小，实现了对响应函数（包括有限直流输运）的解析计算。通过三个应用实例（Hubbard模型、关联跳跃模型、Chern带模型）展示了该方法的有效性，为强关联系统中诸多难题的解决开辟了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联系统中强局域相互作用的解析处理极具挑战性，现有方法难以同时解析计算响应函数（response functions）和有限直流输运（finite DC transport）。本文旨在发展一种受控的、可解析计算的系统化展开框架，以填补这一空白。

Method: 该方法基于一个小参数s²，它度量理论动力学集中所在的动量空间（momentum space）区域面积。在实空间（real space）中，这对应于幅度随长度尺度1/s衰减、在二维中量级为s²的单粒子或关联跳跃项。当s² ≪ 1时，长程自避让隧穿路径主导，使得各种物理量可进行系统化受控计算。

Result: 三个应用实例表明：(i) 在色散集中的Hubbard模型中，解析得到谱展宽（spectral broadening）正比于s²，识别出高温T-线性电阻率（T-linear resistivity）的坏金属（bad metal）态与参数长寿命准粒子共存，以及中间温度的"热FL*"相；(ii) 在关联跳跃模型中揭示了电子-三子（electron-trion）动力学；(iii) 在Chern带模型中实现了Mott半金属（Mott semimetal），并计算了电子与三子谱函数的展宽。

Conclusion: 该方法为强关联系统中诸多挑战性问题（如有限温度输运、准粒子寿命、反常金属态等）的解析处理铺平了道路，并可推广至多种广义情形。

Abstract: We introduce a systematic expansion tailored to systems with strong local interactions and capable of computing response functions, including finite DC transport, analytically. The expansion is controlled by a small parameter $s^2$ that measures the area of the momentum space region where kinematics of the theory is concentrated. In real space, this corresponds to single-particle or correlated hopping terms with amplitudes that decay over a length scale $1/s$ and scale in magnitude as $s^2$ in two dimensions. In the limit $s^2\ll 1$, long, self-avoiding tunneling paths dominate over paths revisiting the same site. This enables systematic controlled calculations of various physical quantities. We illustrate the method with three applications. (i) A Hubbard model with concentrated dispersion: we analytically obtain spectral broadening which scales as $s^2$ and identify a high-temperature bad metal with $T$-linear resistivity coexisting with parametrically long-lived quasiparticles, as well as an intermediate-temperature "thermal FL*" with a small hole pocket that coexists with thermally disordered fluctuating local moments, all within a single controlled framework. (ii) A correlated-hopping model with interesting electron-trion dynamics. (iii) A model of Chern bands with concentrated Berry curvature, motivated by twisted bilayer graphene, which realizes a Mott semimetal where we compute the broadening for the electron and trion spectral functions. At the end, we discuss how our approach paves the way to addressing various challenging questions in strongly correlated systems and outline its various generalizations.

</details>


### [55] [Band Structure and topology of a periodically deformed Kitaev honeycomb model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20181)
*Abdullah AlJishi,Ali AlSwaid,Moayad Ekhwan,Hocine Bahlouli,Raditya Weda Bomantara,Michael Vogl*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了六边形对称形变（deformation）与磁场对蜂窝状Kitaev模型（honeycomb Kitaev model）的联合影响，发现形变缩小了布里渊区（Brillouin zone）并打开了新的能隙，磁场则破坏了时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry），引发了多重能隙闭合与开启以及丰富的拓扑相变，并表现出非平庸的陈数（Chern numbers）和潜在的热霍尔效应（thermal Hall effect）或能斯特响应（Nernst-type response）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受量子自旋液体（spin liquids）、拓扑相（topological phases）以及形变工程（deformation engineering）兴起的研究趋势推动，本文旨在探索形变与磁场在蜂窝状Kitaev模型中的协同效应，以揭示形变物理与量子自旋液体交汇处可能出现的丰富物理现象。

Method: 首先提出一种简化的未形变基模型解法，并将其推广到包含周期形变的情形；随后在Kitaev模型中引入类似摩尔（moiré）物理的六边形对称周期形变，分析其对能带结构的影响；最后引入磁场以破坏时间反演对称性，系统地研究拓扑性质。

Result: 形变导致布里渊区缩小并在新边界处出现能隙，暗示潜在的拓扑转变；磁场的引入在特定参数条件下引发了多次能隙闭合与重新打开；拓扑性质分析发现了非平庸的陈数和大量的拓扑相变；结果预示可能存在热霍尔效应或能斯特型响应。

Conclusion: 本文结果证明了形变与自旋液体物理之间的相互作用可以产生丰富的现象学；同时提出了一种测量陈数的体方法（bulk measurement approach）以及可能的物理实现路径，为后续实验和理论提供了基础。

Abstract: Motivated by the growing interest in spin liquids and topological phases, as well as the rise of deformation engineering, we study the combined effects of deformation and magnetic fields on the honeycomb Kitaev model. The Kitaev model, as one of the prototypical and exactly solvable spin liquid-hosting models, serves as a simple platform that demonstrates the rich physics one can expect at the intersection of deformation physics and quantum spin liquids. Our work builds on a simplified solution to the undeformed base model that we present. This simplified solution allows for a straightforward extension of our analysis to the deformed case. After incorporating periodic deformations into the Kitaev model (chosen for its similarity to moiré physics), we investigate the effects of a hexagonally symmetric deformation on the band structure. We find that deformation leads to a smaller Brillouin zone with new band gaps at the edges, indicating the potential for topological transitions. Finally, we introduce a magnetic field to break time-reversal symmetry and thereby allow for non-trivial topology. We find that, under specific parameter conditions, the magnetic field leads to multiple band-gap closings and openings. An investigation into topological properties reveals nontrivial Chern numbers and a plethora of topological transitions. Our results suggest possible thermal Hall or Nernst-type responses. We also suggest a potential bulk measurement approach for he Chern numbers and possible path to physical realization. Most importantly, our results serve as a demonstration of the rich phenomenology that can arise due to the interplay between deformation and spin-liquid physics.

</details>

### [56] [Hypothesis Tests for Observing Quantum Entanglement in HWW at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19754)
*Vincent Alexander Croft,Lennart Voelz,Andrii Vak,Andre Sopczak,Carsten Burgard*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用条件去噪扩散概率模型（cDDPM）在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上检验希格斯玻色子衰变至W玻色子对中的量子纠缠的新实验策略，通过连续形式的CGLMP不等式和扩散重建方法，在HL-LHC亮度目标下可达到超过5σ的显著性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于贝尔算符（Bell operators）期望值的理论方法对异常值和探测器效应高度敏感，难以在真实对撞机环境中稳健地检验希格斯玻色子衰变中的量子纠缠（quantum entanglement）。

Method: 引入CGLMP不等式的连续形式（continuous formulation），以支持纠缠态与可分离态之间的标准假设检验。针对$H \rightarrow WW^* \rightarrow \ellν\ellν$通道中不可见中微子动量的重建问题，采用条件去噪扩散概率模型（conditional denoising diffusion probabilistic models, cDDPM）提供无偏的多维展开（unfolding），并利用RooFit中的剖面似然假设检验（profile likelihood hypothesis tests）评估重建性能。

Result: 扩散方法能够在真实对撞机环境中实现量子纠缠的稳健假设检验；在约555 fb$^{-1}$积分亮度下可达到3σ证据，在1600 fb$^{-1}$下可超过5σ，完全在HL-LHC预期亮度目标范围内。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于扩散模型的实验策略为在高能对撞机上检验希格斯玻色子衰变中的量子纠缠提供了可行且鲁棒的途径，有望在高亮度大型强子对撞机（HL-LHC）上实现高显著性的验证。

Abstract: We present a novel experimental strategy for testing quantum entanglement in Higgs boson decays to $W$ boson pairs at the Large Hadron Collider. Unlike theoretical approaches that rely on expectation values of Bell operators, which are highly sensitive to outliers and detector effects, we introduce a continuous formulation of the CGLMP inequality that enables standard hypothesis testing between entangled and separable states. To overcome the fundamental challenge of reconstructing invisible neutrino momenta in the $H \rightarrow WW^* \rightarrow \ellν\ellν$ channel, we employ conditional denoising diffusion probabilistic models (cDDPM), which provide unbiased, multidimensional unfolding applicable to the full measured dataset, including backgrounds. We evaluate the diffusion-based reconstruction against analytical methods through profile likelihood hypothesis tests implemented in RooFit, with systematic uncertainties from background normalisation and unfolding shape fully propagated. Our results demonstrate that the diffusion-based approach enables robust hypothesis testing of quantum entanglement in a realistic collider environment, with 3$σ$ evidence of quantum entanglement projected at approximately 555~fb$^{-1}$ and exceeding 5$σ$ at 1600~fb$^{-1}$ to be well within the expected limits of the HL-LHC luminosity targets.

</details>

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上采集的44.55 fb⁻¹ e⁺e⁻碰撞数据，首次测量了3.51至4.95 GeV能区内五十六个质心能量点下e⁺e⁻ → K⁺Ξ⁰\barΣ⁻反应的Born截面，并首次观测到ψ(3770) → K⁺Ξ⁰\barΣ⁻过程（统计显著性6.0σ），这是首个在开粲阈值以上观测到的矢量粲偶素（vector charmonium）的无粲三体重子衰变。其他粲偶素（charmonium-like）态未观测到显著信号，并给出了相应的分支比与电子部分宽度乘积的90%置信度上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粲偶素（charmonium）的无粲（charmless）三体重子衰变是理解强相互作用中重子产生机制的重要探针，但此前在开粲阈值（open-charm threshold）以上从未被观测到。本研究旨在通过高统计量e⁺e⁻碰撞数据，首次测量e⁺e⁻ → K⁺Ξ⁰\barΣ⁻反应的Born截面，并探索相关矢量粲偶素态在此衰变道中的信号。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上采集的44.55 fb⁻¹ e⁺e⁻碰撞数据，在3.51至4.95 GeV范围内的五十六个质心能量点处，测量了e⁺e⁻ → K⁺Ξ⁰\barΣ⁻反应的Born截面（Born cross sections）。通过对着装截面（dressed cross sections）进行拟合，提取了各粲偶素态的贡献及统计显著性。

Result: 首次测量了五十六个质心能量点下的Born截面；首次观测到ψ(3770) → K⁺Ξ⁰\barΣ⁻过程，统计显著性为6.0σ（包含系统误差）；未观测到ψ(4040)、ψ(4160)、Y(4230)、Y(4360)、ψ(4415)、Y(4500)、Y(4660)或Y(4710)的显著信号，并给出了各态分支比与电子部分宽度乘积的90%置信度上限；给出了本工作与先前e⁺e⁻ → K⁰_S\barΞ⁻Σ⁻及K⁻\barΞ⁺\barΣ⁰测量结果的Born截面比值。

Conclusion: 这是首次在开粲阈值以上观测到矢量粲偶素的无粲三体重子衰变，为研究粲偶素衰变机制和重子产生提供了新实验数据。各粲偶素态未观测信号的上限结果以及截面比值可用于检验同位旋对称性（isospin symmetry）相关的理论预言。

Abstract: Using 44.55 fb$^{-1}$ of $e^+e^-$ collision data collected by the BESIII detector at the BEPCII collider, we report the first measurement of the Born cross sections for the $e^+e^- \to K^+Ξ^0\barΣ^-$ reaction at fifty-six center-of-mass energies between 3.51 and 4.95~GeV. A fit to the dressed cross sections reveals the first observation of the $ψ(3770) \to K^+Ξ^0\barΣ^-$ process, with a statistical significance of 6.0$σ$ including systematic uncertainties. This result represents the first observation of charmless three-body baryonic decay of a vector charmonium state above the open-charm threshold. No significant signals for other charmonium(-like) states i.e., $ψ(4040)$, $ψ(4160)$, $Y(4230)$, $Y(4360)$, $ψ(4415)$, $Y(4500)$, $Y(4660)$ or $Y(4710)$ are observed, and the upper limits for the product of the branching fraction and the electronic partial width at the 90% confidence level for each assumed charmonium(-like) state are provided. Additionally, the ratios of Born cross sections between this work and the previous measurements of $e^+e^- \to K^{0}_{S}\barΞ^{-}Σ^-$ and $K^-\barΞ^+\barΣ^0$ are provided, which can be used to validate theoretical predictions related to isospin symmetry.

</details>


### [58] [Search for soft unclustered energy patterns containing muons in the final state in $pp$ collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20015)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用ATLAS探测器在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上采集的140 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据（√s = 13 TeV），搜索了由强耦合隐藏扇区（hidden sector）理论预言、包含末态缪子（muon）的软非团簇能量模式（SUEP）。未发现超出标准模型（Standard Model）预期的显著信号，并对不同质量标量 mediator 的SUEP衰变分支比设置了排除上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软非团簇能量模式（SUEP）是强耦合隐藏扇区（hidden sector）理论预言的一种高多重数、各向同性的低动量粒子分布信号，探索超出标准模型（Standard Model）的新物理场景需要对其开展实验搜索。

Method: 利用ATLAS探测器收集的140 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据（质心能量√s = 13 TeV，2015-2018年运行期），通过胶子-胶子融合（gluon-gluon fusion）产生标量 mediator，在Hidden Valley框架下针对包含末态缪子（muon）的SUEP信号进行搜索。

Result: 未观察到超出标准模型（Standard Model）预期的显著超出。对 mediator 产生截面与衰变至SUEP的分支比的乘积设置排除下限：mediator质量 m_S = 750 GeV时为0.05 fb，m_S = 400 GeV时为0.4 fb，m_S = 125 GeV时为70 fb。最后一种情况对应将 mediator 视为标准模型希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson），转化为SUEP衰变分支比的上限约为0.2%。

Conclusion: 当前数据未支持SUEP信号的存在，但排除了参数空间中部分区域；对轻质量 mediator 区域的排除结果约束了标准模型希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）向SUEP的不可见或低动量衰变分支比在0.2%以下。

Abstract: Soft unclustered energy patterns (SUEPs) refer to high-multiplicity, isotropic distributions of low-momentum particles that could arise in strongly-coupled hidden sector theories. A search for SUEPs whose decay products contain muons in the final state is presented using 140 fb$^{-1}$ of proton-proton collision data at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV collected by the ATLAS detector at the Large Hadron Collider during 2015-2018. The analysis targets SUEP signatures via gluon-gluon fusion production of a scalar mediator in Hidden Valley scenarios. No significant excess over the Standard Model expectation is observed. Exclusion limits are set on the product of the mediator production cross section and the branching fraction for its decay into a SUEP, down to 0.05 fb for a mediator mass of $m_S$ = 750 GeV, 0.4 fb for $m_S$ = 400 GeV, and 70 fb for $m_S$ = 125 GeV; the last value, when identifying the mediator with the Standard Model Higgs boson, translates to an upper limit on the branching fraction of around 0.2%.

### [59] [Frequency-dependent stress response under thermal cycle: A thermal-crystal plasticity and dynamic mode decomposition study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19280)
*Haruki Ohashi,Yoshiteru Aoyagi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过热-晶体塑性模拟（thermal-crystal plasticity simulation）预测不同热循环频率下的热应力场，并采用动态模态分解（DMD）系统提取应力场的时空结构，揭示了频率对热力响应时空行为的影响，展示了DMD作为分析复杂循环热载荷模拟数据框架的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热循环环境在工程中广泛存在，但热循环频率对应力场时空行为和塑性响应的瞬时影响尚未被充分理解，且缺乏能够同时捕捉空间异质性（spatial heterogeneity）与时间演化（temporal evolution）的系统分析方法。

Method: 采用热-晶体塑性模拟预测不同热循环频率下的热应力场，并通过动态模态分解（dynamic mode decomposition, DMD）作为诊断与后处理技术，提取并紧凑表示应力场的时空结构。

Result: 热-力学响应可表示为多个有效时间分量（temporal components）的叠加，反映了系统行为的复杂性增加；DMD能够系统地提取应力场的时空结构，并对频率相关的热应力响应变化进行定量表征，超越了传统平均或快照（snapshot）分析方法的局限。

Conclusion: DMD作为一种分析框架，能够有效组织复杂模拟数据并解释循环热载荷下塑性响应的时间结构，为理解热循环频率对材料响应的影响提供了新的分析手段。

Abstract: Thermal cycle environments involving repeated temperature changes are common conditions observed in modern engineering processes. Under such conditions, materials undergo repeated thermal expansion and contraction, forming complex thermal stress fields. Thermal-crystal plasticity simulations that account for stress fields and thermal conduction at the polycrystalline microstructure scale are an effective method for numerically reproducing thermal cycle environments. However, the influence of thermal cycle frequency on the temporal behavior of the stress field and plastic response has not yet been fully understood, partly because a systematic analysis method capable of simultaneously capturing spatial heterogeneity and temporal evolution remains limited. In this study, we predicted the thermal stress field generated under different thermal cycle frequencies using thermal-crystal plasticity simulations and investigated the effect of frequency on the spatiotemporal structure of the stress response. The present framework illustrates that the resulting thermal-mechanical response can be represented as a superposition of multiple effective temporal components, reflecting the increased complexity of the system behavior. By employing dynamic mode decomposition (DMD) as a diagnostic and post-processing technique, we demonstrate that the spatiotemporal structure of the stress field under thermal cycle conditions can be systematically extracted and compactly represented. This approach enables a quantitative characterization of frequency-dependent changes in the thermal stress response beyond conventional averaging or snapshot-based analyses. The results highlight the utility of DMD as a framework for organizing complex simulation data and for interpreting the temporal structure of plastic response under cyclic thermal loading.

</details>


### [60] [Cryogenically Enhanced Laser-Induced Amorphous Phase Transitions in Crystalline Silicon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19318)
*Conrad Kuz,Andy Lee,Shashu Tomar,Ravleen Kaur,Mohamed Yaseen Noor,Justin Twardowski,Liam Clink,Roberto C. Myers,Enam Chowdhury*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文研究从室温至24K的低温环境对单次飞秒激光照射硅的非晶化（amorphization）过程的影响，发现低温显著增强非晶化效果，并通过载子依赖双温模型（nTTM）揭示其物理机制为声子群体减少、吸收路径改变及晶格弛豫动力学变化协同抑制再结晶、促进非晶冻结。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅的非晶化在光子学（photonics）、微电子学（microelectronics）和太阳能电池技术中具有重要应用。超快激光已用于在室温下通过快速非热熔化和凝固将晶体硅转化为非晶硅，而材料温度可显著影响冷却速率，因此引入温度控制可能为超快激光改性硅提供新的自由度。

Method: 使用1030nm单次飞秒激光脉冲在室温至24K的低温范围内照射硅；通过光学显微镜、拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）和开尔文探针力显微镜（KPFM）表征非晶化增强现象；采用载子依赖双温模型（carrier dependent two-temperature model, nTTM）进行数值模拟。

Result: 低温下非晶化显著增强，拉曼分析确认出现非晶表面层；AFM和SEM成像显示表面形貌出现温度依赖性变化，包括局部熔体重新分布和再凝固材料。nTTM模拟重现了实验趋势。

Conclusion: 低温下声子群体减少（reduced phonon population）、吸收路径改变（modified absorption pathways）及晶格弛豫动力学变化（altered lattice relaxation dynamics）共同促进非晶冻结（amorphous freezing）而非再结晶（recrystallization）。该研究首次详细考察了液氮温度以下硅的超快辐照行为，揭示了温度调控机制，对先进硅微结构加工具有参考意义。

Abstract: Amorphization of silicon is crucial to applications in photonics, microelectronics and solar cell technologies. Ultrafast lasers have been used to generate amorphous silicon from crystalline silicon using rapid nonthermal melting and solidification in room temperature. As material temperature can affect cooling rates significantly, adding temperature control in ultrafast laser modification of silicon may allow a new degree of freedom in ultrafast laser modification. In this work, we investigate the role of cryogenic temperature in governing ultrafast damage pathways via single-shot femtosecond laser irradiation of silicon from room temperature down to 24K at 1030nm. Across this temperature range, we observe a pronounced enhancement of amorphization at lower temperatures, revealed through optical microscopy, Raman spectroscopy, and Kelvin probe force microscopy (KPFM). Raman analysis identifies this ring as an amorphous surface layer, while complementary AFM and SEM imaging show temperature-dependent changes in surface morphology, including localized melt redistribution and refrozen material. To elucidate the physical origins of this behavior, we implement a carrier dependent two-temperature model (nTTM). The simulations reproduce the experimentally observed trends and indicate that reduced phonon population, modified absorption pathways, and altered lattice relaxation dynamics at cryogenic temperatures collectively promote amorphous freezing over recrystallization. This study represents the first detailed examination of silicon under ultrafast irradiation below the liquid-nitrogen regime and reveals temperature-governed mechanisms relevant for advanced silicon microstructuring.

</details>


### [61] [Charge Symmetry Beyond Wyckoff Equivalence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19383)
*Qiu-Shi Huang,Xin-Gao Gong,Su-Huai Wei*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文揭示了压力诱导的电荷转移可以使晶格中晶体学等效位点变为电荷不等效，而晶体学不等效位点却能因隐藏对称性保持电荷等效，表明电子态的等价结构并非由晶格对称性唯一决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统认为晶体学对称性决定电子等价性：相同Wyckoff位置的原子电荷相同，不同Wyckoff位置的原子电荷不同。本文旨在验证这两种预期是否可能在压力下失效，并探索其背后的物理机制。

Method: 构建最小朗道理论（Landau theory），描述压力诱导的电荷转移：压缩增强电荷重分布带来的位点间库仑能（intersite Coulomb energy），直至其克服位点内充电成本（onsite charging cost），从而失稳电荷等价态。以体心立方（BCC）Na和hP4 Na为案例进行验证。

Result: 在BCC Na中，低压下所有位点电荷等价，但压缩驱动相邻位点间电荷转移，产生电子对称性破缺的CsCl型态，而离子框架仍为BCC。在hP4 Na中，两个Na位点分属不同Wyckoff位置，但因低能流形中涌现的规范等价（gauge equivalence）保持电荷等价，形成近费米双重态（near-Fermi doublets）；压缩后电荷转移打破该隐藏等价性，分裂双重态并驱动金属-绝缘体转变。

Conclusion: 压力诱导的电荷转移是一种使电子等价性既可低于也可高于Wyckoff位置所暗示水平的机制，证明晶格对称性约束但并非唯一决定电子态的等价结构。

Abstract: Crystallographic symmetry is usually taken as a guide to electronic equivalence in crystals: atoms on the same Wyckoff position are expected to have the same charge, whereas atoms on different Wyckoff positions are expected to be electronically distinct. Here we show that both expectations can fail in oppo-site ways: crystallographically equivalent sites can become charge-inequivalent under compression, whereas crystallographically inequivalent sites can remain charge-equivalent at low pressure because of an emergent hidden symmetry. We develop a minimal Landau theory of pressure-induced charge transfer, in which compression enhances the intersite Coulomb energy gained by charge redistribution until it overcomes the onsite charging cost and destabilizes the charge-equivalent state. In BCC Na, all sites are charge-equivalent at low pressure, but compression drives charge transfer between neighboring sites, pro-ducing an electronically symmetry-broken CsCl-type state on an unchanged BCC ionic framework. In hP4 Na, the opposite anomaly occurs: two Na sites occupy distinct Wyckoff positions, yet remain charge-equivalent at low pressure because of an emergent gauge equivalence in the low-energy manifold, giving rise to near-Fermi doublets that appear accidental in conventional space-group analysis. Upon compres-sion, pressure-induced charge transfer breaks this hidden equivalence, splits the near-Fermi doublets, and drives a metal-insulator transition. These two complementary cases establish pressure-induced charge transfer as a mechanism by which electronic equivalence can either fall below or rise above what Wyckoff positions alone would suggest, showing that lattice symmetry constrains but does not uniquely determine the equivalence structure of the electronic state.

</details>


### [62] [Octahedral Tilting in Halide Double Perovskites: Disentangling Lone-Pair Chemistry and Geometric Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19414)
*Mehmet Baskurt,Erik Fransson,Madeleine Lindvik,Paul Erhart,Julia Wiktor*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究系统分析了57种卤化物双钙钛矿（HDPs）在0 K下的八面体倾斜行为及其四方相与立方相的相对稳定性，发现Goldschmidt容忍因子是控制倾斜的主要因素，而立体化学活性孤对电子与倾斜的关联本质上源于其对离子尺寸的影响；通过机器学习势能连接了0 K倾斜能量与有限温度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 卤化物双钙钛矿（halide double perovskites, HDPs）作为铅基钙钛矿的有前景替代材料，其结构动力学研究远不如传统卤化物钙钛矿充分，尤其是八面体倾斜（octahedral tilting）的行为和驱动机理尚不清晰。

Method: 采用结构和能量描述符结合简单几何度量，分析57种HDPs在0 K下的八面体倾斜和四方相/立方相稳定性；使用机器学习势（machine-learned interatomic potentials）连接0 K倾斜能量与有限温度行为。

Result: 倾斜角度的大小和倾斜相的能量偏好主要与Goldschmidt容忍因子（t）相关；立体化学活性孤对电子（stereochemically active lone-pair cations）的存在也与增强的倾斜相关，但这一趋势主要反映孤对化学伴随的离子尺寸使t偏离1；无孤对电子但倾斜强烈的化合物同样存在；倾斜相更稳定的化合物具有更高的相变温度（transition temperature），350 K声子谱中出现的软模（soft modes）与容忍因子、倾斜角度和倾斜能量趋势一致。

Conclusion: 本研究为HDPs的结构-稳定性关系提供了系统参考，并阐明孤对电子化学与八面体倾斜之间的关联更多是相关性而非因果关系。

Abstract: Halide double perovskites (HDPs) have emerged as promising alternatives to their lead-based counterparts. However, their structural dynamics is less explored than that of conventional halide perovskites. In this work, we investigate octahedral tilting at 0 K and the relative stability of tetragonal and cubic phases of a set of 57 halide double perovskites (HDPs). By combining structural and energetic descriptors with simple geometric metrics, we identify the main trends controlling the stabilization of one-tilt tetragonal phases across this family. We find that both the magnitude of the tilt angles and the energetic preference for tilted phases correlate primarily with the Goldschmidt tolerance factor $t$. The presence of stereochemically active lone-pair cations also correlates with enhanced tilting; however, this trend largely reflects that lone-pair chemistries in HDPs occur together with ionic sizes that shift $t$ away from unity. Consistent with this picture, we observe several compounds without lone pairs that nonetheless exhibit strong octahedral tilting. Finally, using machine-learned interatomic potentials, we connect the 0 K tilting energetics to finite-temperature behavior: compounds with more strongly stabilized tilt phases exhibit higher transition temperatures, and phonon spectra at 350 K reveal soft and broad modes that are consistent with the trends in tolerance factors, tilt angles, and tilt energies at 0 K. Our results provide a systematic reference for structure-stability relationships in HDPs and clarify when lone-pair chemistry is correlated with, rather than the primary cause of, octahedral tilting.

</details>


### [63] [Evaluation of External Magnetic Flux Density in Piezo-Flexomagnetic Nanobeams Using a Hybrid 1D-2D Finite Element Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19422)
*Lala Samprit Ray,Bishweshwar Babu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过有限元方法数值评估了压电-挠曲磁纳米梁（piezo-flexomagnetic nanobeam）弯曲时在外部空气中产生的磁通密度，揭示了即使在无压磁耦合条件下，自由梁周围仍存在显著的外部磁场分布，为纳米级非接触磁弹性传感系统的设计提供了依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非接触传感器（non-contact sensors）中，周围介质中的感应磁场往往比内部磁响应更具实用价值；然而，大多数关于压电-挠曲磁纳米结构的理论研究忽略了外部磁域（external magnetic domain）的影响。

Method: 采用一种混合有限元公式（hybrid finite element formulation），将一维Timoshenko梁模型（1D Timoshenko beam model）与同时涵盖梁体和周围空气域的二维静磁问题（2D magnetostatic problem）进行耦合求解；数值结果与磁隔离压电-挠曲磁梁的解析解进行了验证。

Result: 结果表明，即使在无压磁耦合（piezomagnetic coupling）的条件下，自由悬浮结构周围仍存在显著的外部磁通分布（external magnetic flux distribution）；敏感性分析（sensitivity analysis）识别出对外部横向磁通密度影响最大的材料参数。

Conclusion: 这些发现为纳米尺度非接触磁弹性传感系统（nanoscale non-contact magnetoelastic sensing systems）的设计提供了重要见解。

Abstract: This study numerically evaluates the external magnetic flux density generated in air by the bending of a piezo-flexomagnetic nanobeam. In several classes of non-contact sensors, the magnetic field induced in the surrounding medium is often more useful than the internal magnetic response. However, most theoretical studies on piezo-flexomagnetic nanostructures neglect the external magnetic domain. The proposed framework employs a coupled hybrid finite element formulation combining a 1D Timoshenko beam model with a 2D magnetostatic problem encompassing both the beam body and the surrounding air domain. The formulation is verified against analytical solutions of magnetically isolated piezo-flexomagnetic beams. The results demonstrate the presence of a significant external magnetic flux distribution in free-standing structures, even in the absence of piezomagnetic coupling. A systematic sensitivity analysis further identifies the material parameters most strongly influencing the external transverse magnetic flux density. These findings provide insight into the design of nanoscale non-contact magnetoelastic sensing systems.

</details>


### [64] [Zero-net-magnetization hybrid magnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19445)
*San-Dong Guo,Shi-Hao Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出零净磁化混合磁体（zero-net-magnetization hybrid magnet）的概念，通过将具有相反自旋极化的磁原子以不同对称性（P、C/M或无对称关联）部分耦合，构建由PT-反铁磁体（PT-antiferromagnet）、交变磁体（altermagnet）或完全补偿亚铁磁体（fully compensated ferrimagnet）组成的复合体系。借助紧束缚模型和第一性原理计算，以Cr₂C₂S₆/CrMoC₂S₆异质结为例，验证了在II型能带排列下仅单一载流子掺杂可诱导净磁矩的特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 零净磁化磁体因具有本征零杂散场和太赫兹（terahertz）动力学特性，在超高密度和超快应用方面具备潜力。本文旨在提出一种零净磁化混合磁体的新概念，拓展其结构实现方式与物理性质调控手段。

Method: 从局域视角出发，将零净磁化混合磁体视为由PT-反铁磁体、交变磁体或完全补偿亚铁磁体组合而成。提出通过三类零净磁化磁性单层构成异质结来实现此类体系，主要研究由两种零净磁化磁体构成的异质结。采用紧束缚（tight-binding, TB）模型进行理论验证，并以PT-反铁磁体和完全补偿亚铁磁体构成的异质结为例展开分析；进一步以Cr₂C₂S₆/CrMoC₂S₆异质结为例，结合电场调制进行第一性原理（first-principles）计算验证。

Result: 当异质结混合磁体呈现II型能带排列（type-II band alignment）时，仅电子掺杂或仅空穴掺杂中的一种能诱导净磁矩（net magnetic moment），另一种则几乎不产生净磁化。紧束缚模型和第一性原理计算结果均支持该理论预言。

Conclusion: 零净磁化混合磁体为设计新型磁功能材料提供了可行思路，其在电场调制下可通过选择性载流子掺杂实现净磁矩的开关调控，有望应用于超快自旋电子学（ultrafast spintronics）领域。

Abstract: Zero-net-magnetization magnets possess ultradense and ultrafast application potential, benefiting from their intrinsic zero stray field and terahertz dynamics characteristics. Herein, we propose the concept of zero-net-magnetization hybrid magnet, in which magnetic atoms with opposite spin polarization are partially coupled via spatial inversion ($P$) symmetry, partially via rotation/mirror ($C/M$) symmetry or partially without any symmetry correlation. From a local perspective and neglecting the interactions between local regions, hybrid magnet can be regarded as being composed of $PT$-antiferromagnet (possessing the combined symmetry ($PT$) of $P$ and time-reversal ($T$)), altermagnet, or fully compensated ferrimagnet. To realize hybrid magnet, we propose that such system can be constructed by forming heterojunction with three types of zero-net-magnetization magnetic monolayers. We mainly investigate the heterojunction composed of two kinds of zero-net-magnetization magnets, among which one type corresponds to fully compensated ferrimagnet. When heterojunction hybrid magnet exhibits a type-II band alignment, only one of electron doping and hole doping can induce a net magnetic moment, while the other hardly generates any net magnetization. Taking the heterojunction constructed by $PT$-antiferromagnet and fully compensated ferrimagnet as an example, we verify our proposal by means of the tight-binding (TB) model. Finally, taking the $\mathrm{Cr_2C_2S_6}$/$\mathrm{CrMoC_2S_6}$ heterojunction as an example, we perform first-principles calculations combined with electric field modulation to validate our TB model and theoretical proposal.

### [65] [High-Throughput Bayesian Optimization of Cement-Salt Hydrates Composites for Seasonal Thermochemical Energy Storage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19494)

Method: 采用基于贝叶斯优化（Bayesian optimization, BO）的高通量实验框架，在由盐类型、盐浓度、水灰比和外加剂-水泥比定义的设计空间中，并行优化比能量（specific energy）和比能量成本（specific energy cost）两个竞争目标。

Abstract: Thermochemical energy storage (TCES) based on salt hydrates is a promising route for seasonal heat storage; however, the design of practical sorbent materials remains challenging due to a non-trivial coupling between composition, synthesis feasibility, performance, and cost. Here, focusing on salt-into-matrix cement-based composites, we demonstrate that a high-throughput experimental framework based on Bayesian optimization (BO) can be used to orchestrate the optimization process of composite materials for low-temperature TCES. Overall, the optimized formulations improved the specific energy of previously developed cement-based materials by up to a factor of five, although it remains below that of state-of-the-art composites based on silica gel and expanded vermiculite. Nonetheless, the present materials, notably CaCl$_2$- and Zn(NO$_3$)$_2$-based composites, offer an attractive cost-to-performance balance, highlighting BO as an effective strategy for accelerated TCES materials discovery.

### [66] [Nanoscale Thermal Imaging of Dislocation-Mediated Heat Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19496)
*Ruilin Mao,Bingyao Liu,Jiaxin Liu,Xiaoyue Gao,Junping Luo,Fachen Liu,Ruochen Shi,Jiade Li,Jinlong Du,Peng Gao*

TL;DR: 本研究利用原位扫描透射电子显微镜-电子能量损失谱（in situ STEM-EELS）直接测量了低角度 SrTiO3 晶界中周期性位错阵列（dislocation array）的局域热阻（local thermal resistance）及其空间范围，定量揭示了位错核心附近更强的热阻与双尺度热输运特征，并通过原子尺度结构与振动分析提供了微观机制解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用原位扫描透射电子显微镜-电子能量损失谱（in situ scanning transmission electron microscopy-electron energy-loss spectroscopy, STEM-EELS）对具有周期性位错阵列的低角度 SrTiO3 晶界进行纳米尺度温度分布成像，并结合原子尺度的结构与振动分析。

Result: 位错阵列上观测到 47 K 的温度降；温度场畸变集中在位错核心附近，表明局域热阻集中在离散位点而非均匀分布；识别出双尺度热输运特征：核心主导效应范围约 4.8-6.2 nm，核心间扩展影响范围约 10.3-14.3 nm；原子级分析揭示了核心处的原子重构与局域光学声子扰动（optical-phonon perturbations）。

Conclusion: 该研究定量解析了位错介导热输运的空间异质性，揭示了其原子尺度机制，为高性能热电材料、半导体、高温结构合金及其他功能晶体材料的缺陷工程设计提供了定量基础。

Abstract: Dislocations in crystalline materials are widely exploited to tailor the thermal conductivity of semiconductors and thermoelectrics, yet a critical gap persists: direct measurement of local thermal resistance at individual buried dislocations, along with its spatial extent, remains elusive due to the limitations of conventional thermal probes. Here, we use in situ scanning transmission electron microscopy-electron energy-loss spectroscopy to map nanoscale temperature distributions across a low-angle SrTiO3 grain boundary with periodic dislocation arrays. Our results reveal a temperature drop of 47 K across the dislocation array. The associated temperature-field distortions are concentrated near the dislocation cores, consistent with stronger local thermal resistance at these discrete sites rather than a uniformly distributed resistance along the array. We further identify a distinct two-scale heat transport characteristic near the dislocation array: core-dominated effects over approximately 4.8-6.2 nm and extended inter-core influences over approximately 10.3-14.3 nm. Atomic-scale structural and vibrational analyses further reveal core-associated atomic reconstruction and localized optical-phonon perturbations, providing a microscopic basis for the stronger local thermal resistance inferred near dislocation cores. These findings quantitatively resolve spatial heterogeneity of dislocation-mediated heat transport, uncover its atomic-scale mechanism, and provide a quantitative basis for defect engineering, guiding the design of high-performance thermoelectrics, semiconductors, high-temperature structural alloys, and other functional crystalline materials.

Abstract: The polymorphism of organic/metal interfaces influences many of their properties. Based on these investigations, we show that the adsorbate-substrate interaction for some adsorption geometries can change significantly with the lattice constant. In addition, due to a transition from repulsive to attractive adsorbate-adsorbate interactions, polymorphs with tight packing become more favorable, if the lattice constant is increased, resulting in a lattice-constant-based phase transition.

Method: 该方法利用形态感知描述符（morphology-aware descriptors）来刻画光吸收（light absorption）、激子解离（exciton dissociation）、非孪生复合（non-geminate recombination）和自由电荷载流子迁移率（free charge carrier mobilities），从而计算包含最多五相（给体非晶相、给体晶相、受体非晶相、受体晶相、混合非晶相）的复杂异质结（heterojunction）的电流-电压（JV）曲线，计算时间极低。

Conclusion: 该方法为快速评估有机太阳能电池多相形貌对器件性能的影响提供了有效工具，并强调形态-性能关系具有材料体系依赖性，无法一概而论。

Abstract: Understanding the relationship between morphology and performance in organic solar cells is essential for developing devices that are both high performing and resilient to aging. This work introduces a unique method capable of calculating the current-voltage (JV) curve of complex heterojunction morphologies containing up to five phases (donor amorphous, donor crystalline, acceptor amorphous, acceptor crystalline, mixed amorphous) with a very low computation time using morphology-aware descriptors of light absorption, exciton dissociation, non-geminate recombination and free charge carrier mobilities. ### [70] [$G_0W_0$@HF and BSE methods in periodic systems from Hartree-Fock theory: gaussian orbital and density fitting approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19746)
*Charles H. Patterson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种从基于高斯轨道（gaussian orbitals）的哈特里-福克（Hartree-Fock, HF）方法出发进行$G_0W_0$计算的方法，避免使用等离激元极点近似（plasmon pole approximation），并通过密度拟合（density fitting）实现极化率（polarizability）与自能（self-energy）的高效计算，应用于半导体和氧化物材料后，有效修正了HF理论高估带隙（band gap）和价带宽度（valence band width）的系统性误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 常见的$GW$方法从基于平面波基组（plane wave basis）的密度泛函理论（DFT）哈密顿量和科恩-沈（Kohn-Sham）轨道出发，而本文希望探索从HF方法和高斯轨道基组出发的$G_0W_0$计算路径，以克服HF理论在材料中高估带隙和价带宽度的固有缺陷。

Method: 采用$G_0W_0$方法，从基于高斯轨道基组的HF方法出发；屏蔽库仑相互作用$W$通过$W = v + vΠv$的方式获得，不使用等离激元极点近似；极化率$Π$在随机相位近似（random phase approximation, RPA）水平处理，通过求解每个独特$\mathbf{Q}$点的贝特-萨佩特方程（Bethe-Salpeter equations, BSE）得到；自能采用收敛策略，$G_0W_0$提供主要贡献，高能虚态剩余部分通过二阶微扰（second-order）计算；HF和$G_0W_0$/BSE计算均采用库仑度量的密度拟合（density fitting with a coulomb metric）。

Result: 将该方法应用于元素半导体（C, Si）和氧化物（MgO, 锐钛矿及金红石TiO$_2$）。HF理论高估带隙和价带宽度的误差得到修正。RPA屏蔽相互作用仍会高估带隙，但$G_0W_0$自能带来的带宽重整化（band width renormalization）使得金刚石（diamond）和硅（Si）的带宽与实验吻合良好。

Conclusion: 基于高斯轨道HF方法的$G_0W_0$计算能够有效修正HF理论的系统误差，其中RPA屏蔽导致带隙高估，而$G_0W_0$自能带宽重整化则使半导体带宽与实验高度一致。该方法为材料准粒子能级（quasi-particle energies）计算提供了一种替代DFT起点的可行方案。

Abstract: The $GW$ method for calculating quasi-particle energies of solids commonly begin from a DFT Hamiltonian and Kohn-Sham orbitals in a plane wave basis. Screening of the coulomb interaction is implemented using the inverse dielectric function in the random phase approximation (RPA). We present $G_0W_0$ calculations which begin from the Hartree-Fock method in a basis of gaussian orbitals. The screened coulomb interaction, $W$, is obtained using a $W$ = $v$ + $vΠv$ approach without invoking a plasmon pole approximation. The polarizability, $Π$, in $W$ is treated at the RPA level. RPA polarizabilities require solution of Bethe-Salpeter equations (BSE) for each unique $\textbf{Q}$ point. A strategy for obtaining self-energies which are converged with respect to number of virtual states is employed in which $G_0W_0$ yields the majority of the self-energy and the remaining part from high energy virtual levels is evaluated at second-order. The methods are evaluated by applying them to elemental semiconductors (C, Si) and oxides (MgO and anatase and rutile TiO$_2$). Common errors of HF theory applied to materials include overestimation of both the band gap and valence band widths. These are corrected in the approach employed here. Typically, the RPA screened interaction results in overestimation of band gaps while the $G_0W_0$ self-energy band width renormalization yields band widths for diamond and Si which are in good agreement with experiment. HF calculations are performed in gaussian orbital basis sets and $G_0W_0$ and BSE calculations are performed using density fitting with a coulomb metric.

</details>

In this study, we employ an advanced and efficient machine learning potential (MLP) to simulate lithium self-diffusion in LiNi0.8Mn0.1Co0.1O2 (NMC811), enabling direct large-scale molecular dynamics (MD) simulations. The workflow integrates a fine-tuned MACE (Message Passing Atomic Cluster Expansion) foundation model as a structural generator and leverages an active learning strategy applied to a near-ground-state dataset. This approach enables the construction of a reliable MLP for NMC811 in a data-efficient manner using a limited number of density functional theory (DFT) reference calculations. Based on this potential, we performed MD simulations to predict lithium diffusion coefficients. The MLP-based simulations preserve the accuracy of DFT while overcoming its time and length scale limitations, thereby allowing direct simulation of lithium self-diffusion in NMC811.

Abstract: UiO-66 is the most widely studied metal-organic framework (MOF), on account of its structural tunability given by its capacity of sustaining high amounts of point defects in its structure. Its synthesis mechanism is largely unknown, with only a few works mostly focused on the formation of the Zr-oxide cluster. In this work, a partially reactive force field to model UiO-66, nb-UiO-FF, is introduced. This force field incorporates node--ligand reactivity via a Morse potential and the introduction of dummy atoms to reproduce the anisotropic charge distribution of the Zr atoms in the node. nb-UiO-FF reproduces structural features of both UiO-66 and its isoreticular analog UiO-67, mechanical properties and framework stability with or without defects, activated or filled with N,N-dimethylformamide or ethanol. The force field is further employed within a molecular dynamics scheme to study the early stages of solvothermal node--ligand binding. Transient structural motifs both thermodynamically and kinetically favored are identified. This force field enables studying the self-assembly of UiO-66, as well as the formation of its point defects.

### [74] [Realization of a parity-violating antiferromagnetic state in LaMnSi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19891)
*Takuma Iwata,K. Shiraishi,T. Aoyama,D. Senba,T. Takeda,Y. Fujisawa,M. Nurmamat,K. Nakanishi,K. Yamagami,M. Arita,T. Yamada,Y. Yanagi,A. Kimura,H. Tanida,Kenta Kuroda*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文通过软X射线角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）和偏振分辨光学二次谐波发生（SHG）显微术，首次提供了LaMnSi中宇称破缺反铁磁（AFM）态的直接实验证据，证实了PT对称性保护下自旋简并但动量不对称的电子能带结构，并指出这类反铁磁材料是实现非互易和非线性电子响应的有前景平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇称破缺反铁磁（antiferromagnetic, AFM）序同时打破空间反演对称性（$\mathcal{P}$）和时间反演对称性（$\mathcal{T}$），却保持组合的$\mathcal{PT}$对称性，从而产生自旋简并但动量不对称的电子能带。这种动量不对称被认为是非常规非互易（nonreciprocal）和非线性响应的微观起源，但其实验验证极具挑战性，因为需要同时确立对称性破缺的磁序及其关联的电子结构。

Method: 采用软X射线角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）解析三维体态能带结构，并结合偏振分辨光学二次谐波发生（second-harmonic generation, SHG）显微术探测来自携带$\mathcal{T}$奇宇称破缺序的反向AFM畴（domains）的非线性光学响应。

Result: 软X射线ARPES解析的三维体态能带结构与AFM相的密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算结果一致；SHG显微术从携带$\mathcal{T}$奇宇称破缺序的相反AFM畴中检测到符号反转的非线性光学响应。两项结果共同为LaMnSi中的宇称破缺AFM态提供了直接证据。

Conclusion: 确认LaMnSi为宇称破缺反铁磁金属，并指出此类反铁磁材料可作为对称性可控的非互易和非线性电子响应的有前景平台。

Abstract: Spontaneous symmetry breaking underlies functional electronic phenomena in quantum materials. Breaking space-inversion ($\mathcal{P}$) or time-reversal ($\mathcal{T}$) symmetry can generate spin-split electronic bands central to modern spintronics. By contrast, parity-violating antiferromagnetic (AFM) order breaks both $\mathcal{P}$ and $\mathcal{T}$ while preserving the combined $\mathcal{PT}$ symmetry, enabling spin-degenerate yet momentum-asymmetric electronic bands. This momentum asymmetry has been proposed as a microscopic origin of unconventional nonreciprocal and nonlinear responses but its experimental verification has remained challenging because it requires establishing both the symmetry-breaking magnetic order and the associated electronic structure. Here we combine soft x-ray angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) and polarization-resolved optical second-harmonic generation (SHG) microscopy to study LaMnSi, a candidate parity-violating AFM metal. Soft x-ray ARPES resolves the three-dimensional bulk band structures in agreement with density functional theory calculations for the AFM phase, whereas SHG microscopy detects sign-reversing nonlinear optical responses from opposite AFM domains that carry $\mathcal{T}$-odd parity-violating order. Together, these results provide direct evidence for parity-violating AFM state in LaMnSi, establish LaMnSi as a parity-violating AFM metal, and identify this class of AFMs as a promising platform for symmetry-controlled nonreciprocal and nonlinear electronic responses.

Motivation: 传统DFTB方法依赖预先计算的Slater-Koster（SK）相互作用表，但其参数化无法灵活适应不同局域原子环境（如金属的不同氧化态），导致在复杂体系中电子结构和能量计算精度受限。因此，作者旨在发展一种能够自适应局部环境的DFTB方案。

Abstract: We propose to adapt the confined pseudo-atomic orbitals underpinning the precalculated Slater-Koster (SK) interaction tables in Density Functional Tight Binding (DFTB) to local atomic environments. We demonstrate significant improvement in electronic structure and energetics in the application to a partially oxidized Ni surface and Li insertion into graphite, where we assign optimal SK parameters to metal atoms in different oxidation states. Further analysis reveals the smoothness of the SK integrals across the varying oxidation states. Exploiting this, we introduce a site-resolved machine-learning scheme for fully adaptive DFTB. Using atomic descriptors and simple regression architectures already established in the context of machine-learning interatomic potentials, our scheme achieves 95% band-structure accuracy across all Ni-O binary compositions in the Materials Project.

### [76] [Mesoscale Domain Evolution Mechanism during Alternating Current (AC) Poling of Relaxor Ferroelectrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20011)
*Yuan-Jie Sun,Bo Wang,Long-Qing Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过相场模拟（phase-field simulations）研究菱方相弛豫铁电单晶中交流极化（AC poling）过程中71°和109°铁电畴壁的运动，发现相邻71°畴壁间距比决定其是否发生不可逆消除，该行为源于长程弹性相互作用导致的畴壁运动不同步（unsynchronized motion），进而打破能量等价畴变体间的对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验观察到弛豫铁电晶体中倾斜畴壁在交流极化下发生不可逆消除，但其介观尺度机制尚不明确，需要从理论模拟层面揭示潜在机理。

Method: 采用相场模拟方法，在准二维层状几何结构中研究含有71°和109°畴壁的菱方相Pb(Mg₁/₃Nb₂/₃)O₃–PbTiO₃单晶在交流极化过程中的畴壁运动。

Result: 1. 畴壁行为取决于71°与109°畴壁的间距比（spacing ratio）：间距较小时71°畴壁不可逆消除，间距较大时保留，109°畴壁始终完整；2. 识别出畴壁消除的阈值间距比，且该阈值依赖于力学边界条件；3. 该现象源于相邻71°畴壁因长程弹性相互作用（long-range elastic interactions）导致的运动不同步，打破能量等价畴变体之间的对称性。

Conclusion: 邻近效应驱动的对称性破缺（proximity-driven symmetry breaking）可作为高畴壁密度铁电材料中畴工程（domain engineering）的介观尺度机制，为理解极化反转过程中集体畴壁演化提供了机理性的见解。

Abstract: Ferroelectric domain variants that are energetically equivalent are expected to remain preserved during polarization reversal under a symmetry-preserving electric field. However, recent experiments on relaxor-ferroelectric crystals have revealed irreversible elimination of inclined domain walls during AC poling, while the underlying mesoscale mechanism remains unclear. Here, we investigate the domain-wall motion during AC poling of rhombohedral Pb(Mg$_{1/3}$Nb$_{2/3}$)O$_3$--PbTiO$_3$ single crystals containing both 71$^\circ$ and 109$^\circ$ domain walls within a quasi-two-dimensional laminated geometry using phase-field simulations. The simulations reveal that the domain-wall behavior during polarization reversal depends on the spacing ratio between the 71$^\circ$ and 109$^\circ$ domain walls. Closely spaced 71$^\circ$ domain walls undergo irreversible elimination, whereas more widely separated walls are preserved, while the 109$^\circ$ domain walls remain intact. A threshold ratio for domain-wall elimination is identified and found to depend on the mechanical boundary conditions. By tracking the domain-wall trajectories during the switching process, we attribute this behavior to unsynchronized motion of neighboring 71$^\circ$ domain walls arising from long-range elastic interactions when the walls become strongly coupled. This collective motion breaks the symmetry between energetically equivalent domain variants and leads to irreversible domain-wall elimination during polarization reversal. These findings provide mechanistic insight into collective domain-wall evolution during polarization reversal and suggest that proximity-driven symmetry breaking may provide a mesoscale mechanism for domain engineering in ferroelectric materials with high domain-wall densities.

### [77] [Geometry-Dependent Crack Interaction and Toughening in Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20017)
*Suyeong Jin,Jung-Wuk Hong,Alexandre F. Fonseca*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用计算模拟（computational simulations）方法，对含平行裂纹的石墨烯在拉伸载荷下的力学响应进行系统研究，重点考察裂纹宽度与裂纹间距（W_gap）两个几何参数的耦合效应。

Conclusion: 提出了裂纹几何设计图谱（crack-geometry design map），用以识别裂纹合并、独立传播（independent propagation）和增韧增强三种不同断裂行为区间。该结果为通过调控裂纹几何实现石墨烯力学性能优化提供了设计指导。

Abstract: The interaction between neighboring cracks has been shown to strongly influence the fracture behavior of graphene. While previous studies focused primarily on crack spacing, the role of crack width remains poorly understood. Here, computational simulations are performed to investigate the coupled effects of crack width and inter-crack spacing $(W_\text{gap})$ on the tensile response of graphene containing parallel cracks. The results show that increasing crack width amplifies the sensitivity of mechanical properties to crack spacing, leading to significant enhancement of peak stress, fracture strain, and toughness at sufficiently large $W_\text{gap}$. For narrow cracks, crack coalescence dominates and causes brittle failure. In contrast, wider cracks promote delayed ligament rupture, increased energy absorption and ductile-like fracture behavior. The normalized toughness and fracture strain exceed those of equivalent single-crack systems by more than twofold. A crack-geometry design map is proposed to identify regimes of crack coalescence, independent propagation, and enhanced toughness.

</details>


### [78] [Spin Response Properties in Electronically Robust Ferromagnetic Strained $\text{CrSiSe}_3$ Monolayer under External Electric Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20021)
