Conclusion: 应变工程CrSiSe₃单层同时实现了电荷免疫的鲁棒性（robust charge immunity）和自旋的灵活可调控性（flexible spin manipulation），这种独特的共存特性使其成为构建稳定自旋电子学器件的理想候选材料。

Abstract: Integrating two-dimensional van der Waals magnets into field-effect spintronic devices requires robust charge stability and tunable spin responses. In this study, we investigate the electronic, topological, magnonic, and magneto-optical properties of the strain-engineered ferromagnetic $\text{CrSiSe}_3$ monolayer under out-of-plane external electric fields by using first-principles calculations. We find that for this material, the intrinsic charge sector, including the indirect band gap, charge Berry curvature, optical conductivities, and magneto-optical Kerr effect spectra, exhibits exceptional robustness against applied fields up to 0.3 V/$Å$. Conversely, the spin degrees of freedom demonstrate highly sensitive tunability. Electrostatic gating significantly modulates the spin Berry-like curvature, driving a non-monotonic enhancement in the spin Hall conductivity. Furthermore, external fields effectively tune collective magnon excitations by modifying microscopic Heisenberg exchange interactions. Such coexistence of robust charge immunity and flexible spin manipulation establishes the strained $\text{CrSiSe}_3$ monolayer as a promising platform for stable spintronic devices.

Abstract: The coherent nonlinear dynamics between collective excitations, such as magnons and phonons, drive emergent phenomena in quantum materials, yet their direct observation remains a central challenge. Here, using double-terahertz-pump optical-probe spectroscopy, we report the direct observation of coherent magnon-phonon three-wave mixing in the layered antiferromagnetic insulator FePS$_{3}$. We resolve both second- and third-order nonlinear responses of antiferromagnetic magnons and identify a suite of nonlinear couplings in two-dimensional (2D) coherent spectra, including definitive sum- and difference-frequency generation between magnons and phonons. These results lay the groundwork for exploiting coherent nonlinearities to entangle magnetic and vibrational excitations, opening avenues for quantum control and hybrid quantum technologies in the terahertz regime.

Conclusion: 通过一个具体的模型体系阐明了一个一般性原则：引入较轻的等价位元素可显著增强自旋极化，这可能为理解与工程化设计Rashba相关体系（Rashba-related systems）提供有用的指导准则。

Abstract: Co-adsorption of Bi and Sb on Ag(111) at room temperature yields a single-layer Bi(1-x)Sb(x) alloy with a rectangular 3xsqrt(3) structure containing four atoms per unit cell (2/3 ML total coverage) and lacking long-range chemical order. We present an electronic structure study of this system combining angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) and density functional theory (DFT) calculations. To investigate the effect of inversion symmetry breaking induced by substituting a heavier atom (Bi) with a lighter isoelectronic one (Sb) within a fixed crystallographic framework, we focused on a Bi-rich composition. Our work illustrates, through a concrete model system, a general principle: incorporating a lighter isovalent element can significantly enhance spin polarization, potentially offering a useful design guideline for understanding and engineering Rashba-related systems.

### [81] [Lattice thermal conductivity decomposition: Peierls vs. non-Peierls contributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20096)
*Andrey Pereverzev*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文比较了利用全经典热流（full classical heat current）及其二次分量（quadratic component）和Peierls热流（Peierls heat current）计算晶格热导率（lattice thermal conductivity）的差异，并评估了弛豫时间近似（relaxation time approximation, RTA）的准确性。研究发现，二次热流与Peierls热流给出的结果差异很小；在α-石英中光学声子（optical phonon）对热导率的贡献超过声学模（acoustic modes）；弛豫时间近似在三种体系（固态氩、交替质量固态氩模型、α-石英）中均系统地低估了热导率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motivation：现有研究中常用Peierls热流或二次热流近似来计算晶格热导率，但这些近似方法相较于全经典热流的准确性尚未得到系统性的定量比较。同时，弛豫时间近似作为简化计算手段的适用性也需要在多种晶体体系中加以评估。

Method: Method：采用Green-Kubo方法基于全经典热流计算晶格热导率，并分别与二次热流分量和Peierls热流的结果进行对比。此外，在弛豫时间近似框架下独立评估热导率。研究对象涵盖三种晶体体系：固态氩、具有交替质量分布的固态氩模型以及α-石英。

Result: Result：在所有研究的材料中，由二次热流和Peierls热流计算得到的热导率之间仅有微小差异。在α-石英中，光学声子对热导率的贡献超过了声学模。弛豫时间近似在所有三种体系下均系统地低估了热导率。

Conclusion: Conclusion：二次热流和Peierls热流近似在计算晶格热导率时是合理且相互近似的，但弛豫时间近似在定性上偏保守。光学声子在α-石英等材料中的主导贡献表明，忽略光学支声子可能会造成显著误差。

Abstract: The Green-Kubo lattice thermal conductivity computed using the full classical heat current of a crystalline solid is compared with results obtained from the quadratic component of the heat current and from the commonly used Peierls heat current. In addition, thermal conductivity within the relaxation time approximation is evaluated. Three crystalline systems are investigated: solid argon, a model of solid argon with alternating masses, and $α$-quartz. For all materials considered, the thermal conductivities calculated using the quadratic and Peierls heat currents differ only slightly. In the case of $α$-quartz, the optical phonon contribution to the thermal conductivity is found to exceed that of the acoustic modes. The relaxation time approximation systematically underestimates the thermal conductivity in all three systems.

### [82] [Systematic study of one-point kinetic energy density functionals for atomic nuclei](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18142)
*Tian Shuai Shang,Jian Li,Haozhao Liang,Xinhui Wu,Cheng Ma,Wenhui Mi,Xuecheng Shao,Yanchao Wang*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文系统测试了36种原本用于凝聚态物理电子系统的动能密度泛函，发现其在核物理中的直接应用效果不一致且存在非物理渐近行为；但通过针对核密度的参数重优化，不同形式的广义梯度近似泛函收敛至约13 MeV的一致误差，表明优化后的半局域泛函成功捕捉了原子核的宏观液滴背景，而残差中周期性的魔数振荡则反映了量子壳效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索无轨道密度泛函理论（orbital-free density functional theory, OF-DFT）在核物理中的适用性，检验原本为电子系统设计的动能密度泛函能否用于核结构计算。

Method: 对36种原本用于凝聚态物理电子系统的一点动能密度泛函（one-point kinetic energy density functionals）进行系统基准测试；通过参数重优化（parameter re-optimization），使其适配核密度分布，并比较不同数学形式的广义梯度近似（generalized gradient approximation, GGA）泛函在优化后的表现。

Result: 原参数直接用于电子系统时性能不一致，部分泛函存在物理上不可接受的渐近行为；经参数重优化后，不同形式的GGA泛函收敛至约13 MeV的均方根误差（root-mean-square error）。

Conclusion: 优化后的半局域GGA泛函成功捕捉了原子核的宏观液滴背景（liquid-drop-like background），残差中在魔数（magic numbers）处出现的周期性振荡反映了量子壳效应（quantum shell effects）。

Abstract: To explore the applicability of orbital-free density functional theory (OF-DFT) in nuclear physics, we perform a systematic benchmark of 36 one-point kinetic energy density functionals, which are originally developed for electron systems in condensed matter physics. It is found that the direct use of the original parameters for electron systems leads to inconsistent performance, with certain functionals exhibiting physically unacceptable asymptotic behaviors. However, through parameter re-optimization targeting nuclear densities, different mathematical forms of generalized gradient approximation (GGA) functionals converge to a consistent root-mean-square error of approximately 13 MeV. From a physical perspective, this consistent behavior signifies that the optimized semi-local GGAs have successfully captured the macroscopic, liquid-drop-like background of the nucleus, while the residual deviations appear as periodic oscillations at the magic numbers that could reflect the quantum shell effects.

### [83] [Importance of nuclear quantum effects on the structure of supercooled water around its liquid--liquid critical point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19175)
*Michael Beerbaum,Julian Heske,Jure Gujt,Thomas D. Kühne*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 通过比较经典分子动力学（classical molecular dynamics）和路径积分分子动力学（path-integral molecular dynamics）模拟，发现核量子效应（nuclear quantum effects, NQE）会明显地改变过冷水（supercooled water）中液-液相变（liquid--liquid phase transition）的结构特征，需要在解释该相变时必须加以考虑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过冷水被认为存在低密度液态与高密度液态之间的液-液相变，该相变可能终止于实验上难以到达的“无人区（no man's land）”中的液-液临界点。由于氢原子质量轻，核量子效应（NQE）可能改变用于识别该相变的结构特征，因此需要评估NQE的影响。

Method: 采用基于柔性q-TIP4P/F类水模型，在深度过冷条件下分别进行经典分子动力学模拟（classical MD）和路径积分分子动力学模拟（path-integral MD），并对两者的结果进行对比分析。

Result: 经典模拟在180 K、180–220 MPa之间显示出明显的密度变化，而路径积分模拟则表现出更平滑的压力依赖性。径向分布函数（radial distribution functions）和键序参数（bond-order parameters）表明，NQE展宽了成对关联，降低了第一水合壳层的四面体有序度（tetrahedral order），并略微增加了Steinhardt $Q_6$参数。

Conclusion: NQE同时改变了低密度液态与高密度液态的结构，因此在解释过冷水中液-液相变的结构特征时必须将核量子效应纳入考虑。

Abstract: Supercooled water is expected to exhibit a liquid--liquid phase transition between low- and high-density liquid states, possibly terminating in a liquid--liquid critical point in the experimentally difficult no man's land. Because the hydrogen atoms are light, nuclear quantum effects (NQE) may alter the structural signatures used to identify this transition. Here, we compare classical molecular dynamics and path-integral molecular dynamics simulations of a flexible q-TIP4P/F-like water model in the deeply supercooled regime. The classical simulations show a pronounced density change at 180 K between 180 and 220 MPa, whereas the path-integral simulations exhibit a smoother pressure dependence. Radial distribution functions and bond-order parameters show that NQE broaden pair correlations, reduce the tetrahedral order of the first hydration shell, and slightly increase the Steinhardt $Q_6$ parameter. These results demonstrate that NQE modify both low- and high-density liquid structures and therefore need to be included when interpreting structural signatures of the liquid--liquid transition in supercooled water.

### [84] [Prebiotic magnetite enables chirality-magnetic surface feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19387)
*Jose A. P. M. Devienne,Ziwei Liu,Clancy Z. Jiang,Nicholas J. Tosca,Thomas Ginnis,Dimitar D. Sasselov,Richard J. Harrison,S. Furkan Ozturk*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过模拟前生物条件下磁铁矿的合成，发现其以单涡旋和多涡旋磁畴态为主导，并利用三维微磁学模拟证明这些颗粒在与自旋极化的同手性化合物相互作用时会发生不可逆的交换驱动再磁化，从而为早期地球生物分子手性均一性的建立和维持提供了一种鲁棒机制。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本研究通过两种地球化学上可行的途径——紫外驱动光氧化和亚硝酸盐介导的Fe(II)氧化——合成磁铁矿，并对产物进行磁性测量和电子显微镜表征。同时采用三维微磁学模拟（3D micromagnetic simulations）分析磁畴态及其与自旋极化手性化合物的相互作用。

Result: 合成的磁铁矿以单涡旋和多涡旋磁畴态（single-vortex and multi-vortex magnetic domain states）为主，其磁性特征与先前CISS实验常用的纳米制备薄膜基底显著不同。模拟表明，单畴（single-domain）和涡旋态颗粒在与自旋极化（spin-polarized）的同手性化合物相互作用时会发生不可逆的交换驱动再磁化（exchange-driven re-magnetization）。

Conclusion: 磁铁矿的这种磁性不可逆性为储存和增强微弱的手性偏差（chiral bias）提供了一种鲁棒机制，表明前生物磁铁矿可能对早期地球上手性偏差的出现和稳定化有所贡献。

Abstract: The emergence of biomolecular homochirality requires both an initial symmetry-breaking event and a mechanism to amplify and preserve a chiral imbalance. Magnetic minerals have been shown to function as chiral agents through the chiral-induced spin selectivity (CISS) effect and may have enabled homochirality on early Earth, yet the magnetic properties of magnetite formed under realistic prebiotic conditions remain unexplored. Here we show that magnetite synthesized through two geochemically plausible pathways - UV-driven photo-oxidation and nitrite-mediated oxidation of Fe(II) - produces particles dominated by single-vortex and multi-vortex magnetic domain states. Magnetic measurements and electron microscopy confirm that these populations differ markedly from the nano-fabricated thin-film substrates conventionally used in previous CISS experiments. Using 3D micromagnetic simulations, we demonstrate that single-domain and vortex-state grains undergo irreversible, exchange-driven re-magnetization when interacting with spin-polarized homochiral compounds. This magnetic irreversibility provides a robust mechanism for storing and reinforcing weak chiral bias, suggesting that prebiotic magnetite could have contributed to the emergence and stabilization of persistent chiral bias on the early Earth.

### [85] [Accelerated "on-the-fly" coupled-cluster path-integral molecular dynamics: Impact of nuclear quantum effects on an asymmetric proton](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19858)
*Thomas Spura,Hossam Elgabarty,Thomas D. Kühne*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限温度模拟中，电子关联（electron correlation）和核量子效应（nuclear quantum effects）通常分开处理，缺乏能同时高效兼顾这两者的计算方法。为实现可预测的非对称氢键模拟，亟需发展能够同时处理相关电子结构与核量子涨落的计算框架。

Method: 该方法基于量子环聚合物收缩（quantum ring-polymer contraction, qRPC）技术：廉价的Hartree-Fock势在全环聚合物（full ring-polymer）上评估，而昂贵的耦合簇（coupled-cluster）修正仅在质心（centroid）上评估。qRPC分解进一步与第二类Car-Parrinello类动力学（用于Hartree-Fock参考）以及基组一致的耦合簇与去激发振幅外推相结合。三种加速层的组合是实现可行关联PIMD计算的关键。

Result: 应用于水与甲醛共享质子的体系。核量子效应使共价X–H键长分布展宽，降低了共享质子偏向甲醛的偏差，平均质子转移坐标从0.206 Å移至0.135 Å。质子更靠近甲醛的概率从81.7%降至61.1%。核磁屏蔽张量（nuclear magnetic shielding tensor）显示，电子关联与核量子效应量级相当且可能作用方向相反。

Conclusion: 非对称氢键的可预测模拟需要同时处理相关电子结构与核量子涨落，本文提出的加速PIMD方法为此类模拟提供了可行的计算途径。

Abstract: We present an accelerated ``on-the-fly'' coupled-cluster path-integral molecular dynamics (PIMD) method for finite-temperature simulations in which electron correlation and nuclear quantum effects are treated simultaneously. The approach is based on our quantum ring-polymer contraction (qRPC) technique, in which the inexpensive Hartree-Fock potential is evaluated on the full ring-polymer, while the expensive coupled-cluster correction is evaluated on the centroid only. This qRPC decomposition is combined with a second-generation Car-Parrinello-like dynamics of the Hartree-Fock reference and a basis-consistent extrapolation of the coupled-cluster and de-excitation amplitudes. The combination of all three acceleration layers is essential for making correlated PIMD calculations feasible. We apply the method to a proton shared by water and formaldehyde. Relative to classical nuclei, nuclear quantum effects broaden covalent X--H bond-length distributions, reduce the bias of the shared proton toward formaldehyde, and shift the mean proton-transfer coordinate from 0.206 to 0.135A. The probability of finding the proton closer to formaldehyde decreases from 81.7$\%$ to 61.1$\%$. The corresponding nuclear magnetic shielding tensors show that electron correlation and nuclear quantum effects are of comparable magnitude and can act in opposite directions. These results demonstrate that predictive simulations of asymmetric hydrogen bonds require a simultaneous treatment of correlated electronic structure and nuclear quantum fluctuations.

</details>

### [86] [Multi-mode Floquet NEGF method for driven quantum transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19296)
*Vahid Mosallanejad,Wenjie Dou*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于非微扰Floquet的非平衡格林函数（NEGF）方法，用于研究受多个独立驱动项（多模）同时驱动的量子系统中的电子输运。该方法通过两步变换从Kadanoff-Baym方程导出双模Floquet NEGF，并推广至多驱动情况，通过双驱动下的电流抑制测试验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以处理量子系统同时受到多个独立驱动（multi-mode）时的电子输运问题，传统微扰方法在多驱动场景下适用性受限。

Method: 基于非微扰（non-perturbative）Floquet理论建立非平衡格林函数（NEGF）框架。首先通过两步变换从Kadanoff-Baym方程推导推迟-超前格林函数（retarded-advanced Green's function），得到双模Floquet NEGF；随后将双模情况推广至任意多驱动情形，并通过对数算符（number operator）和流算符（current operator）的期望值进行详细阐述完成推导。

Result: 测试结果表明，额外施加的一个正弦非对角驱动（sinusoidal off-diagonal driving）在仔细选择驱动频率的条件下，能够显著改变由另一个驱动导致的电流抑制（current suppression）现象。

Conclusion: 所建立的方法可广泛应用于受复杂多驱动项驱动的开放量子系统（open quantum systems）中的输运问题研究。

Abstract: We present a non-perturbative Floquet-based non-equilibrium Green's function (NEGF) method to study electron transport in a quantum system driven simultaneously by multiple independent terms (multi-mode). We first derive the two-mode Floquet NEGF based on two-step transformations of the retarded-advanced Green's function from the Kadanoff-Baym equation. This derivation proceeds by elaborating on the expectation values of the number and current operators. The two-mode Floquet NEGF is then extended to cases with multiple drivings. The method is tested by investigating current suppression in the presence of two drivings. We show that an extra sinusoidal off-diagonal driving can cause substantial modification to the current suppression, provided careful selection of the driving frequency. Consequently, we expect that the established method has broad applications in a wide range of open quantum systems driven by complicated drivings.

### [87] [Self-Decelerating Bright Exciton-Polariton Solitons in Bound-State-in-Continuum Microcavities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19913)
*Xingran Xu,Chunyu Jia*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用驱动-耗散型Gross-Pitaevskii方程（driven-dissipative Gross-Pitaevskii equation），并与描述激子库（excitonic reservoir）的速率方程（rate equation）耦合；利用拉格朗日变分方法（Lagrangian variational approach）推导孤子轨迹与速度的解析表达式。

Result: BICs能够有效稳定凝聚态，抑制辐射衰变（radiative decay）；BIC工程化的亮孤子在传播过程中表现出显著的自减速（self-deceleration），最终停止于由初始动量和系统内禀参数共同决定的位置。

Conclusion: 研究表明，基于BICs的亮激子-极化激元孤子为在非厄米体系中操纵极化激元流提供了新途径，其自减速行为具有潜在的应用价值。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the formation and dynamics of bright exciton-polariton solitons in systems engineered with Bound States in the Continuum. By employing a driven-dissipative Gross-Pitaevskii equation coupled with a rate equation for the excitonic reservoir, we demonstrate that BICs provide a robust platform for stabilizing the condensate against radiative decay. Using a Lagrangian variational approach, we derive analytical expressions for the trajectory and velocity of these bright solitonic excitations. We find that the propagation of these BIC-engineered structures exhibits distinct self-deceleration, eventually halting at a final position determined by the initial momentum and intrinsic system parameters. Furthermore, we analyze the dynamical stability of these solitons. Our findings offer valuable insights into the manipulation of polaritonic flows in non-Hermitian systems.

### [88] [4D and 5D Layer Codes through Color Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18961)
*Andrew C. Yuan,Nouédyn Baspin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种显式的Calderbank-Shor-Steane（CSS）码构造，将Layer码推广到D=4,5维度。该构造基于嵌入量子低密度奇偶校验码（qLDPC codes），通过引入“颜色路由”（color routing）克服了此前推广尝试中的障碍，并精确饱和了D=4,5维度的BPT界限。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于嵌入量子低密度奇偶校验码（qLDPC codes）的显式Calderbank-Shor-Steane（CSS）码构造。从一个参数为[[n,k,d]]且能量壁垒为Δ的码出发，构造出D=4,5维的Layer码。核心创新在于使用“颜色路由”（color routing）技术来解析检查层（check layers）和线缺陷（line defects）的结构，从而克服了此前推广尝试中遇到的难题。

Result: 所构造的D=4,5维度Layer码的参数为[[Θ(n^{D/(D-2)}), k, Θ(dn^{1/(D-2)})]]，能量壁垒为Ω(Δ)。当使用良好的qLDPC码作为输入时，该构造精确饱和了D=4,5维度的BPT界限（BPT bounds）。

Conclusion: 本文的构造展示了更高维度Layer码的模块化（modular）特性，使其尽管在物理上受限于三维空间，仍适用于由模块化网络补丁（modular network patches）构成的架构。该工作通过颜色路由成功解决了此前推广中存在的结构性问题。

Abstract: We introduce and explicit Calderbank-Shor-Steane (CSS) code construction that generalizes the Layer codes to $D=4,5$ dimensions. Much like its predecessor, the present construction is based on embedding quantum low-density parity check (qLDPC) codes; from an $[[n,k,d]]$ code with energy barrier $Δ$, we obtain a $D=4,5$ dimensional Layer code with parameters $[[Θ(n^{D/(D-2)}), k, Θ(dn^{1/(D-2)})]]$ and energy barrier $Ω(Δ)$. Using good qLDPC codes as input, our construction saturates the $D=4,5$ dimensional BPT bounds exactly. The higher dimensional Layer Codes are modular, and thus well suited to architectures composed of modular network patches, despite our physical limitation to three dimensions. We overcome the hurdles encountered by previous generalization attempts through the use of \textit{color routing}, allowing us to resolve the structure of the check layers and line defects.

*Sebastian Holmén,T. Rick Perche*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计一组无带隙粒子探测器构成晶格，将其作为局域探针；利用时空多极展开分析探测器的受扰响应，量化有限大小相互作用区域带来的偏差；将场的两点函数表示为探测器可观测关联（detector correlations）的函数形式。

Result: 该方法为非微扰且完全基于实验可测量的探测器关联来重构量子场的两点函数提供了可行协议；同时，通过多极展开定量刻画了有限大小相互作用区域导致的偏差。

Conclusion: 该协议赋予了量子场论中“态”以操作性定义，为非微扰框架下场关联函数的局域探针测量提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We present a non-perturbative method through which local probes can access the two-point function of a quantum field within a region of spacetime. By considering a lattice of gapless particle detectors, we identified the probe observables that encode the field's two-point function. We quantify the discrepancies introduced by physical finite-sized interaction regions by performing a spacetime multipole expansion of the smeared two-point function. Our protocol expresses the two-point function entirely in terms of measurable detectors correlations, providing an operational notion of states in QFT.

### [90] [Quantum Magic Reveals CP Phases Invisible to Entanglement in Spin-0 Decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19117)
*Nicolas Viaux,Ariel Norambuena,Pedro Orellana*

TL;DR: 该论文指出标准量子信息度量在自旋-0→ff衰变中对CP（电荷宇称）不敏感，而引入基于稳定子魔力的Rényi熵作为新的CP观测量，给出了闭式解，并提出了两种可实验检验的CP（电荷宇称）探针，其中线性振幅在HL-LHC（高亮度大型强子对撞机）上对H→τ⁺τ⁻具有发现级灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准标量量子信息度量（如并发度（concurrence）、纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）等）在理想自旋-0→ff衰变中对CP（电荷宇称）角度不敏感，存在“盲点”问题，亟需构造新的CP敏感观测量。

Method: 引入稳定子魔力（stabilizer magic）概念，在自旋分析的物理泡利框架（Pauli frame）中固定，利用稳定子Rényi熵（stabilizer Rényi entropy）构造对CP角度敏感的闭式解，并据此提出两种魔力启发的CP观测量（CP witnesses）。

Result: 稳定子Rényi熵在CP确定相和Clifford相位（Clifford phases）处为零，在最大非Clifford混合（non-Clifford mixing）处达到峰值；线性振幅CP探针的效率是四次方对应物的14.3倍，且在HL-LHC（高亮度大型强子对撞机）上对H→τ⁺τ⁻过程能达到发现级灵敏度。

Conclusion: 稳定子魔力可以突破标准量子信息度量在CP探测中的盲点，为高能物理中对撞机实验（如HL-LHC）提供更高效的CP破缺检验工具。

Abstract: All standard scalar quantum-information measures -- concurrence, negativity, entanglement entropy, the optimized CHSH bound, and quantum Fisher information -- are CP-blind in ideal \\ spin-0 $\to f\bar f$ decays because the two-qubit spin state is maximally entangled for every CP angle. We show that stabilizer magic, fixed in the physical Pauli frame of spin analysis, escapes this blind spot: the stabilizer Rényi entropy admits an exact closed form, vanishing at CP-definite and Clifford phases and peaking at maximal non-Clifford mixing. Two experimentally accessible, magic-inspired CP witnesses follow; the linear amplitude is $14.3\times$ more efficient than its quartic counterpart and reaches discovery-level sensitivity at the HL-LHC for $H\toτ^+τ^-$.

### [91] [Spin-Induced Non-Markovian Time-Crystal-Like Dynamics and Fractal Scaling in the Bateman Dual Oscillator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19917)
*Partha Nandi,Giuseppe Vitiello*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Bateman双振子框架下证明，封闭量子系统无需外部驱动即可产生持续的类时间晶体动力学。通过自旋诱导的空间变形构造有效Bateman振子结构，系统由时间无关厄米哈密顿量描述，在全局幺正演化下，对放大扇区求迹后得到的非马尔可夫约化动力学可维持子系统可观测量的持续振荡，产生无需周期性驱动或自发对称破缺的类时间晶体时间序，并展示对数螺线轨迹与自相似分形标度。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Bateman双振子框架，在非相对论(2+1)维系统中通过自旋诱导的空间变形构造有效Bateman振子结构；对系统进行量子化后获得描述阻尼振子与放大振子相干耦合的时间无关厄米哈密顿量，并通过对放大扇区求迹导出有效非马尔可夫约化动力学。

Result: 非马尔可夫记忆效应维持了子系统可观测量的持续振荡，产生了无需外部周期性驱动或平衡态自发对称破缺的类时间晶体时间序；该动力学还展示了对数螺线轨迹和自相似分形标度，揭示了相干耗散动力学、非马尔可夫记忆效应与涌现时间序之间的直接联系。

Conclusion: 该机制源于非平衡约化子系统动力学而非全哈密顿量的平衡态期望值，因此不满足平衡态时间晶体禁戒定理的假设条件，在全局幺正量子系统中实现了类时间晶体有序的涌现。

Abstract: Can a closed quantum system generate persistent time-crystal-like dynamics without external driving? Within the Bateman dual oscillator framework, we show that the answer is affirmative. We consider a nonrelativistic (2+1)-dimensional system in which spin-induced spatial deformation generates an effective Bateman oscillator structure. After quantization, the system is governed by a time-independent Hermitian Hamiltonian describing coherent coupling between damped and amplified oscillator sectors while preserving the total energy of the global doubled system. Tracing over the amplified sector, we derive an effective non-Markovian reduced dynamics for the observable subsystem. The resulting memory effects sustain persistent oscillations of subsystem observables and generate emergent time-crystal-like temporal ordering without external periodic driving or equilibrium spontaneous symmetry breaking. Since the oscillatory behavior originates from nonequilibrium reduced subsystem dynamics rather than equilibrium expectation values of the full Hamiltonian, the mechanism lies outside the assumptions of conventional no-go theorems for equilibrium time crystals. The same dynamics further exhibits logarithmic-spiral trajectories and self-similar fractal scaling, revealing a direct connection between coherent dissipative dynamics, non-Markovian memory effects, and emergent temporal ordering in a globally unitary quantum system. In this specific sense, "watching the growth" of these self-similar structures corresponds to observing the gradual formation of time-crystal-like ordering.

### [92] [Noise-induced Simulability Transition from Operator Scrambling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18943)
*Neil Dowling,Xhek Turkeshi,Jacopo De Nardis,Guglielmo Lami*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过算子稳定子Rényi熵（operator stabilizer Rényi entropies）的矩，确定了随机量子电路（random quantum circuits）在无噪声和有局部噪声两种情况下的有限深度Pauli谱（finite-depth Pauli spectrum），揭示了无噪声电路中的层次化热化行为以及噪声诱导的算子复杂度相变（noise-induced transition in operator complexity），并严格证明在特定噪声阈值以下经典模拟依然指数困难。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体动力学（quantum many-body dynamics）或量子计算在海森堡绘景（Heisenberg picture）中的复杂度由初始简单算子指数级地展开为众多Pauli串（Pauli strings）的叠加所决定。该展开系数构成Pauli谱（Pauli spectrum），其结构直接影响基于截断Pauli展开的经典算法的性能。本文旨在系统刻画随机量子电路中Pauli谱的有限深度行为，并探究噪声如何影响算子复杂度及经典可模拟性。

Method: 通过算子稳定子Rényi熵（operator stabilizer Rényi entropies）的矩（moments）来刻画随机量子电路的Pauli谱。分别分析无噪声和有局部噪声两种情况下的有限深度电路。

Result: 在无噪声电路中，低阶矩在相对较浅深度便达到平衡，而高阶矩由于对罕见的大振幅Pauli系数敏感，需要远更大的深度才能平衡。在有噪声电路中，每个周期（cycle）的误差存在一个临界值 γ_c N = O(1)：高于此阈值时算子无法达到完全热化分布，仅支撑于异常稀疏的Pauli串子集上；低于此阈值时，经典模拟依然指数困难。

Conclusion: 噪声并非自动导致经典可模拟性；在低于临界噪声的区域内，量子动力学的内在困难性依然保持。噪声诱导的算子复杂度相变界定了本质上困难的量子动力学与经典可访问的动力学之间的分界线。

Abstract: The complexity of simulating quantum many-body dynamics, or quantum computations, in the Heisenberg picture is governed by the scrambling of initially simple operators into superpositions of exponentially many Pauli strings. The corresponding expansion coefficients define the Pauli spectrum, whose structure controls the performance of classical algorithms based on truncating Pauli expansions. Here we determine the finite-depth Pauli spectrum of random quantum circuits, both in the noiseless case and in the presence of local noise, through its moments, given by the operator stabilizer Rényi entropies. In noiseless circuits, we uncover a hierarchy in the approach to the fully scrambled regime: low moments equilibrate at relatively short depths, while higher moments, which are sensitive to rare, large-amplitude Pauli coefficients, require parametrically larger depths. In noisy circuits, scrambling competes with an effective suppression of operator spreading. Above a critical error per cycle $γ_c N=\mathcal{O}(1)$, the operator fails to reach the fully scrambled distribution and remains supported on an atypically sparse subset of Pauli strings. Conversely, below this scale, we rigorously show that classical simulation remains exponentially hard, demonstrating that finite noise does not automatically imply classical simulability. The resulting noise-induced transition in operator complexity therefore delineates the boundary between intrinsically hard quantum dynamics and those that remain classically accessible.

</details>


### [93] [Translation-invariant quantum low-density parity-check codes from compactified fracton models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19298)
*Cassandra M. Hopkin,Victor V. Albert,Dominic J. Williamson*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文为一大类平移不变量子纠错码（包括局域和长程校验、分形码(fracton codes)以及所有阿贝尔双块群代数(A2BGA)码）提供了一个统一的理论框架，揭示了它们通过超图乘积分形模型(parent code)的紧致化(compactification)而产生的层级关系。该框架将双变量自行车(BB)码等主要实例联系起来，并扩展了码参数界限与对穿门(transversal gates)及能垒(energy barriers)的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平移对称且局域校验的量子纠错码（如三维及更高维度的分形码(fracton codes)）缺乏统一的描述框架；同时，具有长程校验的平移不变码在二维小尺寸实例中表现出惊人性能，但缺乏普适性理解。本文旨在为这两类平移不变码（局域与长程）提供统一的图像，以揭示其深层结构关联。

Method: 本文利用A2BGA码的平衡积(balanced product)结构，将其提升为高维超图乘积分形模型(parent code)；通过对该parent code进行不同的紧致化操作，生成多种后裔码(descendant codes)，从而建立起统一的理论框架。

Result: 所有具有相同校验权重的BB码均源自同一个parent超图乘积分形模型；Wang与Pryadko关于广义自行车码(generalized bicycle codes)的码参数界限被成功推广至A2BGA码。此外，本文提供了穿门(transversal gates)与能垒(energy barriers)受限于parent分形模型的猜想。

Conclusion: 本文建立的平衡积统一框架不仅涵盖了众多分形码和A2BGA码（包括BB码），还揭示了平移不变后裔码的性质受其parent分形模型限制，为未来研究穿门操作和能垒提供了理论方向。

Abstract: Quantum error-correcting codes with translation symmetry and local checks have been studied extensively, leading to a wide variety of fracton codes in three or more dimensions which lack a complete unifying picture. Recently, the study of translation-invariant codes with long-range checks has revealed impressive performance for small fixed-size instances in two dimensions. Here, we provide a unifying picture for a large family of translation-invariant codes, both local and long-range, that captures many fracton codes and all Abelian Two-Block Group Algebra (A2BGA) codes, including the Bivariate Bicycle (BB) codes. The balanced product structure of A2BGA codes leads to a local parent code that is a hypergraph product fracton model in a higher dimension. Different compactifications of a parent code produce a wide variety of descendant codes which provides a unifying picture for their properties. In particular, all BB codes with the same check weight are derived from a single parent hypergraph product fracton model. This construction allows us to extend Wang and Pryadko's code-parameter bounds for Generalized Bicycle codes to A2BGA codes. We conjecture that the transversal gates and energy barriers of the translation-invariant descendant codes are limited by those of their parent fracton models.

</details>


### [94] [Subsystem relaxation and a calibrated sampling diagnostic for programmable quantum annealers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19381)
*Luis Lozano*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在D-Wave量子退火器上实施子系统-环境协议，发现大或强耦合环境可使子系统达到初始状态无关，并利用记忆序参量与条件玻尔兹曼参考的距离诊断错误的盆地俘获，同时指出局部更新模型严重误预测松弛行为，而非局域经典采样能有效恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可编程量子退火器（quantum annealer）被用作开放系统采样器，但反向退火（reverse annealing）何时擦除制备记忆、读出结果代表什么尚不清楚，因此需要系统性验证。

Method: 在两个D-Wave量子退火器上实施子系统-环境协议，改变环境大小、耦合强度、无序、制备方式、几何结构和量子处理单元（QPU）代际。

Result: 六量子比特子系统在环境大或强耦合时实现初始状态独立；淬火无序（quenched disorder）和非典型环境状态会阻碍弛豫。记忆序参量与校准后的条件玻尔兹曼参考（conditional-Boltzmann reference）的距离诊断出仅靠记忆缺失无法发现的少见的错误盆地俘获（wrong-basin trapping）；记忆保持条件远离参考（中位数0.35）。弛豫后的铁磁读出近乎确定，因此小距离仅作为一致性检查而非热力学测试。局部更新模型对QPU松弛的预测误差约七倍，而非局域经典采样能恢复实际行为。

Conclusion: 提供了量子退火器采样的子系统级验证协议，揭示了记忆擦除的条件与诊断方法。

Abstract: Programmable quantum annealers are used as open-system samplers, but it is unclear when reverse annealing erases preparation memory and what the readout represents. Here we implement a subsystem-environment protocol on two D-Wave quantum annealers, varying environment size, coupling, disorder, preparation, geometry and QPU generation. A six-qubit subsystem becomes initial-state independent when the environment is large or strongly coupled, while quenched disorder and atypical environment states arrest relaxation. Pairing the memory order parameter with the distance to a calibrated conditional-Boltzmann reference yields a diagnostic that flags rare wrong-basin trapping memory loss alone misses; memory-retaining conditions stay far from the reference (median 0.35). Relaxed ferromagnetic readouts are near-deterministic, so small distances there are a consistency check, not a thermometric test. In a mixed-frustration benchmark, the local-update model practitioners assume mispredicts QPU relaxation roughly sevenfold, whereas non-local classical sampling recovers it. We provide a subsystem-level validation protocol for quantum-annealer sampling.

### [95] [Universal logic gates for coupled period-doubling systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19477)
*Emmanuel D. G. U,Roy D. Jara,Jayson G. Cosme*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于周期驱动系统倍周期态的通用逻辑门架构，通过单个脉冲耦合输入与输出节点，利用耦合强度和脉冲时长精确控制节点状态，实现NAND和NOR逻辑操作。该架构在耗散参量振荡器（DPO）、Kerr参量振荡器（KPO）以及模拟离散时间晶体（DTCs）的开环Dicke晶格模型（DLM）等不同物理系统中均验证了普适性，并展示了在涨落环境下的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在经典与量子计算中，实现通用逻辑操作是计算架构的基础需求。现有方案往往针对特定系统设计，缺乏跨物理平台的普适性。本文旨在提出一种通用的逻辑门架构，能够适配不同类型（经典与量子）的周期驱动系统，并具备鲁棒性。

Method: 提出一种通用架构，利用周期驱动系统中倍周期态（period-doubled states）编码经典信息，通过施加单个脉冲同时耦合两个输入节点和一个输出节点。通过调节耦合强度（coupling strength）和脉冲时长（pulse duration）来精确控制节点状态，实现NAND和NOR逻辑门操作。该架构在三种不同系统中进行验证：耗散参量振荡器（dissipative parametric oscillators, DPO）经典网络、Kerr参量振荡器（Kerr parametric oscillators, KPO）量子网络，以及模拟离散时间晶体（discrete time crystals, DTCs）的周期驱动开环Dicke晶格模型（open Dicke lattice model, DLM）。

Result: 识别出该逻辑门架构成立的有效参数区间，并在存在涨落（fluctuations）的条件下展示了该架构的鲁棒性（robustness）。通过多系统验证，证明了该协议在经典和量子周期驱动系统中的普适性（universality）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的通用逻辑门架构为在周期驱动系统中实现通用计算提供了一种跨平台可行的方案，兼具鲁棒性和可调性，适用于包括离散时间晶体模拟系统在内的多种物理平台。

Abstract: We propose a general architecture for universal logic operations using NAND and NOR gates on classical information encoded in period-doubled states of periodically-driven systems. The protocol involves applying a single pulse that simultaneously couple two input nodes with an output node. We show that the states of the nodes can be precisely controlled by tuning the coupling strength and pulse duration, allowing for robust logic gate operation. To highlight the universality of the protocol, we demonstrate its applicability on different systems, such as classical networks of dissi- pative parametric oscillators (DPO), quantum networks of Kerr parametric oscillators (KPO), and the periodically-driven open Dicke lattice model (DLM) emulating discrete time crystals (DTCs). We identify the parameter regimes in which the logic gate architecture is valid, and we showcase its robustness in the presence of fluctuations.

### [96] [Stochastic trajectories and excursions in a double quantum dot system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20166)
*Guilherme Fiusa,Pedro E. Harunari,Alberto J. B. Rosal,John M. Nichol,Gabriel T. Landi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用随机游走（stochastic excursions）这一新形式化框架，对双量子点系统的轨迹层级动力学进行研究，提取热力学流与游走时间之间的复杂关联，并通过计数可观测量与状态可观测量的分析，结合热力学精确性与不确定性关系，揭示了该系统中非平衡涨落的结构与性能约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的全计数统计（full counting statistics）方法难以直接解析复杂轨迹中不同子过程之间的关联。本文旨在引入随机游走框架，通过将复杂轨迹过滤为子轨迹，以更精细地揭示双量子点系统中热力学流与游走时间之间的内在关联，并考察非平衡涨落的结构。

Method: 采用随机游走形式化框架，对双量子点系统进行轨迹层级分析。定义计数可观测量（counting observables）为一次游走内跃迁计数与分配权重的线性组合，并引入状态可观测量（state observables）以分析系统占据状态及其关联。通过计算平均与噪声贡献，结合热动力学不确定性关系（thermo-kinetic uncertainty relations）分析电流精确性的约束来源。

Result: 针对电荷流、动力学活动性与熵产生三个主要计数可观测量，计算了其平均与噪声贡献，揭示了双量子点系统运行机制。在轨迹层级分析了输运结果分布，并将结果与成功/非成功事件之间的权衡关联。通过热动力学不确定性关系表明，不同区间下电流精确性分别受熵产生或动力学活动性的根本约束。

Conclusion: 本研究展示了随机游走框架作为分析非平衡涨落与多种感兴趣量的工具箱的实用性，揭示了双量子点系统中热力学流与不确定性的结构特征，并为精炼不确定性关系及理解介观系统输运提供了新方向。

Abstract: We investigate the trajectory-level dynamics of a double quantum dot system using the newly developed formalism of stochastic excursions. This approach extends full counting statistics by enabling a filtering of complex trajectories into sub-trajectories, which provide access to the intricate correlations between thermodynamic currents and excursion times. Counting observables are the main object of study in the stochastic excursion framework. Those are defined as a linear combination of transition counts multiplied by their assigned weights within one excursion. For three main counting observables -- charge current, dynamical activity, and entropy production -- we compute averages and noise contributions and show how they provide insights into the operation of the double quantum dot system. At the trajectory level, we analyze outcome distributions for transport and connect the results with trade-offs between successful and unsuccessful events that shape overall performance. We further introduce state observables, which depend on the state visited rather than the transition itself, and discuss the population of the two dots, as well as their correlations. Finally, we discuss thermodynamics of precision through thermo-kinetic uncertainty relations, showing how current precision in different regimes is fundamentally constrained either by entropy production or by dynamical activity. Altogether, our work is a case study that highlights the utility of the excursion framework as a toolkit to analyze many quantities of interest and to uncover the structure of nonequilibrium fluctuations. Moreover, it also suggests new avenues for refining uncertainty relations and understanding transport in mesoscopic systems.

</details>

Here, we demonstrate the direct observation of transient modulation of HPhPs induced by local photocarrier generation in WS$_2$/hBN heterostructures using ultrafast infrared scanning near-field optical microscopy. We implement grating-based spectral filtering of broadband near-field scattering to simultaneously achieve nanoscale and femtosecond spatiotemporal resolution together with fine spectral selectivity. This ultrafast nano-imaging technique reveals that photocarriers in WS$_2$ modulate the polaritonic field amplitudes and wavelengths of HPhPs in hBN. ### [98] [Near-Field Vibrational Energy Transfer for Mid-Infrared Upconversion in Plasmonic Nanogaps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19498)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Förster能量转移是现代光子学的基础，但在中红外（MIR）区域建立类似的振动能量转移路径极具挑战性，因为亚皮秒级分子内振动再分布（intramolecular vibrational redistribution, IVR）会抑制分子间耦合。本研究旨在克服IVR竞争，实现MIR振动供体-受体转移。

Method: 利用自组装分子间隔层定义的金属-分子-金属环形腔（metal–molecule–metal ring cavities）产生亚2纳米等离激元纳米间隙（plasmonic nanogaps），实现极端横向场约束。连续波（continuous-wave）MIR激发选择性布居-C≡N振动供体，通过等离激元增强的近场耦合将能量转移至附近电子受体，产生反斯托克斯（anti-Stokes）可见发射。

Result: 观察到上转换效率超过0.3%，该效率受到等离激元介导的转移速率与IVR之间竞争的限制。

Abstract: Förster energy transfer underpins modern photonics, yet establishing an analogous vibrational pathway in the mid-infrared (MIR) remains highly challenging, as sub-picosecond intramolecular vibrational redistribution (IVR) suppresses intermolecular coupling. Here we demonstrate vibrational donor--acceptor transfer in the MIR and subsequent upconversion to visible luminescence enabled by sub-2 nm plasmonic nanogaps. The extreme lateral field confinement in metal--molecule--metal ring cavities defined by self-assembled molecular spacers couples efficiently to in-plane molecular dipoles. Continuous-wave MIR excitation selectively populates $-\mathrm{C}\equiv\mathrm{N}$ vibrational donors, and plasmon-enhanced near-field coupling transfers this energy to nearby electronic acceptors, generating anti-Stokes visible emission under low power densities. Upconversion efficiencies exceeding $0.3\%$ are observed, limited by competition between the plasmon-mediated transfer rate and IVR. These results show that extreme plasmonic confinement can redirect molecular vibrational relaxation pathways, opening a route toward vibrational nanophotonics, intermolecular interactions for bioimaging, and room-temperature MIR detection based on molecular degrees of freedom.

### [99] [Engineering Tunable Synthetic Su-Schrieffer-Heeger Chains in Liquid Crystal Microcavities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19664)
*Joanna Mędrzycka,Luciano S. Ricco,Piotr Kapuściński,Marcin Muszyński,Przemysław Morawiak,Rafał Mazur,Rafał Węgłowski,Eva Oton,Przemysław Kula,Wiktor Piecek,Jacek Szczytko*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学微腔是模拟传统材料中难以实现的拓扑相的有力平台，而液晶微腔（LCMC）在室温下具备优异的可调谐性，但此前尚未将LCMC用于构建可调谐的合成拓扑哈密顿量。本文旨在设计一种二聚化ULH纹理的LCMC，以实现电压调控的拓扑光子态。

Result: 所设计的LCMC中的光子势描述了具有正交线偏振的两条耦合SSH链，偏振自由度作为有效的赝自旋。外加电压可连续调谐链间耦合，从而控制偏振依赖的相互作用。

Conclusion: 液晶微腔（LCMC）被证明是一种适用于可调谐合成拓扑哈密顿量的多功能平台，能够通过电压灵活调控拓扑光子态，为室温下的拓扑光子学（topological photonics）研究提供了新途径。

Abstract: Optical microcavities have emerged as a powerful platform for emulating topological phases challenging to realize in conventional materials, offering precise control over dispersion, light confinement, and interactions. Here, we design a LCMC hosting a dimerized ULH texture and show that the corresponding photonic potential describes two coupled Su-Schrieffer-Heeger chains with orthogonal linear polarisations, acting as an effective pseudospin degree of freedom. The applied voltage tunes the interchain coupling, enabling polarisation-dependent interactions. These results establish LCMCs as a versatile platform for tunable synthetic topological Hamiltonians.

### [100] [Gang-Kim-Yoon integrality conjectures on adjoint Reidemeister torsions for torus knots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19460)
*Yuji Terashima,Yoshikazu Yamaguchi*

Main category: math.GT

TL;DR: 本文证明了环面结（torus knot）的伴随Reidemeister挠率（adjoint Reidemeister torsion）的(g-1)次幂之和为整数的猜想对所有非负整数g成立。为证明该猜想，作者从模S矩阵（modular S-matrix）角度引入了环面结的Verlinde数（Verlinde numbers），推导了其递推公式与初值，并构建了环面结特征簇（character variety）的双有理模型（birational model），展示了如何从该模型的Hessian矩阵恢复伴随Reidemeister挠率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在证明关于环面结的伴随Reidemeister挠率的(g-1)次幂之和为整数这一猜想，并建立该猜想与模S矩阵及Verlinde数之间的深层联系。

Method: 从模S矩阵（modular S-matrix）出发，引入环面结的Verlinde数（Verlinde numbers），推导其递推公式（recursion formulas）与初值（initial values）。同时，构建环面结特征簇（character variety）的双有理模型（birational model），并利用该定义多项式的Hessian矩阵恢复伴随Reidemeister挠率。

Result: 证明了环面结的伴随Reidemeister挠率的(g-1)次幂之和为整数的猜想对所有非负整数g成立；给出了Verlinde数的递推公式与初值；构造了环面结特征簇的双有理模型，并证明了可通过该模型的Hessian矩阵恢复伴随Reidemeister挠率。

Conclusion: 该猜想对所有环面结及所有非负整数g成立，且Verlinde数的递推公式为整数性提供了直接证明。此外，双有理模型为理解环面结的模S矩阵与特征簇的几何结构提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study the conjecture that a sum of the (g-1)st powers of adjoint Reidemeister torsions for a torus knot is an integer. We prove that the conjecture is true for any torus knot and all non-negative g. To prove the conjecture, we introduce the Verlinde numbers for torus knots from the viewpoint of modular S-matrix and show the recursion formulas and initial values of them. The recursion formulas of Verlinde numbers prove the integrality of the sum of the (g-1)st powers of adjoint Reidemeister torsions. Related to a modular S-matrix, we also provide a birational model of the character variety for a torus knot and show how to recover the adjoint Reidemeister torsion for a torus knot from the Hessian of the polynomial defining the birational model.

</details>

### [101] [Collective charge measurement in quantum dot chains: controlling barrier occupation and tunneling current](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19001)
*Alok Nath Singh,Rafael Sánchez,Andrew N. Jordan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了三量子点（triple-quantum-dot, TQD）系统中受全局量子点接触（quantum point contact, QPC）连续测量影响的非平衡输运，发现全局测量相比单点测量能通过工程化退相干（structured dephasing）显著提升势垒占据率和隧穿电流，并在强测量极限下使稳态独立于哈密顿量参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索全局连续测量（global continuous measurement）对三量子点系统中非平衡输运（nonequilibrium transport）的影响，揭示其与单点测量在机制上的定性差异，并寻找通过工程化退相干优化输运性能的可能性。

Method: 建立一个三量子点系统模型，其中中心量子点作为离散隧道势垒（discrete tunnel barrier），所有三个量子点均与一个量子点接触（QPC）电容耦合，且耦合强度可独立调节。通过该全局测量方案引入结构化的退相干，分析其对势垒占据率和隧穿电流的影响。

Result: 全局测量以与单点测量定性不同的方式影响输运；工程化退相干可显著提高势垒占据率和隧穿电流；在强测量极限下，稳态不再依赖底层哈密顿量参数，势垒占据率在适当测量配置下可趋近1/2；识别出了最大化稳态电流的最优测量配置，并发现简单的中心点读出方案即可实现近最优性能。

Conclusion: 全局量子点接触测量通过工程化退相干为调控三量子点系统的非平衡输运提供了有效手段，强测量极限下的稳态简并性及中心点读出的近最优性具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: We investigate nonequilibrium transport in a triple-quantum-dot (TQD) system, where the central dot acts as a discrete tunnel barrier, subject to continuous monitoring by a quantum point contact (QPC) that is capacitively coupled to all three dots with independently tunable strengths. We show that this global measurement scheme affects transport in a qualitatively distinct manner from single-site measurement. By engineering structured dephasing, measurement provides a significant improvement in the barrier occupation and tunneling current. In the strong-measurement limit, the steady state becomes independent of the underlying Hamiltonian parameters, and the barrier occupation can approach 1/2 for suitable measurement configurations. We identify an optimal measurement configuration that maximizes the steady-state current and show that near-optimal performance can be achieved with a simple central-dot readout scheme.

</details>


### [102] [Optical control of conductivity type and valley polarization via persistent photoconductivity in (Pb,Sn)Se quantum wells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19025)
*Alexander Kazakov,Gauthier Krizman,Valentine V. Volobuev,Michał Szot,Wojciech Wołkanowicz,Chang-Woo Cho,Benjamin A. Piot,Tomasz Wojciechowski,Gunther Springholz,Tomasz Wojtowicz,Tomasz Dietl*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明了持续光电导（persistent photoconductivity, PPC）能够调控(Pb,Sn)Se/(Pb,Eu)Se量子阱中的载流子密度、导电类型及谷极化（valley polarization），并建立了一种无需器件加工的光学栅控（optical gating）手段，用于可重构谷电子学（reconfigurable valleytronic）架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半导体费米能级（Fermi level）的可调谐能力是现代电子学的核心。本文旨在探索能否利用持续光电导（PPC）效应，在不进行器件加工的条件下实现IV-VI族量子阱中载流子类型与谷极化的有效调控。

Method: 实验上，研究者对(Pb,Sn)Se/(Pb,Eu)Se量子阱样品进行光照，诱发费米能级移动；利用霍尔效应（Hall effect）符号反转与量子霍尔平台（quantum Hall plateau）简并度变化确认导电类型转变，并测量高达35 T磁场下的输运性质。理论上，采用朗道能级（Landau level）$k\cdot p$模型进行定量计算。此外，通过弱场磁阻（weak-field magnetoresistance）研究量子局域化（quantum localization）现象，并结合光谱学（spectral studies）确定可逆转PPC效应的光子能量与势垒材料的作用。

Result: 光照使系统从三重简并$\bar{M}$谷二维空穴气（two-dimensional hole gas）转变为具有类似迁移率的单$\bar{\Gamma}$谷极化电子气（electron gas）。该光致状态在低温下持续超过$10^3$分钟。霍尔斜率符号反转与量子霍尔平台简并度变化证实了上述转变。$k\cdot p$模型计算与实验数据定量吻合。弱场磁阻研究揭示了补偿型窄带隙半导体中弱局域化与强局域化之间的量子局域化转变。光谱研究确定了对PPC效应具有逆转作用的特定光子能量，并将费米能级的光致上移归因于施主与受主缺陷态的具体能量位置。

Conclusion: 持续光电导（PPC）是IV-VI族量子阱中一种有效的光学栅控手段，为可重构谷电子学架构提供了多功能平台。

Abstract: The ability to tune the Fermi level of semiconductors is at the heart of modern electronics. Here, we demonstrate that persistent photoconductivity (PPC) enables tuning of carrier density, conductivity type, and, consequently, the valley polarization in (Pb,Sn)Se/(Pb,Eu)Se quantum wells. Illumination of these samples induces Fermi level shifts that convert the system from a threefold-degenerate $\bar{M}$-valley two-dimensional hole gas to a single $\barΓ$-valley-polarized electron gas with similar values of mobility. The optically induced state persists for more than $10^{3}$ minutes at cryogenic temperatures and enables stepwise optical gating without the need for device processing. These transitions are confirmed by the sign inversion of the Hall slope and the modification of quantum Hall plateau degeneracies measured in magnetic fields up to 35 T. Landau level $k\cdot p$ model calculations quantitatively reproduce the experimental data. Furthermore, studies of weak-field magnetoresistance demonstrate the significance of quantum localization phenomena at the transition between the weakly and strongly localized regimes in compensated narrow-gap semiconductors. Spectral studies allow us to identify the critical role of the barrier material and determine the photon energies that can reverse the PPC effect. The persistent light-induced upward shift of the Fermi level in the $p$-type quantum well is explained in terms of specific energy positions of donor and acceptor defect states in the studied system. Our results demonstrate that PPC is a powerful optical gating tool for the IV-VI quantum wells, a versatile platform for reconfigurable valleytronic architectures.

</details>


### [103] [Transconductance as a Probe of Valley Thermodynamics in Multilayer WSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19212)
*Katsunori Wakabayashi,Souren Adhikary,Tomoaki Kameda*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究发现，在多层WSe₂晶体管中，跨导（transconductance）不仅受电荷积累和迁移率控制，还会因K谷和Γ谷之间的载流子谷间重新分布（inter-valley carrier redistribution）而产生非线性输运特征；通过引入谷磁化率（valley susceptibility）χ_v进行量化，表明跨导可作为探测内部电子自由度（internal electronic degrees of freedom）的电学探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为场效应晶体管（field-effect transistor, FET）的跨导主要取决于电荷积累和载流子迁移率，但多层WSe₂中观察到的异常跨导行为无法用单谷输运模型（single-valley transport model）解释，需要揭示其背后的物理机制。

Method: 通过对比双层、三层WSe₂与单谷系统的输运特性，分离出谷间载流子重新分布对跨导的贡献；引入谷磁化率χ_v ≡ ∂f_Γ/∂V_GS，并证明其受限于固有热力学上限(4k_BT)^{−1}，以此量化谷间响应。

Result: 谷间载流子重新分布在双层WSe₂中抑制跨导，在三层WSe₂中使跨导符号反转，而在单谷系统中完全缺失；该异常不影响亚阈值摆幅（subthreshold swing），且无法被陷阱态填充（trap-state filling）或接触电阻（contact resistance）等外在机制复现；在室温阈值附近，双层WSe₂的谷磁化率达到约0.20 V^{−1}。

Conclusion: 跨导异常的符号、幅度和温度依赖性提供了可直接测量的谷热力学（valley thermodynamics）指纹，表明跨导可作为探测内部电子自由度的电学探针，揭示了标准晶体管测量中此前隐藏的非线性响应。

Abstract: Transconductance is a central figure of merit in field-effect transistors, typically governed by charge accumulation and carrier mobility. In multilayer WSe$_2$ transistors, however, it is shown to carry a nonlinear transport signature of inter-valley carrier redistribution between the $K$ and $Γ$ valleys. This valley-crossover contribution suppresses transconductance in bilayer WSe$_2$ and reverses sign in trilayer, while remaining absent in single-valley systems. Unlike extrinsic mechanisms such as trap-state filling or contact resistance, the anomaly leaves the subthreshold swing unchanged and cannot be reproduced within conventional single-valley transport models. Introducing the valley susceptibility $χ_v \equiv \partial f_Γ/\partial V_{\rm GS}$, bounded by an intrinsic thermodynamic limit $(4k_BT)^{-1}$, we quantify this response and show that it reaches ${\sim}0.20\,\mathrm{V}^{-1}$ in bilayer WSe$_2$ near threshold at room temperature. The sign, magnitude, and temperature dependence of the anomaly provide directly measurable fingerprints of valley thermodynamics, establishing transconductance as an electrical probe of internal electronic degrees of freedom and revealing a previously hidden nonlinear response in standard transistor measurements.

</details>


### [104] [Non-Bloch Quantum Geometry of Non-Hermitian Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19272)
*Junsong Sun,Huaiming Guo,Bohm-Jung Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文为非厄米系统在开边界条件下构建了量子几何（quantum geometry）的统一框架，证明了实空间积分量子度量（integrated quantum metric）与非布洛赫积分量子度量（non-Bloch integrated quantum metric）之间的严格等价性，并引入非布洛赫万尼尔函数（non-Bloch Wannier functions）描述非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect）的局域化性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统布洛赫能带理论（Bloch band theory）无法有效描述开边界条件下非厄米系统（non-Hermitian systems）的量子几何性质，因此需要建立超越布洛赫框架的新理论方法。

Method: 分别在实空间表示（real-space representation）和非布洛赫表示（non-Bloch representation）中定义量子几何量，并在广义布里渊区（generalized Brillouin zone）上建立两者之间的精确等价关系；同时引入局域化的非布洛赫万尼尔函数。

Result: 核心结果是实空间积分量子度量与非布洛赫积分量子度量之间的严格等价性；此外，非布洛赫积分量子度量给出了非布洛赫万尼尔函数扩展泛函（spread functional）的规范不变部分。

Conclusion: 量子几何为表征开边界条件下非厄米能带结构以及趋肤模的局域化性质提供了自然框架。

Abstract: We formulate quantum geometry for non-Hermitian systems under open boundary conditions. By defining quantum-geometric quantities in both real-space and non-Bloch representations, we establish a unified framework beyond conventional Bloch band theory. Our central result is an exact equivalence between the real-space integrated quantum metric and a non-Bloch integrated quantum metric defined on the generalized Brillouin zone. We further introduce localized non-Bloch Wannier functions in the presence of the non-Hermitian skin effect and show that the non-Bloch integrated quantum metric gives the gauge-invariant part of their spread functional. These results establish quantum geometry as a natural framework for characterizing open-boundary non-Hermitian band structures and the localization properties encoded in skin modes.

</details>


### [105] [Nonlinear Stabilization of Non-Adiabatic Magnonic Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19647)
*A. M. Tishin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于η算法（η-algorithm）的非线性磁振子（magnonic）平台，用于纳米铁氧体结构中有界非绝热参量激发，通过非线性频率调节器U抑制参量增长、实现动态局域化低占有数磁振子态，并以Co掺杂钇铁石榴石（YIG:Co）为例进行了数值验证和能量规模分析，表明该机制可为低能耗波基信息处理提供物理基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有纳米尺度铁氧体结构中的非绝热参量激发（non-adiabatic parametric excitation）缺乏有效的有界控制机制，参量驱动容易导致无限制增长和能量耗散。论文旨在提出一种非线性自限幅（self-limited）方案，利用介质的非简谐谱失谐（anharmonic spectral detuning）来实现动态有界且低占有数的磁振子态，从而为低能耗波基信息处理奠定物理基础。

Method: 采用η算法，其中非绝热性参量（non-adiabaticity parameter）η量化参量驱动的强度，非线性频率调节器U代表介质非简谐谱失谐。以Co掺杂钇铁石榴石（YIG:Co）为代表性材料系统，在截断Fock基（truncated Fock bases）中进行数值验证，分析非线性失谐对参量增长的抑制作用，并讨论了磁阻尼（magnetic damping）、交换隙约束（exchange-gap confinement）和声子透明度（phonon transparency）对相干磁振子动力学维持的作用。

Result: 有限调节器U能够有效抑制向高阶模式的泄漏，在非绝热激发下保持有界动力学。实验报道的YIG:Co中超快开关的能量密度对应一个20×20×10 nm³单元的开关能量约为22 aJ，为低能共振态形成提供了物理相关的能量尺度。

Conclusion: 非线性自限幅非绝热动力学在铁氧体纳米结构中可能为低能耗波基信息处理提供物理基础。

Abstract: We propose a nonlinear magnonic platform for bounded non-adiabatic parametric excitation in nanoscale ferrite structures. The approach is based on the η-algorithm, where the non-adiabaticity parameter quantifies the strength of the parametric drive, while the nonlinear frequency regulator U represents the anharmonic spectral detuning of the medium. Using Co-doped yttrium iron garnet (YIG:Co) as a representative material system, we analyze how nonlinear detuning suppresses uncontrolled parametric growth and drives the system toward a dynamically localized low-occupancy magnonic state. Numerical verification in truncated Fock bases shows that a finite regulator U can suppress leakage into higher-order modes and preserve bounded dynamics under non-adiabatic excitation. The experimentally reported absorbed energy density for ultrafast switching in YIG:Co corresponds to an estimated switching energy of approximately 22 aJ for a 20x20x10 nm3 cell, providing a physically relevant scale for low-energy resonant state formation. We further discuss the role of magnetic damping, exchange-gap confinement, and phonon transparency in maintaining coherent magnonic dynamics over multiple operation cycles. These results suggest that nonlinear self-limited non-adiabatic dynamics in ferrite nanostructures may provide a physical basis for low-energy wave-based information processing.

</details>


### [106] [Tunable Phonon-Driven Magnon Spin Currents in Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19659)
*Sofie Helene Ursin,Mathias Kläui,Kjetil M. D. Hals*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从微观理论出发，推导了二维交替磁体（altermagnet）中由声子诱导产生的磁振子自旋流（magnon spin current），发现其具有d波对称性，且可通过调节声子频率实现自旋流方向完全逆转，表明交替磁体是实现可调谐太赫兹（terahertz）声子驱动磁振子自旋流的潜力平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交替磁体因其对称性调控的自旋电子学（spintronic）性质而受到广泛关注，但其声子-磁振子耦合体系中的自旋流行为尚不明确，本文旨在探索该机制。

Method: 从耦合磁振子-声子系统（coupled magnon-phonon system）的微观理论出发，推导了由选择性声子激发（selective phonon excitations）产生的非平衡磁振子分布（nonequilibrium magnon distribution）。

Result: 声子诱导的自旋流相对于声子动量（phonon momentum）呈现显著的d波对称性（d-wave symmetry）；沿交替磁方向的声子自旋流可通过调节声子频率（phonon frequency）实现完全反转。

Conclusion: 交替磁体为构建高度可调谐、声子驱动的相干太赫兹磁振子自旋流提供了有前景的材料平台。

Abstract: Altermagnets have recently attracted considerable interest due to their unique symmetry-governed spintronic properties. Here, we investigate phonon-induced magnon spin currents in a two-dimensional altermagnet. Starting from a microscopic theory of the coupled magnon-phonon system, we derive the nonequilibrium magnon distribution generated by selective phonon excitations. We show that the resulting spin currents exhibit a pronounced d-wave symmetry with respect to the phonon momentum. Moreover, the spin current along the altermagnetic directions can be completely reversed by tuning the phonon frequency. These findings establish altermagnets as promising platforms for realizing highly tunable, phonon-driven coherent terahertz magnon spin currents.

</details>


### [107] [An Energy Integration Free Kubo-Bastin Formula Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19670)
*Ousmane Ly*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种对 Kubo-Bastin 分解的重构（reformulation），通过解析积分替代数值能量积分，大幅降低了周期性系统中输运系数（transport coefficients）的计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kubo 公式（Kubo formulae）是现代自旋电子学（spintronics）和凝聚态物理（condensed matter physics）中研究线性响应（linear regime）输运性质的基础，但广泛使用的 Kubo-Bastin 分解（Kubo-Bastin decompositions）需要数值能量积分（numerical energy integration），计算成本较高。

Method: 针对通用周期性系统（generic periodic systems），对 Kubo-Bastin 分解中的能量积分进行解析积分（analytic integration），从而重新表述该分解方法。

Result: 新方法无需数值能量积分，显著降低了计算成本，并简化了输运系数的评估过程。

Conclusion: 该重构方法为周期性系统中输运系数的计算提供了一种更高效、更简洁的替代方案。

Abstract: Kubo formulae play a central role in modern spintronics and condensed matter physics, serving as the foundational ground for studying transport responses in the linear regime. In this work, we propose a reformulation of the widely used Kubo-Bastin decompositions that eliminates the need for numerical energy integration. By performing these integrations analytically for generic periodic systems, our approach drastically reduces computational cost and simplifies the evaluation of transport coefficients.

</details>


### [108] [Polar optical scattering in ellipsoidal nanoclusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19686)
*Hrach Nikoghosyan,Gor Nikoghosyan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了InAs/GaAs纳米团簇（呈高度扁平旋转椭球体形状）中三维约束（three-dimensional confinement）的具体几何结构对电子-振动耦合（electron-vibrational coupling）的影响，分析了光学声子弛豫过程及手性光学声子（chiral optical phonons）的发射条件，并讨论了零角动量LO声子发射导致的各向异性与非单调尺寸依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究特定三维约束几何（高度扁平旋转椭球体）对InAs/GaAs纳米团簇中电子-振动耦合的影响，以及该几何结构如何调制光学声子弛豫过程与角动量守恒行为。

Method: 基于角动量投影守恒定律（law of conservation of angular momentum projection）以及维度约束的空间对称性，对光学声子弛豫过程进行分析；同时分析携带轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum）的手性光学声子沿结构生长轴发射的条件。

Result: 发现零角动量LO声子发射的弛豫跃迁具有发射方向的特征各向异性（characteristic anisotropy），导致电子-声子耦合系数（e-ph coupling coefficient）呈现非单调（nonmonotonic）的尺寸依赖关系。

Conclusion: 三维约束的特定几何形状显著影响纳米团簇中电子-振动耦合行为，手性光学声子的发射条件与角动量守恒及空间对称性密切相关。

Abstract: The influence of the specific geometry of three-dimensional confinement on electron- vibrational coupling in InAs/GaAs nanoclusters shaped as highly oblate ellipsoids of revolution is considered. Optical phonon relaxation processes are analyzed taking into account the law of conservation of angular momentum projection and the spatial symmetry of the dimensional confinement. The conditions for the emission of chiral optical phonons carrying orbital angular momentum along the structure's growth axis are analyzed. Intraband relaxation transitions with the emission of LO phonons with zero angular momentum, with characteristic anisotropy of the emission direction, leading to nonmonotonic size dependences for the e-ph coupling coefficient, are considered.

</details>


### [109] [Twisted light generates robust many-body states for practical quantum computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19873)
*Ferney J. Rodriguez,Luis Quiroga,Neil F. Johnson*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出利用携带轨道角动量（OAM）的扭曲光（twisted light）实现量子点中多电子关联扇区的光学操控，提供了一种超越Kohn定理的量子计算控制机制，并在可解析求解的Calogero相互作用极限下给出了完整的门参数解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭曲光可以激发均匀偶极探针无法触及的受限相互作用电子暗态（"beyond-Kohn's-Theorem"光学通道），该研究旨在探索这一通道能否成为量子计算的具体控制基元，填补非均匀光学探针在量子点量子计算中的应用空白。

Method: 利用携带指定OAM指数和偏振的扭曲光脉冲，通过选择定则Δ|m|=±(l+σ)实现对少电子量子点中关联扇区（由相对角动量量子数表征）的光学写入、读取和可扩展寻址。在可解析求解的Calogero（1/r²）相互作用极限下，推导出能谱和扭曲光矩阵元的闭合表达式，由此显式给出Rabi频率、量子比特频率、非谐性和泄漏率等门参数。对于N=3体系，采用1/N展开方法进行半解析扩展，并识别出主要的退相干通道为四极电荷噪声（quadrupolar charge noise）。

Result: 关联扇区在对称性保护的选择规则和持久的手性光谱指纹意义上具有鲁棒性，三个及以上电子时具有完整的拓扑能隙保护。在Calogero极限下获得了门参数的解析形式，并将结果映射到通用单量子比特门集；提出了基于相邻量子点间状态依赖的库仑耦合实现两量子比特纠缠机制。识别了主导退相干机制为四极电荷噪声。

Conclusion: 扭曲光可以在统一的光子学控制层中实现写入（脉冲创建关联扇区）、读取（光谱诊断关联）和扩展（空间光调制器光学寻址）三种核心操作；屏蔽库仑相互作用与裸库仑相互作用均保持与可解析极限相同的定性手性光谱指纹特征。

Abstract: Twisted light carries orbital angular momentum (OAM) and can drive excitations of confined, interacting electrons that are dark to uniform dipolar probes. Here we show how this ``beyond-Kohn's-Theorem'' optical channel can become a concrete control primitive for quantum computing. Correlation sectors in few-electron quantum dots -- characterized by the relative angular momentum quantum number -- form a tunable ladder of many-body states that are robust in the limited sense of symmetry-protected selection rules and persistent chiral spectroscopic fingerprints; full topological gap protection requires three or more electrons. A twisted-light pulse with prescribed OAM index and polarization provides fast optical write, read, and scalable addressing of these sectors via the selection rule $Δ|m|=\pm(l+σ)$. In the analytically solvable Calogero ($1/r^2$) interaction limit, both the energy spectrum and the twisted-light matrix elements are closed-form functions of the interaction strength, allowing gate parameters (Rabi frequency, qubit frequency, anharmonicity, and leakage rates) to be written down explicitly. We map these results onto a universal single-qubit gate set, propose a concrete two-qubit entangling mechanism via state-dependent Coulomb coupling between adjacent dots, and identify the dominant decoherence channel (quadrupolar charge noise). A semi-analytic $N=3$ extension using the $1/N$ expansion provides a design-level scaffold for the topological roadmap, including quasihole sector addressing. The central operational message is that twisted light enables WRITE (pulse-create a correlation sector), READ (spectroscopically diagnose correlations), and SCALE (optical addressing via spatial light modulator) in a unified photonic control layer. Throughout, screened and Coulomb interactions preserve the same qualitative chiral fingerprints established in the solvable limit.

### [110] [Non-Hermitian thermoelectric transport in graphene: Tunable anomalous transmission through complex barriers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19907)
*Daniel A. Bonilla,Juan A. Cañas,J. C. Pérez-Pedraza,A. Martín-Ruiz*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 基于朗道散射框架，本文严格求解了有限复势垒下单层石墨烯（monolayer graphene）的狄拉克-外尔（Dirac-Weyl）问题，揭示了复势垒虚部使散射矩阵非幺正、导致规范破缺，并系统分析了虚部对电导、热导及热电优值（figure of merit）的调控作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索复势垒（complex barrier）能否在石墨烯中实现超出传统厄米 n-p-n 结的输运行为，并澄清虚部势在微观模型缺失时的有效描述意义。

Method: 在朗道散射框架（Landauer scattering framework）内精确求解二维单层石墨烯中带复数势垒的狄拉克-外尔方程，推导广义通量平衡关系，并计算线性响应系数及有限温度下的热电系数。

Result: 复势垒虚部使散射矩阵非幺正，通量守恒被广义平衡关系取代；特定共振通道被选择性地衰减或放大，改变角度响应和电导轮廓；电极分辨电导依赖于偏压分配，标志着有效两端响应中规范不变性（gauge invariance）的破缺；增益提升电导与热导，而损耗更有效地抑制热导，并在考察参数范围内获得最大热电优值。

Conclusion: 复势垒扩展了石墨烯输运行为的可及范围，其虚部可作为未解析源-漏通道或额外耦合探针的有效约化描述。

Abstract: We investigate thermoelectric transport in monolayer graphene across a finite complex barrier within a Landauer scattering framework. Solving the Dirac-Weyl problem exactly, we show that the imaginary part of the barrier renders the scattering matrix nonunitary and replaces the usual Hermitian flux conservation by a generalized flux-balance relation determined by the net gain or loss inside the barrier. In the Hermitian limit, the standard graphene $n$-$p$-$n$ barrier behavior is recovered, including perfect transmission at normal incidence and Fabry-Perot-type resonances. For a finite imaginary part, however, the same resonant channels are selectively attenuated or amplified, which significantly modifies both the angular response and the conductance profile. We further show that the lead-resolved conductances become dependent on the bias partition, providing a direct signature of the breakdown of gauge invariance in the effective two-terminal response. At finite temperature, the exact linear-response coefficients reveal a clear trade-off controlled by the imaginary part of the barrier: gain enhances both the electrical and thermal conductances, whereas loss suppresses the thermal conductance more efficiently and yields the largest thermoelectric figure of merit within the parameter range considered. These results demonstrate that complex barriers extend the range of transport behaviors accessible in graphene beyond the usual Hermitian $n$-$p$-$n$ junction. They also suggest a practical interpretation of the imaginary potential as an effective reduced description of unresolved source-sink channels or additional probes coupled to the device, particularly when a fully microscopic model of the environment is not available.

</details>


### [111] [Ellipticity effects on diffusive magnon spin and heat transport in easy-plane ferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19998)
*Nicolas Vidal-Silva,Alejandro O. Leon*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文基于Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert方程和玻尔兹曼输运方程，系统研究了易平面铁磁体中椭圆磁振子（elliptical magnons）的扩散输运行为，量化了椭圆率（ellipticity）对磁振子自旋导率和热导率的影响，并发现该效应在垂直于平面方向为易轴或难轴时分别表现为增强或减弱，而磁振子热输运在两种情况下均被增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当磁性材料中存在自旋波激发（磁振子，magnon）时，局域磁化可沿圆形或椭圆轨道旋转，椭圆轨道自然出现在存在垂直于平衡磁化方向的磁各向异性的情形中。本文旨在探究椭圆磁振子在易平面铁磁体中的扩散输运特性，以澄清椭圆率对磁振子输运性质的影响。

Method: 本文首先从具有垂直磁各向异性（perpendicular magnetic anisotropy）的Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert方程出发，推导磁振子色散关系（dispersion relation）和磁振子自旋（magnon spin）；随后采用弛豫时间近似（relaxation time approximation）下的玻尔兹曼输运方程（Boltzmann transport equation）并结合微扰分析（perturbation analysis），计算磁振子自旋导率（magnon-spin conductivity）和磁振子热导率（magnon thermal conductivity），从而量化绝缘体中的磁振子输运。

Result: 计算表明，在三维和二维系统中，椭圆率对磁振子输运系数的影响表现为：当垂直于平面方向的磁轴为易轴时输运增强，为难轴时输运减弱；而磁振子热输运在易轴和难轴两种磁系统中均呈现增强效应。

Conclusion: 本项研究支持了先前关于磁振子椭圆率的工作，并在阐明椭圆率对磁振子输运性质的影响方面迈出了重要一步。

Abstract: When a magnetic material hosts spin-wave excitations, or magnons, the local magnetization can rotate in circular or elliptical orbits, the latter arising naturally in the presence of magnetic anisotropies transverse to the equilibrium magnetization. This article investigates the diffusive transport of elliptical magnons in easy-plane ferromagnets. Our analysis starts with the derivation of the magnon dispersion relation and magnon spin from the Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert equation with a perpendicular magnetic anisotropy. Then, using the Boltzmann transport equation in the relaxation time approximation and perturbation analysis, the magnon-spin and magnon thermal conductivities are obtained, quantifying the magnon transport in the insulator. Our calculations demonstrate that, in both three- and two-dimensional systems, the effects of ellipticity on magnon transport coefficients result in an enhancement or a decrease, depending on whether magnets with a easy or hard perpendicular-to-plane axis are considered, respectively. On the other hand, our results predict an enhancement of the magnon heat transport for both easy- and hard-axis magnetic systems. Our study supports previous works on magnon ellipticity and makes a step towards clarifying its effect on magnon transport properties.

### [112] [Spectral and transmission properties of multiple correlated quantum dots made simple](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20083)
*Nahual Sobrino,Stefan Kurth*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文采用稳态密度泛函理论（i-DFT）计算与电子库耦合的一般相互作用纳米区域的谱学与透射特性，为不同相互作用和耦合几何构造了交换关联泛函，并通过从库仑阻塞到近藤区的多量子点应用展示了该方法捕捉量子相变等现象的能力，结果与多体方法高度一致但计算成本极低。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用稳态密度泛函理论（steady-state density functional theory），即 i-DFT，针对不同的相互作用方式和耦合几何结构构造了相应的交换关联泛函（exchange-correlation functionals）。

Result: 该方法成功应用于多种多量子点体系，覆盖从库仑阻塞（Coulomb blockade）到近藤（Kondo）区间的物理行为，并能够捕捉量子相变（quantum phase transitions）等复杂现象；计算结果与多体方法（many-body approaches）高度吻合。

Conclusion: i-DFT 能够在显著降低计算成本的前提下，达到与多体方法相当的计算精度，是一种具有潜力的高效计算框架。

Abstract: Steady-state density functional theory, called i-DFT, is employed to compute spectral and transmission properties of general interacting nanoscale regions coupled to electronic reservoirs. Exchange-correlation functionals are constructed for different interactions and coupling geometries. The potential of the method is illustrated by applications to various multiple quantum dots from the Coulomb blockade to the Kondo regime, capturing phenomena such as quantum phase transitions. The results are in excellent agreement with many-body approaches at a fraction of the computational cost.

### [113] [Probing tunable Kerr nonlinearity in graphene Josephson junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20155)
*Priyanka Samanta,Joydip Sarkar,Ashish Abhraham Samuel,Madhavi Chand,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Mandar M. Deshmukh*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文实验研究了石墨烯约瑟夫森结（graphene Josephson junction）中可调谐克尔非线性（Kerr nonlinearity）对栅极电压、温度和直流偏置的依赖关系，发现克尔系数可在300 kHz至1.2 MHz的宽范围内调谐，为下一代放大器和传感器设计提供了重要参考。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯约瑟夫森结（graphene Josephson junction）具有丰富的安德烈夫物理（Andreev physics）和优异的热学、磁场兼容性等优点，其核心非线性机制是克尔非线性（Kerr nonlinearity）。然而，关于石墨烯JJ中可调谐克尔非线性的详细研究此前从未开展。

Method: 本研究通过实验测量了石墨烯约瑟夫森结中克尔非线性（Kerr nonlinearity）对三个外部参数的依赖关系：栅极电压（gate voltage）、温度（temperature）和直流偏置（DC bias），其中直流偏置是此前较少被探索的调控手段。

Result: 通过调节上述参数，克尔系数（Kerr coefficient）的幅值在300 kHz至1.2 MHz的宽范围内实现了可调谐。

Conclusion: 该工作为深入理解石墨烯约瑟夫森结中的非线性机制提供了宝贵资源，并对设计具有增强性能的下一代放大器和传感器具有重要指导意义。

Abstract: Josephson junction (JJ) is a key nonlinear element in superconducting devices such as qubits, amplifiers, and bolometers. Recently, gate-tunable JJs based on graphene and semiconductors have gained interest due to their rich Andreev physics and wide applications in circuit quantum electrodynamics devices. In addition to gate tunability, it offers many advantages over conventional JJs, such as exceptional thermal properties for bolometric sensors, magnetic-field compatibility, and operability at elevated temperatures above 1 K. Like conventional Al-AlOx-Al JJs, graphene JJs also act as nonlinear inductors, and at their heart lies the Kerr nonlinearity. Additionally, in graphene JJs, the nonlinearity is tunable via external knobs in a single device. However, a detailed exploration of the tunable Kerr nonlinearity in graphene JJs has never been performed. In this work, we study the dependence of the Kerr nonlinearity on gate voltage, temperature, and DC bias - an interesting knob that has been less explored. Using these parameters, we show that the magnitude of the Kerr coefficient can be tuned over a wide range, from 300 kHz to 1.2 MHz. Our work will be a valuable resource for further understanding of the nonlinearity in graphene JJs and for the design of next-generation amplifiers and sensors, with enhanced performance.

### [114] [Scalar Field Reconstructions of Standard, Power Law and Logarithmic Holographic Dark Energy with a Gauss-Bonnet IR cut-off](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18934)
*Antonio Pasqua*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了以高斯-邦内特不变量（Gauss-Bonnet invariant）倒数平方根为红外截断的全息暗能量（Holographic Dark Energy, HDE）模型及其幂律和对数熵修正版本，推导了平坦与非平坦宇宙中、有无相互作用的态参数、减速参数及暗能量密度演化，并建立了与多种标量场模型的对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全息暗能量（HDE）模型是解释宇宙加速膨胀的重要候选理论，但标准HDE模型在红外截断（infrared cut-off）的选择上存在诸多可能性。本文旨在探索以高斯-邦内特不变量（Gauss-Bonnet invariant）为截断的新形式，并考察其熵修正版本在平坦与非平坦宇宙、有/无相互作用情形下的宇宙学行为。

Method: 采用红外截断$L=\mathcal{G}^{-1/4}$（其中$\mathcal{G}$为高斯-邦内特不变量），构建标准HDE、幂律熵修正HDE（Power Law entropy corrected HDE）和对数熵修正HDE（Logarithmic entropy corrected HDE）三类模型。基于此推导了态参数（Equation of State parameter, $\omega_D$）、减速参数（deceleration parameter, $q$）和暗能量密度分数演化形式$\Omega_D'$，分别针对平坦与非平坦宇宙（包含与不包含暗物质相互作用的情形），并分析暗能量主导时期的渐近行为。此外，建立了上述HDE模型与速子（tachyon）、k-本质（k-essence）、精质（quintessence）、广义恰普雷金气体（Generalized Chaplygin Gas, GCG）、杨-米尔斯（Yang-Mills）及非线性电动力学（Nonlinear Electrodynamics）等标量场模型之间的对应关系。

Result: 获得了三类HDE模型在平坦和非平坦宇宙中、有无暗物质相互作用时的态参数$\omega_D$、减速参数$q$以及暗能量密度分数演化形式$\Omega_D'$的解析表达式，并分析了暗能量主导时期的渐近行为。成功建立了所考虑HDE模型与多种标量场模型（速子、k-本质、精质、GCG、杨-米尔斯、非线性电动力学）之间的对应关系。

Conclusion: 以高斯-邦内特不变量倒数平方根为红外截断的HDE模型及其熵修正版本在宇宙学上具有自洽性，能够描述平坦与非平坦宇宙、有无相互作用下的暗能量演化，并且可以与多种标量场模型建立形式对应，表明该截断选择具有丰富的理论内涵和潜在的应用价值。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the Holographic Dark Energy (HDE) model and its entropy-corrected versions, namely the Power Law and Logarithmic entropy corrected HDE models, by considering the infrared cut-off $L=\mathcal{G}^{-1/4}$, where $\mathcal{G}$ is the Gauss-Bonnet invariant. We derived the Equation of State parameter $ω_D$, the deceleration parameter $q$ and the evolutionary form of the fractional energy density of DE $Ω_D'$ for flat and non-flat universes, with and without interaction between DE and Dark Matter. We also analyzed the asymptotic behavior in the DE dominated epoch. Furthermore, correspondences between the considered HDE models and several scalar field models, including tachyon, k-essence, quintessence, Generalized Chaplygin Gas, Yang-Mills, and Nonlinear Electrodynamics models, were established.

### [115] [Quasinormal modes of Proca and Maxwell fields in $d$-dimensional Schwarzschild-AdS black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18947)
*David C. Lopes,Tiago V. Fernandes,José P. S. Lemos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了d维Schwarzschild-AdS黑洞中Proca场和Maxwell场的线性扰动及其拟正则模（QNMs），通过解析推导与两种数值方法互补计算，重点分析了Proca质量、黑洞半径和时空维度对QNM谱的影响，并首次在大d≥5的Schwarzschild-AdS黑洞中数值发现标量型Maxwell扰动存在纯虚低频模式，该模式与AdS/CFT对偶中的线性化流体动力学 regime 相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究d维Schwarzschild-AdS黑洞背景下Proca场与Maxwell场的拟正则模（quasinormal modes, QNMs）谱，探讨Proca质量的效应以及AdS/CFT对偶（AdS/CFT correspondence）中流体动力学模式的对应关系。

Method: 将Proca场方程简化为一个解耦和两个耦合的径向波动方程；采用两种互补的数值方法专门处理渐近AdS时空；对于小黑洞，通过中间区域匹配渐近展开推导QNM频率的解析表达式。

Result: Maxwell方程可从Proca系统的零质量极限（zero-mass limit）恢复；在大d≥5的Schwarzschild-AdS黑洞中，标量型Maxwell扰动存在纯虚低频模式（purely imaginary low-frequency modes），类似于矢量型引力扰动；解析表达式与数值结果吻合良好。

Conclusion: Proca质量、黑洞半径和时空维度对QNM谱均有显著影响；纯虚低频标量型Maxwell模式在d≥5的大黑洞中存在，其在AdS/CFT框架下对标于对偶共形场论（conformal field theory）的线性化流体动力学 regime。

Abstract: Proca and Maxwell fields in $d$-dimensional Schwarzschild black holes with anti-de Sitter (AdS) asymptotics are investigated through their linear perturbations and associated quasinormal modes (QNMs) with Dirichlet boundary conditions at infinity. The Proca field equations reduce to one decoupled and two coupled radial wave-like equations. We demonstrate how the Maxwell equations emerge from the zero-mass limit of the Proca system. Several analytical properties of the corresponding QNM spectrum are examined. To compute the QNM frequencies, we employ two complementary numerical methods particularly suited to asymptotically AdS spacetimes. Using these techniques, we determine the QNMs modes of Proca field perturbations in $4$, $5$, $6$, and $7$-dimensional Schwarzschild-AdS backgrounds. As a new result, we find numerically that scalar-type Maxwell perturbations in large $d\geq 5$ Schwarzschild-AdS black holes exhibit purely imaginary low-frequency modes, analogous to those found in vector-type gravitational perturbations. The presence of such modes is especially relevant within the AdS/CFT correspondence, as they correspond to the linearized hydrodynamic regime in the dual conformal field theory. We also analyze the influence of the Proca mass on the QNM spectrum, also emphasizing how Maxwell modes are recovered in the massless limit. The dependence of the spectrum on the black hole radius is explored. In addition, analytic expressions for the QNM frequencies of vector-type and monopole Proca perturbations, as well as Maxwell modes, are derived for small $d$-dimensional Schwarzschild-AdS black holes by matching asymptotic expansions using an intermediate region. These analytic results show good agreement with the numerical findings, confirming, in particular, the existence of purely imaginary low-frequency scalar-type Maxwell modes in large $d\geq 5$ Schwarzschild-AdS spacetimes.

</details>


### [116] [Affine ANEC selects the closed FRW branch for geodesically complete cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18965)
*Nathan L. Burwig,Damien A. Easson*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究经典广义相对论中FRW宇宙的测地完备性、平均零能量条件（ANEC）和空间曲率之间的关系。证明在平坦或开放的FRW时空中，非静态模型无法同时满足零测地完备性和ANEC；而封闭（k=+1）几何中正曲率项可消除这一阻碍，支持存在满足ANEC的无奇点、测地完备的宇宙模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨在经典广义相对论框架下，FRW宇宙学中测地完备性（geodesic completeness）、平均零能量条件（averaged null energy condition, ANEC）与空间曲率（spatial curvature）之间的内在关系，并回答哪些曲率类型的FRW时空可以同时满足ANEC和零测地完备性。

Method: 沿径向零测地线（radial null geodesics）使用仿射参数化的ANEC（affinely parameterized ANEC），推导出包含空间曲率项的ANEC恒等式，并据此对不同曲率类型（平坦、开放、封闭）的非静态规则FRW时空进行分类分析。通过显式标量场构造（包括二次重建解析解和三次根重建闭式积分解）验证封闭模型的可实现性。

Result: 平坦（k=0）和开放（k=-1）的非静态规则FRW时空不能同时满足零测地完备性和ANEC。有界振荡或循环模型也无法避免这一阻碍，因其负的仿射ANEC体项（bulk term）在无限多个周期中累积至负无穷。封闭（k=+1）FRW几何中正曲率项在仿射ANEC恒等式中符号相反，可支持满足NEC（零能量条件）的、无奇点且测地完备的宇宙模型。在现有曲率约束下，正曲率对平坦模型重建中有效幻像态（effective phantom equation of state）的偏差仅为百分之一量级。

Conclusion: ANEC兼容的永恒FRW宇宙学存在曲率分类：平坦和开放分支受到测地不完备性阻碍，而封闭分支允许存在显式的完备实现，其中全局德西特时空（global de Sitter）作为真空极限代表出现。

Abstract: We study the relation between geodesic completeness, the averaged null energy condition (ANEC), and spatial curvature in Friedmann--Robertson--Walker (FRW) cosmology within classical general relativity. Using the affinely parameterized ANEC along radial null geodesics, we prove that non-static flat or open FRW spacetimes in the regular classes considered here cannot be both null geodesically complete and ANEC-satisfying. Bounded oscillatory or cyclic flat/open models do not circumvent the obstruction: the negative affine-ANEC bulk term accumulates over infinitely many cycles, giving \(I_{\rm ANEC}=-\infty\) for non-static periodic cases. Equivalently, within these classes, non-static ANEC-satisfying flat or open models are null incomplete. The sign obstruction is absent in closed \((k=+1)\) FRW geometry, where the positive curvature term enters the affine ANEC identity with the opposite sign and can support nonsingular, geodesically complete cosmologies with ordinary NEC-respecting matter. We give explicit closed-FRW scalar-field constructions, including a fully analytic quadratic reconstruction and a cubic-root reconstruction in closed quadrature, and contrast them with their flat realizations, which require NEC-violating support. Furthermore, we quantify how positive curvature can bias flat-model reconstructions toward an effective phantom equation of state, finding only a percent-level effect under current curvature bounds. The result is a curvature classification of ANEC-compatible eternal FRW cosmology: flat and open branches are obstructed, while the closed branch admits explicit complete realizations, with global de Sitter appearing as the vacuum limiting representative.

</details>


### [117] [Collective excitations in quantum gravity condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18977)
*Andrea Calcinari,Adrià Delhom,Daniele Oriti*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力中的一个核心开放问题是理解连续时空如何在无背景设定（background-independent setting）下从量子几何自由度中涌现出来。尽管群场论（group field theory）形式主义已明确实现了这一涌现图像，但平均场框架之外的量子涨落效应仍然在很大程度上未被探索。

Method: 将Bogolyubov理论（Bogolyubov theory）引入量子引力凝聚体（quantum gravity condensates），在群场论框架下构建一个可解模型，其中量子几何原子的凝聚体可复现非奇异的膨胀宇宙学，进而推导出超越平均场的领头阶修正。

Conclusion: 这些结果识别了一类新的量子引力激发，并在微观量子引力动力学、多体集体现象与时空涌现的可观测特征之间建立了受控的理论桥梁。

Abstract: A central open problem in quantum gravity is to understand how continuum spacetime emerges from quantum-geometric degrees of freedom in a background-independent setting. A many-body perspective suggests that spacetime emerges as a hydrodynamic phase of many atoms of quantum geometry. This idea underlies several approaches to quantum gravity, and it has been explicitly realised in the group field theory formalism. However, quantum fluctuations beyond the mean-field regime remain largely unexplored. We fill this gap by importing Bogolyubov theory to quantum gravity condensates, showing that leading beyond-mean-field effects manifest as collective excitations, in direct analogy with phonons in laboratory BECs. We implement the construction in a tractable group field theory model, where condensates of quantum-geometric atoms reproduce nonsingular expanding cosmologies, and derive the leading beyond-mean-field corrections to the emergent Friedmann dynamics. These results identify a new class of quantum-gravity excitations and establish a controlled bridge between microscopic quantum-gravitational dynamics, many-body collective phenomena, and signatures of spacetime emergence.

Here, the performance and results of the GstLAL real-time analysis are reported. The analysis is designed to identify candidates with low latency, high detection efficiency, and sustained operational uptime over long observing periods. During the run, the analysis contributed to 250 candidates classified as astrophysically plausible, provided the first upload for 222 of these, and was the sole contributor for 75. Among Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog events with a false-alarm rate below one per year, 88% were identified as significant in low latency and promoted for expert vetting and public dissemination.
