### [120] [Locality in effective field theory for inflationary soft modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19331)
*Takahiro Tanaka,Yuko Urakawa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过引入量子态的局域性条件（locality condition），统一了暴胀软模（soft modes）的有效描述、广义软定理（generalized soft theorem）、硬模（hard modes）圈修正的抑制以及红外正则性（infrared regularity）等关键问题，为梯度展开（gradient expansion）的有效性提供了模型无关的诊断标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在暴胀宇宙学中，梯度展开和分离宇宙方法是对软模进行有效描述的常用工具，但其适用范围及硬模圈修正何时会破坏该描述并不明确。本文旨在建立一种基于量子态局域性的统一判据，以模型无关的方式诊断硬模增强修正何时会使得梯度展开失效。

Method: 本文提出了一个关于量子态的局域性条件：要求每个局域宇宙中的硬模态仅通过同补丁内的局域软模值依赖于软模。在此条件下，粗粒化后的软模动力学保持局域性，且硬模对超视界关联函数（superhorizon correlators）的圈修正被微扰地抑制。同时，该局域性条件被证明可推导出广义软定理，并保证大规范变换（large gauge transformation）下不变算符的关联函数无红外发散。

Result: 局域性条件成立时，硬模圈修正被微扰抑制，从而保证了梯度展开的有效性。该条件还推出了广义软定理，在额外假设下可还原为标准的一致性关系（consistency relations）。此外，局域性条件确保了可观测关联函数的红外正则性。

Conclusion: 量子态的局域性条件为暴胀软模的有效描述、广义软定理、硬模圈修正的抑制以及可观测关联函数的红外正则性提供了统一判据。该公式阐明了在多场系统或非吸引子背景（non-attractor background）下可能出现偏离标准一致性关系的原因。

Abstract: The gradient expansion and the separate universe approach provide an effective description of inflationary soft modes after coarse-graining shorter-wavelength degrees of freedom. We formulate a locality condition on the quantum state, requiring that the hard-mode state in each local universe depend on the soft modes only through the local soft-mode values in the same patch. When this condition is satisfied, the coarse-grained soft-mode dynamics remains local, and loop corrections from hard modes to superhorizon correlators of the adiabatic curvature perturbation are perturbatively suppressed. This provides a model-independent diagnosis of when enhanced corrections due to hard modes can invalidate the gradient expansion. We further show that the same locality condition implies a generalized soft theorem, from which the standard consistency relations follow under additional assumptions. This formulation clarifies the origin of possible deviations from the standard consistency relations in multi-field systems or in a non-attractor background. We also show that the locality condition guarantees the absence of infrared divergences for the correlators of operators invariant under a large gauge transformation. Thus, locality of the hard-mode state provides a unified criterion for the effective description of inflationary soft modes, generalized soft theorems, the suppression of hard-mode loop corrections, and the infrared regularity of observable correlators.

### [121] [Timing-Window Mechanism for Chain-Like Transients in Collisions of Radially Excited Boson Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19572)
*Bo-Xuan Ge*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 径向激发玻色子星正碰撞中的链状瞬态过程由二元碰撞时间（binary collision time）主导，而非仅由径向激发决定。孤立的呼吸窗口（breathing windows）可作为参考时钟，数值相对论模拟表明，只有当碰撞时间与孤立呼吸时钟兼容时才会形成可见链。分离扫描（separation scan）通过偏移碰撞时间确认了该时间窗机制。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 选取自相互作用配置参数 \(n=2, \lambda=400\)，通过孤立演化定义呼吸窗口（breathing window）作为参考时钟；采用数值相对论模拟（numerical-relativity simulation）进行正碰撞实验，并实施分离扫描（separation scan）以调整碰撞时机。

Result: 可见链仅在碰撞时间与孤立呼吸时钟相容时出现；分离扫描通过将碰撞时间相对于同一时钟偏移，验证了时间窗机制（timing-window mechanism）的有效性。

Conclusion: 径向激发玻色子星碰撞中链状结构的产生并非由激发本身唯一决定，而是受到二元碰撞时间与孤立呼吸时钟匹配程度的控制，揭示了时间窗机制的核心作用。

Abstract: We show that chain-like transients in head-on collisions of radially excited boson stars are controlled by the binary collision time, not by radial excitation alone. For selected \(n=2\), \(λ=400\) self-interacting configurations, isolated evolutions define breathing windows that serve as reference clocks. Numerical-relativity simulations show that visible chains form only when the collision time is compatible with the isolated breathing clock. A separation scan shifts the collision time relative to the same clock, confirming the timing-window mechanism.

### [122] [Bessel-Hagen currents for the Fierz-Pauli action](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19719)
*Michael Hobson,Will Barker,Anthony Lasenby*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了Bessel-Hagen方法（最初用于电磁场构造规范不变的能量-动量张量）能否推广到无质量自旋-2场（Fierz-Pauli作用量）。研究发现，不存在严格规范不变的局域二次张量，但通过正确处理规范对称性的非精确性，可以在商空间中得到规范不变的诺特（Noether）流等价类，从而提供自旋-2版本的类比，但无法得到一个优先的局域规范不变能量-动量张量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bessel-Hagen方法在闵可夫斯基时空电磁学中能够直接导出规范不变的能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor），其关键在于用补偿的电磁规范变换（gauge transformation）补充坐标变换生成的形式变分。本文的核心动机是探究这一构造能否推广到由Fierz-Pauli作用量描述的无质量自旋-2场（massless spin-2 field）。

Method: 论文首先证明不存在非零的、由对称场h_{μν}一阶导数构成的局域二次张量（local quadratic tensor），能够在自旋-2规范变换下严格不变。随后，在正确对待Fierz-Pauli规范对称性的非精确性（inexact nature）后，应用Bessel-Hagen构造，通过改变补偿的自旋-2规范参数以及独立的自旋-2规范变换，分析诺特流（Noether current）的变化行为。

Result: 改变补偿规范参数只会引入正比于Fierz-Pauli场方程（field equations）的项；对h_{μν}施加独立的自旋-2规范变换，则只会引入一个由反对称超势（antisymmetric superpotential）散度加场方程项构成的平凡流（trivial current）。由此得到的是诺特流等价类（equivalence class）意义上的规范不变性，而非一个优先的局域规范不变能量-动量张量。

Conclusion: Bessel-Hagen构造可以推广到自旋-2场，但仅在守恒流（conserved currents）的商空间（quotient space）中成立，无法像电磁情形那样得到一个唯一的、局域的规范不变能量-动量张量。这是自旋-2场与电磁场之间的根本差异。

Abstract: For electromagnetism in Minkowski spacetime, the Bessel-Hagen method gives a particularly direct Noetherian derivation of the standard gauge-invariant energy-momentum tensor. The key step is to supplement the form variation generated by an infinitesimal coordinate transformation with a compensating electromagnetic gauge transformation. In this paper we ask whether the same idea can be applied to the massless spin-2 field described by the Fierz-Pauli action. We first prove that no nonzero local tensor quadratic in first derivatives of the symmetric field $h_{μν}$ can be strictly invariant under the spin-2 gauge transformation $h_{μν}\mapsto h_{μν}+\partial_μξ_ν+\partial_νξ_μ$; the direct electromagnetic analogue of the Bessel-Hagen construction therefore cannot exist. Once the inexact nature of the Fierz-Pauli gauge symmetry is treated correctly, however, the Bessel-Hagen construction does produce a gauge-invariant equivalence class of Noether currents. Changing the compensating spin-2 gauge parameter changes the current only by terms proportional to the Fierz-Pauli field equations; performing an independent spin-2 gauge transformation on $h_{μν}$ changes the current only by a trivial current given by the divergence of an antisymmetric superpotential plus field-equation terms. This provides the natural spin-2 analogue of Bessel-Hagen's electromagnetic construction, but only in the quotient space of conserved currents, and not as a preferred local gauge-invariant energy-momentum tensor.

</details>


### [123] [Neutron stars more compact than black holes in quasi-topological gravity: Equilibrium configurations and radial stability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19731)
*Liang Liang,Zhe Luo,Shoulong Li,Hongwei Yu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义相对论（general relativity）中，黑洞被视为宇宙中致密性的终极基准；然而，近期在高曲率理论——准拓扑引力（quasi-topological gravity, QTG）中构建的中子星模型显示出可以超越黑洞致密性极限，因此有必要对这一类构型的平衡结构与径向稳定性进行详细分析。

Method: 通过对多种代表性物态方程（equations of state）和不同引力耦合常数值进行系统分析，研究QTG中中子星的平衡结构及其径向稳定性。

Result: 在高中心密度（high-central-density）区域，超越黑洞极限的致密性在QTG中表现出普适行为；QTG修正随中心密度增大而显著增强，并能在广泛的参数范围内稳定那些在广义相对论中径向不稳定的构型。

Conclusion: QTG中的超致密中子星在理论上被确立为可行的强场构型，为进一步研究其动力学行为和现象学（phenomenological）意义提供了基础。

Abstract: Within general relativity, black holes are widely regarded as the ultimate benchmark for compactness in the Universe. Recently, however, neutron star models have been constructed in a higher-curvature theory -- quasi-topological gravity (QTG) -- whose compactness can exceed the black-hole limit~\cite{LD19666}. Here we present a detailed analysis of both the equilibrium structure and radial stability of such configurations in QTG. By examining several representative equations of state and different values of the gravitational coupling constant, we find that in the high-central-density regime the compactness exceeding the black-hole bound exhibits a universal behavior in QTG. We further show that QTG corrections grow increasingly significant at large central densities and can stabilize configurations that are radially unstable in general relativity over a broad parameter range. These results establish ultra-compact neutron stars in QTG as theoretically viable strong-field configurations and provide a foundation for further investigations of their dynamical and phenomenological implications.

</details>


### [124] [Non-singular Inflation-Dark Energy Unification Model Based on Loop Quantum Cosmology and Mass-Varying Neutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19791)
*Zhiming Shuai,Xiangdong Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在圈量子宇宙学（Loop Quantum Cosmology, LQC）的有效动力学框架下，结合质量可变中微子（Mass-Varying Neutrinos, MaVaNs）机制，构建了一个从量子反弹延续至今的非奇异精粹暴胀（quintessential inflation）宇宙学模型，并利用Ia型超新星、DESI重子声学振荡和CMB距离先验等观测数据对模型参数进行了严格约束，结果表明该统一框架与当前精密宇宙学观测高度一致。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于广义正则化方案（Generalized Regularization Scheme）下的圈量子宇宙学有效动力学，利用量子几何效应以量子反弹（quantum bounce）代替初始奇点；引入标量场（scalar field）与有质量中微子的耦合（MaVaNs机制），当中微子在暴胀后演化为非相对论性时，其反作用使标量场冻结，从而触发晚期加速膨胀；数值追踪从量子反弹至今的完整背景动力学（background dynamics）。

Conclusion: 所提出的非奇异常规暴胀模型能够在圈量子宇宙学框架下统一描述从量子反弹到晚期暗能量加速膨胀的完整宇宙演化，并且得到了多种观测数据的支持，为解决早期-晚期宇宙统一以及巧合问题（coincidence problem）提供了一条可行路径。

Abstract: Unifying the early-universe inflationary paradigm with late-time cosmic acceleration, while resolving the initial Big Bang singularity, remains one of the most profound challenges in modern cosmology. In this paper, we propose a non-singular quintessential inflation model embedded within the effective dynamics of Loop Quantum Cosmology (LQC) based on a Generalized Regularization Scheme. The quantum geometry effects naturally replace the initial singularity with a quantum bounce, followed by a phase of superinflation that sets robust initial conditions for the subsequent slow-roll inflation. To achieve a viable late-time dark energy epoch and address the coincidence problem, we introduce a coupling between the scalar field and massive neutrinos, known as Mass-Varying Neutrinos (MaVaNs). As neutrinos become non-relativistic in the post-inflationary evolution, their backreaction effectively freezes the scalar field, triggering the late-time accelerated expansion. We numerically trace the full background dynamics from the quantum bounce to the present day. Furthermore, we tightly constrain the model parameters utilizing the observational data, including the Type Ia supernovae sample, the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) Baryon Acoustic Oscillations (BAO) and Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) distance priors. Our results demonstrate that this unified LQC-MaVaNs quintessential framework is highly consistent with current precision cosmological observations.

Conclusion: 本文为评估引力辐射能量及其通量在宇宙学语境中的相关性提供了一致的理论基础（consistent theoretical basis）。

Abstract: The article deals with the role of gravitational radiation energy in the large-scale dynamics of the universe. Motivated by the observed accelerated expansion, we investigate whether gravitational energy, treated as a well-defined physical quantity within the teleparallel equivalent of general relativity, contributes to cosmological acceleration through its associated energy flux. Using radiative space-times described by the Bondi--Sachs framework, we analyze the total gravitational energy and the corresponding energy flux evaluated in asymptotic regions. Particular emphasis is placed on the cumulative character of gravitational radiation over long time scales and on the fact that gravitational energy in this formulation is not positively definite. The present analysis provides a consistent theoretical basis for assessing the relevance of gravitational radiation energy and its flux in cosmological contexts.

### [126] [A novel pre-inflationary model in view of the lack of angular correlation of CMB](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20076)
*M. Montes,José Edgar Madriz Aguilar,A. Bernal,Diego Allan Reyna*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用单标量场框架，构建从普朗克时间开始的暴胀前阶段（decelerated expansion）到暴胀阶段（accelerated inflationary regime）的统一演化；运用Mukhanov-Sasaki形式（Mukhanov-Sasaki formalism）处理标量场的量子涨落，并基于能量最小化（energy minimization）进行正则量子化（canonical quantization）。

Result: 真空态仅在暴胀起始时的亚视界模式（sub-horizon modes）上有明确定义，从而在原初功率谱（primordial power spectrum）中引入自然截断；所得谱在大尺度上受到抑制，在小尺度上保持近尺度不变性（nearly scale-invariant），并在适当极限下恢复标准的de Sitter结果。

Conclusion: 该模型可在一致暴胀框架内解释大尺度CMB异常，暴胀前动力学对大尺度结构具有重要影响，且结果与当前观测约束一致。

Abstract: In this paper we propose a novel unified cosmological model that connects a pre-inflationary epoch, starting at the Planckian time, with the onset of inflation within a single scalar-field framework. The pre-inflationary phase is characterized by a decelerated expansion with an increasing comoving Hubble horizon, followed by a gradually transition to an accelerated inflationary regime. This early dynamics leads to a modified causal structure that naturally accounts for the suppression of large-angle $(θ\gtrsim 60^\circ)$ correlations in the cosmic microwave background (CMB) reported by the satellite PLANCK. We study the quantum fluctuations of the scalar field using the Mukhanov-Sasaki formalism and a canonical quantization procedure based on energy minimization. We find that the vacuum state is well-defined only for sub-horizon modes at the onset of inflation, which induces a natural cutoff in the primordial power spectrum. The resulting spectrum exhibits a suppression at large scales while remaining nearly scale-invariant at small scales. In the appropriate limit, the model recovers the standard de Sitter result, in agreement with current observational constraints. These results highlight the relevance of pre-inflationary dynamics for addressing large-scale anomalies within a consistent inflationary framework.

### [127] [Vacuum, ma non troppo: hidden matter distribution in symmetry-transformed electrovacuum spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18967)
*Carlos A. R. Herdeiro,João P. A. Novo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将两类变换后的度规重新表达为Weyl形式（Weyl form），通过分析Weyl坐标下的度规结构识别其物质源（半无限环形质量分布），并比较原始Schwarzschild类坐标与Weyl坐标下赤道零测地线的行为差异。

Result: 两类度规在Weyl坐标下均表现为由赤道面上的半无限环形质量分布支撑，而非真正的真空解；在原始Schwarzschild类坐标中，赤道零测地线可在有限仿射参数（affine parameter）内到达空间无穷远（r→∞），而在Weyl坐标下这些测地线趋近环的内缘，坐标映射在此退化。

Conclusion: 这些度规并非真空解，而是隐藏了物质源，其坐标奇异性在Weyl表示中得以揭示；原始坐标下的无穷远行为对应于Weyl坐标下环内缘的坐标映射退化，需谨慎解释其物理意义。

Abstract: We analyse two static spacetimes, recently generated from a Schwarzschild--Bertotti--Robinson electrovacuum seed through distinct symmetry transformations. The electromagnetic field of the transformed solutions can be set to zero and both solutions were presented as vacuum solutions of General Relativity. However, we show that once recast in Weyl form, both metrics are seen to be supported by a semi-infinite annular mass distribution on the equatorial plane. Thus, these metrics harbour a hidden matter source, visible in Weyl coordinates. In the original Schwarzschild-like coordinates equatorial null geodesics reach spatial infinity ($r\to\infty$) in finite affine parameter. In the Weyl representation, these geodesics approach the inner edge of the annulus, where the coordinate map degenerates.

### [128] [Spin-Hair Induced Chaos of Spinning Test Particles in Rotating Hairy Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19673)
*Surojit Dalui,Xian-Hui Ge*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究旋转有毛黑洞（rotating hairy black hole）周围有质量自旋测试粒子的有限时间不稳定性，发现自旋-曲率耦合与毛发几何（hairy geometry）会改变轨道演化，且不稳定性在自旋与毛发径向轮廓协同作用的局部区域中出现，而非单调增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究引力退耦合（gravitational decoupling）生成的旋转有毛黑洞附近有质量自旋测试粒子的有限时间不稳定性，理解毛发参数如何影响强场区粒子动力学。

Method: 采用完整Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon方程与Tulczyjew自旋补充条件描述粒子运动，使用零角动量观测者（ZAMO）投影的有限时间Lyapunov分析测量对初值的敏感性，并扫描自旋S与径向毛发参数β构成的参数平面。

Result: 自旋-曲率耦合与毛发几何可使演化轨道偏离种子参数，小自旋与测地线轨迹接近规则行为，大自旋轨迹呈现更强的有限时间增长。不稳定性在(S,β)平面上呈局部化出现，而非单调增长，出现在粒子自旋与毛发径向轮廓协同作用的区域。

Conclusion: 有毛背景并非简单缩放克尔结果（Kerr result），而是重组了自旋粒子所采样的强场相空间区域。

Abstract: We investigate the finite-time instability of massive spinning test particles around a rotating hairy black hole generated through gravitational decoupling. The particle motion is described by the full Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon equations with the Tulczyjew spin supplementary condition, and the sensitivity to initial conditions is measured using a ZAMO-projected finite-time Lyapunov analysis. The hairy deformation is controlled by two parameters: $α$, which sets the deviation from Kerr, and $β$, which changes the radial localization of the deformation. We show that spin-curvature coupling and the hairy geometry can shift the evolved orbit away from the requested seed parameters, making the empirical orbital map essential for interpreting the dynamics. Small-spin and geodesic trajectories remain close to regular behavior, whereas large-spin trajectories show stronger finite-time growth. A scan of the $(S,β)$ plane shows that the instability does not grow monotonically, but appears in localized regions where the particle spin and the radial profile of the hair act cooperatively. Thus, the hairy background does not simply rescale the Kerr result; it reorganizes the strong-field phase-space region sampled by spinning particles.

### [129] [Bifurcation of the quasi-stationary velocity of strongly discrete transition waves driven by gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18926)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注弱离散过渡波在驱动力下的动力学，而强离散条件下过渡波可能展现出连续极限（continuum limit）无法预测的行为，亟需深入探究。

Method: 通过倾斜双稳态链（bistable chain），在动力学方程中引入重力微扰项（gravitational perturbation term），并分析强离散区间的过渡波动力学行为。

Result: 在强离散区间，重力驱动的过渡波展现出准静态速度平台，且平台数量随倾斜角增加先增多后减少；理论揭示该现象源于重力驱动与声子辐射的平衡，平衡点在辐射共振处发生分岔。

Conclusion: 该研究将过渡波的探讨拓展至强离散区间，多速度平台的发现为可编程孤波（programmable solitary waves）开辟了新可能。

Abstract: Transition waves are common in multistable mechanical metamaterials, and the dynamics of weakly discrete transition waves under driving forces have been extensively discussed. However, as lattice effects become more pronounced, strongly discrete transition waves may exhibit dynamics that cannot be predicted by the continuum limit. Here, by tilting a bistable chain, we introduce a gravitational perturbation term into the dynamical equations, under which the transition waves are continuously accelerated. In the strongly discrete regime, we find that transition waves under gravitational driving possess quasi-stationary velocity plateaus (QSVPs), and the number of these plateaus first increases and then decreases as the tilt angle increases. We theoretically elucidate that the emergence of the velocity plateaus originates from the balance between gravitational driving and phonon radiation. In further analysis, the theoretical model reveals that the balance point undergoes a bifurcation at the radiation resonance, which leads to a change in the number of velocity plateaus. Our study extends the investigation of transition waves into the strongly discrete regime, and the emergence of multiple velocity plateaus opens up new possibilities for programmable solitary waves.

### [130] [Top Pair Threshold Revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19546)
*Torbjörn Sjöstrand,Valery A. Khoze,Christian T. Preuss*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文复活并重新推导了35年前提出的非相对论性质格林函数形式（non-relativistic Green's function formalism），用于统一描述顶夸克对（ttbar）在阈值区域（threshold region）之上和之下的产生行为。改进后的形式更适合蒙特卡洛事件生成（Monte Carlo event generation），计算得到的阈值之下截面约为6.5 pb，与CMS和ATLAS合作组观测到的5–10 pb超出量相符，新代码已在Pythia事件生成器中公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CMS和ATLAS合作组最近在阈值区域发现了顶夸克对产生截面（ttbar cross section）意外偏大的证据，比连续微扰计算（continuum perturbative calculations）多出约5–10 pb，现有理论计算无法解释这一超出量，因此需要重新审视和改进旧有的理论形式。

Method: 采用非相对论性质格林函数形式（non-relativistic Green's function formalism）统一处理阈值之上和之下的顶夸克对产生行为；重新审视（revive and dissect）35年前的旧形式，并以更一致的形式重构，使其适用于蒙特卡洛事件生成（Monte Carlo event generation），并加入实用的规范化方案。

Result: 改进后的形式计算得到的阈值之下（below-threshold）截面约为6.5 pb，与CMS和ATLAS合作组观测到的5–10 pb超出量处于同一量级。新代码已集成到Pythia事件生成器中，可用于更详细的对比研究。

Conclusion: 非相对论性质格林函数形式能够有效地统一描述阈值区域之上和之下的顶夸克对产生，其计算出的截面与当前实验观测的超出量一致，表明该旧形式经过重构后仍适用于当前条件，并为理解这一异常信号提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Recently the CMS and ATLAS collaborations have found evidence for an unexpectedly large ttbar cross section in the threshold region, with an excess of the order of 5-10 pb relative to continuum perturbative calculations. A convenient approach to the theoretical study of this region, unifying the above- and below-threshold behaviour, is the non-relativistic Green's function formalism. It was first applied to top production more than 35 years ago, well before the discovery of the top. We therefore revive and dissect the old formalism, and put it back together in a more consistent form, suited for Monte Carlo event generation. Combined with some practical prescriptions, it can be applied to current conditions. As an example, the below-threshold cross section comes out to be of the order of 6.5 pb, i.e. comparable with the CMS and ATLAS numbers. The new code is publicly available in the Pythia event generator so can be used for more detailed comparisons.

### [131] [Lindblad-driven quarkonium production in heavy-ion collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19985)
*Néstor Armesto,Miguel Ángel Escobedo,Elena G. Ferreiro,Víctor López-Pardo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于林德布拉德方程（Lindblad equation）的开放量子系统框架，研究了极端相对论性重离子碰撞中传统夸克偶素（quarkonium）态的产生。从复值介质势出发，推导了各态的解离温度和热衰变宽度，计算了经历比约肯膨胀（Bjorken expansion）的系统中夸克偶素的存活概率；进一步将框架扩展至包含夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）中热化粲夸克和底夸克的重组过程，在绝热近似下从林德布拉德方程导出夸克偶素的聚变模型（coalescence model）。该方法提供了粲偶素（charmonium）和底偶素（bottomonium）抑制与重组过程的统一、基于第一性原理（first-principles-inspired）的描述。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在极端相对论性重离子碰撞中，夸克偶素（quarkonium）的产生涉及抑制（suppression）与重组（recombination）两个竞争过程，现有理论框架难以统一描述两者。本文旨在建立一个基于开放量子系统的统一理论框架，从第一性原理出发同时处理夸克偶素的解离与重组。

Method: 采用基于林德布拉德方程（Lindblad equation）的开放量子系统框架，从复值介质势（complex-valued in-medium potential）出发推导解离温度与热衰变宽度，计算比约肯膨胀（Bjorken expansion）下的存活概率；并在绝热近似（adiabatic approximation）下从林德布拉德方程导出一个包含热化重夸克重组的聚变模型（coalescence model）。

Result: 推导了各夸克偶素态的解离温度与热衰变宽度，计算了系统经历比约肯膨胀时的存活概率；并基于林德布拉德方程在绝热近似下推导出描述重组过程的聚变模型。

Conclusion: 该框架为粲偶素和底偶素的抑制与重组提供了一种统一的、源自第一性原理（first-principles-inspired）的描述方法。

Abstract: We study the production of the conventional quarkonium states in ultrarelativistic heavy-ion collisions using an open quantum system framework based on the Lindblad equation. Starting from the complex-valued in-medium potential, we derive the dissociation temperature and thermal decay width for each state, and compute their survival probabilities for a system undergoing Bjorken expansion. We then extend the framework to include recombination from thermalized charm and bottom quarks in the quark-gluon plasma, deriving a coalescence model for quarkonia from the Lindblad equation under the adiabatic approximation. The methodology provides a unified, first-principles-inspired description of suppression and recombination for both charmonium and bottomonium.

</details>


### [132] [Probing the Rare Four-Bottom Higgs Decay $H\to b\bar b b\bar b$ at the HL-LHC and ILC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19935)
*Alexander Belyaev,Eduard Boos,Vyacheslav Bunichev,Guliya Nurbakova,Saniya Rustembayeva*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出将稀有希格斯衰变过程 H→bbbb 作为探测希格斯与底夸克及规范玻色子相互作用结构的手段，并作为新物理搜索的基准。计算了主要贡献，包括主导的 H→bbg→bbbb 拓扑、可观的 H→ZZ*→bbbb 通道以及圈诱导的 H→gg→bbbb 贡献，发现分支比约为1.6×10⁻³，且主导振幅间的相消干涉在现象学上具有相关性。通过基于提升决策树的多变量分析，证明该衰变可在HL-LHC和ILC上被探测：在HL-LHC的pp→WH→Wbbbb过程中，3000 fb⁻¹下统计显著性约3.5；在ILC的e⁺e⁻→ZH→Zbbbb过程中，300 fb⁻¹下显著性即超过5σ，积分亮度达1-3 ab⁻¹时可将分支比测量至百分之几的精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提出稀有希格斯衰变 H→bbbb 作为探测希格斯与底夸克及规范玻色子相互作用结构的探针，并为涉及四底夸克末态的新物理搜索提供标准模型基线。

Method: 计算了该衰变的主要贡献，包括主导的 H→bbg→bbbb 拓扑、H→ZZ*→bbbb 通道以及圈诱导的 H→gg→bbbb 贡献；针对 HL-LHC 和 ILC 分别采用基于提升决策树（boosted decision trees, BDT）的多变量分析（multivariate analysis），利用四-b运动学观测量之间的关联。

Result: H→bbbb 的分支比约为 1.6×10⁻³，且主导振幅之间存在具有现象学相关性的相消干涉。在HL-LHC上，pp→WH→Wbbbb过程在3000 fb⁻¹下统计显著性约3.5，高纯度工作点的信噪比S/B≈5%，显著性接近3σ。在ILC上，e⁺e⁻→ZH→Zbbbb过程在300 fb⁻¹下多变量分析给出超过5σ的显著性，积分亮度达1-3 ab⁻¹时可将分支比测量至百分之几的精度。

Conclusion: 该稀有衰变可在高亮度LHC和ILC上被观测到；ILC由于其更洁净的对撞环境，能够以更高精度测量分支比。

Abstract: We propose the rare SM Higgs decay $H\to b\bar b b\bar b$ as a probe of the structure of Higgs interactions with bottom quarks and gauge bosons, and as a baseline for searches for new physics producing four-bottom final states in Higgs decays. We compute the leading contributions to this decay, including the dominant $H\to b\bar b g\to b\bar b b\bar b$ topology, the sizeable $H\to ZZ^\ast\to b\bar b b\bar b$ channel, and the loop-induced $H\to gg\to b\bar b b\bar b$ contribution. We find a branching ratio of order $1.6\times10^{-3}$ and show that destructive interference among the leading amplitudes is phenomenologically relevant.
  We demonstrate that this decay can be probed in associated Higgs production at both the HL-LHC and the ILC. For $pp\to WH\to Wb\bar b b\bar b$ at $\sqrt{s}=14$ TeV, we use a multivariate analysis based on boosted decision trees to exploit correlations among the four-$b$ kinematic observables. At $3000~{\rm fb}^{-1}$, the statistical significance reaches about $3.5$, while a tighter high-purity working point gives $S/B\simeq5\%$ with significance close to $3σ$. A combined high-luminosity LHC dataset could therefore make this rare decay observable.
  For $e^+e^-\to ZH\to Zb\bar b b\bar b$ at the ILC with $\sqrt{s}=250$ GeV, we demonstrate that the cleaner collider environment gives a high-purity signal sample. In the nominal setup, the multivariate analysis gives a significance above $5σ$ already at $300~{\rm fb}^{-1}$. At integrated luminosities of order $1-3~{\rm ab}^{-1}$, the branching ratio can be measured with several-percent precision.

### [133] [Non-Relativistic Cosmological Collider Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20102)
*Matheus C. Ferreira,F. T. Falciano*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种非相对论性的无助推宇宙对撞机（boostless cosmological collider）实现方案，在该方案中，暴胀相互作用由一个巨大的倾斜-鬼影规范场（massive tilted-ghost spectator field）介导。与非相对论性对撞机标准构造不同，本框架中的主导效应直接来源于规范场模式的传播，而非相互作用顶点。非相对论性修正使体函数（bulk mode functions）发生倾斜，从而改变in-in关联子并产生独特的对撞机信号。该结构的一个核心特征是涌现出一个类似化学势（chemical-potential-like）的有效参数，控制两个晚期振荡分支的相对权重。倾斜-鬼影模式表现出独特的动力学特征，与传统的化学势形变不同。研究表明，倾斜-鬼影场景提供了一个简单的有效框架，其中无助推对撞机现象学和类似化学势的分支不对称性自然源自非相对论性传播效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索无助推宇宙对撞机的一种新实现机制，其中主导信号来源于规范场模式的传播而非相互作用顶点，从而揭示非相对论性传播效应如何产生类似化学势的分支不对称性。

Method: 通过引入一个巨大的倾斜-鬼影规范场（massive tilted-ghost spectator field）作为暴胀相互作用的媒介，分析非相对论性修正对体函数（bulk mode functions）的变形效应，并采用in-in形式论计算关联子，考察挤压极限非高斯性（squeezed-limit non-Gaussianity）的结构特征。

Result: 非相对论性修正使体函数产生倾斜，从而修改in-in关联子并生成独特的对撞机信号；挤压极限非高斯性定性地再现了无助推宇宙对撞机信号的典型结构，但源于不同的动力学机制；涌现出一个类似化学势的有效参数，控制两个晚期振荡分支的相对权重；根据倾斜符号的不同，非高斯信号可被增强或抑制。

Conclusion: 倾斜-鬼影场景提供了一个简单的有效框架，其中无助推对撞机现象学和类似化学势的分支不对称性自然源自非相对论性传播效应，且该框架与传统的化学势形变具有不同的动力学特征。

Abstract: We investigate a non-relativistic realization of the boostless cosmological collider in a scenario where inflationary interactions are mediated by a massive tilted-ghost spectator field. Unlike standard boostless collider constructions, in which the characteristic non-Gaussian signatures are mainly generated by boost-breaking interaction vertices, the dominant effect in the present framework arises directly from the propagation of the spectator modes. Non-relativistic corrections deform the bulk mode functions, inducing a tilt that modifies the in-in correlators and generates a distinctive collider signal. The resulting squeezed-limit non-Gaussianity reproduces the qualitative structure of boostless cosmological-collider signals while originating from a fundamentally different dynamical mechanism. A central feature of the construction is the emergence of an effective chemical-potential-like parameter that controls the relative weight of the two late-time oscillatory branches. However, the tilted-ghost mode exhibits distinctive dynamical features and does not correspond to a conventional chemical-potential deformation. Depending on the sign of the tilt, the corresponding non-Gaussian signal can be either enhanced or suppressed. We show that the tilted-ghost scenario provides a simple effective framework in which boostless-collider phenomenology and chemical-potential-like branch asymmetries arise naturally from non-relativistic propagation effects.

</details>


### [134] [WIMP-like Dark Matter Without Thermalization At Freeze-Out](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20186)
*Dan Hooper,Gordan Krnjaic,Gabriele Montefalcone*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文论证隐藏 sector（hidden-sector）模型可以在暗物质（dark matter）与标准模型（Standard Model）于极高温度下解耦后，依然通过相似的温度演化实现与标准热遗迹（thermal relic）模型相当的湮灭截面（$\sigma v \sim 10^{-26}$ cm$^3$/s），从而得到观测到的遗迹密度（relic density）。这使得两 sector 之间的耦合可以极小，远超当前探测灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准热遗迹场景中，暗物质（dark matter）通过与标准模型（Standard Model）辐射浴保持化学平衡直至冻结（freeze-out），所需的湮灭截面（annihilation cross section）约为 $\sigma v \sim 10^{-26}$ cm$^3$/s。本文旨在探索是否可以在隐藏 sector（hidden-sector）模型中自然实现相近的截面，同时允许两 sector 在极高温下解耦并拥有独立热历史。

Method: 通过理论分析，考虑隐藏 sector（hidden-sector）模型：暗物质（dark matter）与标准模型（Standard Model）在极高温度 $T \gg m_X$ 时解耦，此后各自经历独立的热历史（separate thermal histories）。分析在此条件下两 sector 在冻结（freeze-out）时期的温度关系及其对遗迹密度（relic density）的影响。

Result: 尽管两 sector 在极高温下解耦，它们在冻结（freeze-out）时期仍具有相近的温度，使得湮灭截面（annihilation cross section）可达到与标准热遗迹（thermal relic）模型相当的 $σv \sim 10^{-26}$ cm$^3$/s，从而产生观测到的遗迹密度（relic density）。这允许标准模型与隐藏 sector（hidden-sector）之间的耦合极小，使直接探测（direct detection）和对撞机（collider）信号远低于可预见的灵敏度阈值。

Conclusion: 隐藏 sector（hidden-sector）模型能够自然地实现与标准热遗迹（thermal relic）场景相当的湮灭截面（annihilation cross section），从而符合观测的暗物质遗迹密度（relic density）。由于两 sector 间耦合可以极弱，传统直接探测（direct detection）和对撞机（collider）信号可能远低于未来可及灵敏度，对现有实验策略提出挑战。

Abstract: In the standard thermal relic scenario, dark matter remains in chemical equilibrium with the Standard Model radiation bath until freeze-out occurs at $T \sim m_X/20$, where $m_X$ is the dark matter mass. In this familiar class of models, the observed relic density is obtained for annihilation cross sections of order $σv \sim 10^{-26}$ cm$^3$/s. We show that comparable cross sections can naturally be realized in hidden-sector models in which the dark matter and Standard Model sectors decouple at a very high temperature, $T \gg m_X$, and subsequently evolve with separate thermal histories. Despite this decoupling, the two sectors have similar temperatures during freeze-out, leading to the usual thermal relic abundance. As a consequence, the coupling between the Standard Model and hidden sectors can be extremely small, potentially placing direct detection and collider signals far below foreseeable sensitivities.

</details>


### [135] [Spectral fringes without subcycles in Schwinger pair production and Dirac materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19086)
*I. A. Aleksandrov,M. A. Dorodnyi,E. D. Akimkina*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现即使在平滑、无载波的单瓣电场脉冲下，Schwinger 粒子对的产生谱中也能出现显著的干涉条纹，这一效应源于鞍点主导性转变（turning-point dominance transition）导致的亚主导轨迹干涉，并在固体Schwinger类似系统中得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为Schwinger对产生（Schwinger pair creation）中的光谱条纹（spectral fringes）源于结构化驱动（structured driving），如载波振荡、脉冲串或多产生事件。本文旨在检验这一固有认知，探究平滑单瓣脉冲是否也能产生类似的干涉条纹。

Method: 本文对比了两种在实时上几乎不可区分的高斯脉冲（Gaussian pulse）与弱变形脉冲的纵动量谱，分别在标量和旋量QED（scalar and spinor QED）中进行了精确数值求解，并结合半经典转折点分析（semiclassical turning-point analysis）追溯条纹来源。

Result: 在非绝热交叉区（nonadiabatic crossover），高斯脉冲谱保持平滑，而弱变形脉冲却在Keldysh参数（Keldysh parameter）趋近于1时产生强烈条纹。该效应由鞍点主导性转变（turning-point dominance transition）引起，即主导鞍点变得无关，亚主导鞍点（subleading contributions）产生干涉。同样的机制在固体Schwinger类似系统（solid-state Schwinger analog）——即SiC上外延石墨烯（epitaxial graphene on SiC）相关的有隙二维Dirac模型（gapped two-dimensional Dirac model）中也得到验证。

Conclusion: 光谱条纹的产生并不必然要求结构化驱动，平滑脉冲下鞍点主导性转变同样可诱导出显著条纹。文中还讨论了通过能量分辨泵浦-探测（energy-resolved pump-probe）方案观测这一预言调制的实验路径。

Abstract: Spectral fringes in Schwinger pair creation are usually attributed to structured driving, such as carrier oscillations, pulse trains, or multiple creation events. We show that pronounced fringes can arise even for smooth, carrier-free single-lobe electric-field pulses. Two bell-shaped profiles that are nearly indistinguishable in real time - a Gaussian pulse and a weakly deformed variant - produce qualitatively different longitudinal momentum spectra in the nonadiabatic crossover: the Gaussian spectrum remains smooth, whereas the deformed pulse develops strong fringes as the Keldysh parameter approaches unity. Exact numerical solutions in scalar and spinor QED agree with a semiclassical turning-point analysis and trace the effect to a turning-point dominance transition, where the leading saddle becomes irrelevant and subleading contributions interfere. We demonstrate the same mechanism in a solid-state Schwinger analog described by a gapped two-dimensional Dirac model relevant to epitaxial graphene on SiC, and discuss an energy-resolved pump-probe route to observing the predicted modulation.

</details>

### [136] [The linear Cahn-Hilliard equation with an interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20130)
*Andreas Chatziafratis,Alain Miranville,Tohru Ozawa*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文利用Fokas统一变换方法（unified transform method）首次针对四阶算子，获得了线性化Cahn-Hilliard方程在全非齐次界面问题下的新积分表示解，该解以复傅里叶平面上的围道积分形式表达，适用于任意初始数据和一般界面条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cahn-Hilliard型模型在应用数学中广泛出现，涉及数学物理、连续介质力学、化学和生物学中的多种现象。本文旨在为线性化Cahn-Hilliard方程的全非齐次界面问题提供新的显式积分表示，以服务于解的正则性、渐近行为分析以及非线性情形适定性和自由边界问题的研究。

Method: 采用Fokas统一变换方法（unified transform method），并首次将其实现于四阶算子情形。通过将问题转化为复傅里叶平面（complex Fourier plane）上的围道积分（contour integral）表示，处理了非齐次项、任意初始数据和原点处的一般界面条件带来的挑战。

Result: 获得了线性化Cahn-Hilliard方程在全非齐次界面问题下的新的积分表示，其形式为复傅里叶平面上的围道积分表达式。该显式公式可直接用于分析解的正则性（regularity）和渐近行为（asymptotic behavior）。

Conclusion: 所得显式解公式为探索解的定性性质提供了直接工具，并对非线性Cahn-Hilliard方程的适定性（well-posedness）研究以及自由边界问题（free-boundary problem）和扩散界面问题（diffuse-interface problem）具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: We obtain new integral representations, expressed as contour integrals in the complex Fourier plane, for the solution of fully nonhomogeneous interface problems for the linearized Cahn-Hilliard equation with arbitrary initial data on the line and general interface conditions prescribed at the origin. Cahn-Hilliard-type models emerge in applied mathematics in connection to a spectacular variety of phenomena of mathematical physics, continuum mechanics, chemistry and biology. A novel implementation of Fokas' unified transform method is in force herein for a fourth-order operator for the first time, with particular challenges arising due to the nature and the generality of the problems under consideration. Our explicit formulae directly lend themselves to exploration of the solution's qualitative properties such as regularity and asymptotic behavior. This work is also useful in the investigation of well-posedness for nonlinear counterparts as well as in the study of free-boundary and diffuse-interface problems.

### [137] [Detecting vortex motion through spatially correlated nonequilibrium noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18941)
*Yifan F. Zhang,Rhine Samajdar,Sarang Gopalakrishnan*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出利用协方差磁力测量（covariance magnetometry）技术，通过探测超导薄膜上方磁性噪声（magnetic noise）的空间各向异性，来区分电阻输运（resistive transport）源于准粒子（quasiparticle）运动还是涡旋（vortex）运动。该方法的核心在于：施加电流后，普通载流子平行于电流漂移，而涡旋因马格努斯力（Magnus force）垂直于电流漂移，由此产生可被噪声协方差检测到的各向异性信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导相附近的电阻输运既可源于正常态准粒子的运动，也可源于涡旋的运动，但仅凭电导率（conductivity）无法区分这两种机制。因此需要一种无歧义的实验方法来鉴别输运的微观起源。

Method: 利用基于金刚石氮-空位中心（nitrogen-vacancy centers）的协方差磁力测量技术，实时探测样品上方磁性噪声的时空关联（spatiotemporal correlations）。通过分析施加电流后噪声协方差的空间各向异性（anisotropy）来区分输运机制：普通载流子沿电流方向漂移，而涡旋因马格努斯力垂直于电流漂移。

Result: 计算了代表性薄膜超导体上预期的噪声关联，结果表明各向异性信号在现有实验能力可达到的测量范围内。

Conclusion: 协方差磁力测量能够通过磁性噪声的各向异性指纹有效识别涡旋驱动的输运，为区分超导电阻输运机制提供了一种无歧义的实验工具。

Abstract: Resistive transport near a superconducting phase can arise from the motion of normal-state quasiparticles or that of vortices. The conductivity alone does not distinguish between these mechanisms. We propose an unambiguous method for telling them apart, using the recently developed experimental tool of covariance magnetometry, which uses nitrogen-vacancy centers in diamond to probe real-time spatiotemporal correlations in magnetic noise. Our key insight is that, under an applied current, the underlying charge carriers leave a directional fingerprint in the spatially correlated magnetic noise above the sample: ordinary electric carriers drift parallel to the current, whereas vortices, owing to the Magnus force, drift perpendicular to it. The noise covariance detects this anisotropy and identifies the vortex-driven nature of transport. We compute the noise correlations expected for a representative thin-film superconductor and demonstrate that the anisotropic signal is well within the reach of current experimental capabilities.

</details>


### [138] [Signatures of Gaussian superconducting fluctuations in nonlocal noise magnetometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18970)
*Dror Orgad*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用含时金兹堡-朗道理论（time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory）计算了由高斯超导涨落（Gaussian superconducting fluctuations）产生的两点磁噪声谱（two-point magnetic noise spectrum），该量可直接通过自旋量子比特对（如金刚石中的氮-空位中心）测量，并对比了涡旋液体（vortex liquid）的预期信号，以探索高温超导体中涨落的本质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁噪声谱是自旋量子比特对可直接测量的物理量，但此前由超导涨落贡献的磁噪声尚未被系统计算。本文旨在填补这一空白，并为区分不同涨落机制（如高斯涨落与涡旋液体）提供理论依据。

Method: 采用含时金兹堡-朗道理论（time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory）描述涨落库珀对（fluctuating Cooper pairs）对电流关联函数（current correlations）的直接贡献，从而计算磁噪声谱。研究对象包括二维系统和纳米线（wires），并分别考虑平衡态和均匀电场（uniform electric field）下的情形。

Result: 信号在高温超导体（high-temperature superconductors）中最强；二维系统与纳米线在不同条件下的磁噪声谱特征被给出。

Conclusion: 通过与涡旋液体（vortex liquid）的预期信号进行对比，本文提供了一条额外途径来阐明高温超导体中涨落的本质；磁噪声测量有望成为区分不同超导涨落机制的有效实验手段。

Abstract: We calculate the two-point magnetic noise spectrum arising from Gaussian superconducting fluctuations, a quantity directly measurable by spin qubit pairs such as nitrogen vacancy centers in diamond. The analysis utilizes the time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory, reflecting the direct contribution of fluctuating Cooper pairs to the current correlations and consequent magnetic noise. We treat both two-dimensional systems and wires, considering them in equilibrium and under a uniform electric field. The signal is expected to be strongest in high-temperature superconductors, and we contrast our findings with the predicted signatures of a vortex liquid to offer an additional route to elucidate the nature of fluctuations in these systems.

</details>


### [139] [Nearly perfect Fermi surface nesting in hole-doped La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ enables bulk superconductivity without pressure or strain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19297)
*Chengliang Xia,Jiale Chen,Hongquan Liu,Hanghui Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算发现，在环境压力下，空穴掺杂可诱导层状镍氧化物La₃Ni₂O₇中Ni-d_{3z²-r²}衍生的γ费米口袋从圆形演变为菱形，并在掺杂浓度x≈0.4时实现近乎完美的费米面嵌套（Fermi surface nesting），从而显著增强反铁磁自旋涨落（antiferromagnetic spin fluctuations）并提升超导本征值至实验可观测水平，为无需压力或应变的环境压力体超导电性提供了机制与实验路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ruddlesden-Popper镍氧化物（Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates）的高温超导电性已在高压体样品或压缩应变薄膜中被发现，但环境压力下的真正体超导电性（bulk superconductivity）尚未实现，这阻碍了比热（specific heat）和超流密度（superfluid density）等关键测量。因此，寻找环境压力下体超导的实现机制与可行方案是本研究的主要动机。

Method: 本研究结合密度泛函理论（density-functional-theory, DFT）、动力学平均场理论（dynamical-mean-field-theory, DMFT）和随机相位近似（random-phase-approximation, RPA），求解环境压力下空穴掺杂双层镍氧化物La₃₋ₓSrₓNi₂O₇体材料的超导能隙方程（superconducting gap equation）。

Result: 研究发现，空穴掺杂在费米面上诱导出一个由Ni-d_{3z²-r²}轨道衍生的γ费米口袋，掺杂浓度x既是该口袋大小的调谐参数，也是其形状的调谐参数。当x接近0.4时，γ口袋从圆形变为菱形，并扩展至覆盖半个布里渊区（Brillouin zone），产生以最优嵌套矢量Q=(π, π)为核心的近乎完美的费米面嵌套，从而强烈增强反铁磁自旋涨落，显著提升超导主导本征值（leading superconducting eigenvalue）至实验可观测水平。

Conclusion: 本研究为在La₃Ni₂O₇中无需压力或应变即可实现长期追寻的环境压力体超导电性提供了一种稳健的微观机制（robust mechanism）和一条实验上可行的路线。

Abstract: The discovery of high-temperature superconductivity in Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates has drawn great attention. However, unlike cuprates and iron-based superconductors, Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates exhibit superconductivity either under high pressure in bulk samples or under compressive strain in thin films. Genuine bulk superconductivity under ambient pressure has remained elusive in these materials, precluding key measurements such as specific heat and superfluid density. In this work, we combine density-functional-theory, dynamical-mean-field-theory, and random-phase-approximation to solve the superconducting gap equation for bulk hole-doped bilayer nickelate La$_{3-x}$Sr$_x$Ni$_2$O$_7$ at ambient pressure. We find that hole doping induces a Ni-$d_{3z^2-r^2}$-derived $γ$ pocket on the Fermi surface, and serves as a tuning parameter for both its size and \textit{shape}. As $x$ approaches 0.4, the $γ$ pocket evolves from circular to diamond-shaped and expands to span half of the Brillouin zone, resulting in nearly perfect Fermi surface nesting with the optimal nesting vector $\textbf{Q} = (π, π)$. This, in turn, strongly enhances antiferromagnetic spin fluctuations and substantially increases the leading superconducting eigenvalue to a level at which superconductivity becomes experimentally observable. Our work provides both a robust mechanism and an experimentally feasible route to inducing the long-sought bulk superconductivity in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ without pressure or strain.

</details>


### [140] [The Ultrafast Superconducting Diode Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19675)
*E. Wang,M. Chavez-Cervantes,J. Satapathy,T. Matsuyama,G. Meier,X. Zhang,L. You,F. Marijanovic,J. B. Curtis,E. Demler,A. Cavalleri*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文报道了在中心反演对称超导体（centrosymmetric superconductors）中发现的超快非互易输运（ultrafast non-reciprocal transport）现象。利用准直流超电流偏置的NbN薄膜，皮秒级电流脉冲根据其极性分别表现出电阻性或电感性响应，该效应速度比传统超导二极管快至少三个数量级，并实现了100 GHz信号的整流，能耗仅为每周期几个fJ。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超导非互易输运依赖于涡旋（vortex）的不对称运动，但涡旋输运本质上是耗散且受速度限制的，这阻碍了超导电子学向更快、更低功耗的方向发展。因此，需要探索一种新型、超快且低耗散的非互易输运机制。

Method: 研究采用中心反演对称的NbN薄膜作为实验体系，通过施加准直流超电流（quasi-DC supercurrent）进行偏置，然后注入皮秒级电流脉冲，测量其对不同极性脉冲的电阻性与电感性响应差异。

Result: 与偏置电流同极性的皮秒脉冲经历电阻性阻抗（resistive impedance），而相反极性的脉冲则表现出感应性响应（inductive response）。该非互易效应的速度比传统超导二极管快至少三个数量级，仅受限于超快电流诱导的退配对（current-induced depairing）。该系统实现了100 GHz信号的整流，每个周期的能耗仅为几个fJ。

Conclusion: 该发现预示着未来可能实现基于超导的逻辑元件（superconducting logic elements），其工作频率可达太赫兹（THz）比特率，每次操作能耗仅为aJ（attojoule）量级，为超高速、超低功耗超导电子学开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Nonreciprocal transport is generally observed in superconductors in which time reversal and inversion symmetries are simultaneously broken. This effect, which may become one of the backbones for future superconducting electronics, arises because of asymmetric vortex transport in a magnetic field. However, vortex transport is also intrinsically dissipative and limited in speed. Here, we report on the discovery of ultrafast non-reciprocal transport in centrosymmetric superconductors. For NbN films biased with a quasi-DC supercurrent, picosecond current pulses with the same sign as the bias experience resistive impedance, whereas pulses of opposite polarity encounter an inductive response. Strikingly, the effect is at least three orders of magnitude faster than in conventional superconducting diodes, limited only by ultrafast current-induced depairing. We demonstrate rectification of a 100 GHz signal, with dissipation levels of a few fJ per cycle. We foresee potential for superconducting logic elements, operating at THz bit rates with aJ energy dissipation per operation.

</details>


### [141] [Secondary Collective Excitations in Intermediate to Strong-Coupling Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20059)
*Joshua Althüser,Götz S. Uhrig*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用迭代运动方程（iEoM）方法，研究了由能量转移依赖的有效电子-电子相互作用在中等至强耦合各向同性超导体中诱发的次级相位模与振幅模，发现这些次级集体激发存在于连续谱下方，且其行为几乎独立于晶格类型和费米能级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在中等至强耦合（intermediate-to-strong-coupling）超导体中，系统导出的能量转移依赖的有效电子-电子相互作用如何导致次级相位模与振幅模的出现，并分析这些模式在不同晶格和耦合强度下的行为。

Method: 采用迭代运动方程（iterated equations of motion，iEoM）方法计算响应函数，并扩展到本征算符（eigenoperator）的计算，以识别激发各次级模式的特定线性组合。

Result: 弱耦合下在 ω=2Δ 和 ω=0 处分别观察到常规的初级振幅模和相位模；中等耦合时振幅模向低能方向脱离准粒子连续谱；进一步增大耦合导致连续谱下方出现长寿命次级集体激发；若系统不具备粒子-空穴对称性（particle-hole symmetry），振幅模与相位模会耦合；次级模式的本征算符系数呈现类似氢原子波函数的节点结构。

Conclusion: 次级集体激发现象在很大程度上独立于晶格结构和具体费米能级（Fermi level），表明该机制在中等至强耦合超导体中具有普适性。

Abstract: Considering systematically derived energy-transfer-dependent effective electron-electron interactions leads to the appearance of secondary phase and amplitude modes in isotropic superconductors in the intermediate-to-strong-coupling regime. We study the implications of such interactions on Bravais lattices by computing the corresponding response functions using the iterated equations of motion (iEoM) approach. In the weak-coupling regime, we find the conventional, primary amplitude and phase modes at $ω=2Δ$ and $ω=0$, respectively. For intermediate coupling, the amplitude mode detaches from the quasiparticle continuum towards lower energies. Increasing the coupling further leads to additional, long-lived secondary collective excitations below the continuum. This phenomenon is largely independent of the underlying lattice and the specific Fermi level. The amplitude and phase modes couple if the system is not particle-hole symmetric. Additionally, we extend the method to compute eigenoperators, i.e., linear combinations of operators that excite each secondary mode specifically. We identify nodal structures in the coefficients for these eigenoperators reminiscent of wave functions in the Hydrogen problem.

### [143] [After the Fluid: Subexponential Decay in AdS$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18978)
*John R. V. Crump,Jorge E. Santos*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究施瓦西-反德西特四维黑洞膜（Schwarzschild-AdS$_4$ black branes）非线性扰动的晚期行为，发现实解析初始数据会进入由准正规模式（quasinormal mode）谱大$k$尾部主导的区域，导出了边界观测量的拉伸指数衰减律（stretched-exponential decay）$\exp(-c\, t^{5/6})$，并通过完全非线性数值演化加以验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解黑洞膜非线性扰动的晚期行为，揭示实解析初始数据下边界观测量衰减的普适规律，并验证该规律是否源于几何光学（geometric-optics）而非流体动力学模式。

Method: 利用平面AdS$_4$黑洞膜的准正规模式谱渐近标度$\mathrm{Im}\,ω_{k\,n} \sim k^{-1/5}$进行理论推导；采用傅里叶谱方法（Fourier spectral method）和间断伽辽金方法（discontinuous Galerkin method）进行完全非线性数值演化。

Result: 理论预言边界观测量以拉伸指数形式衰减$\exp(-c\, t^{5/6})$（含轻微多项式前因子）；数值结果对小黑洞完全证实该行为，对较大黑洞在压制长寿命低$k$模式后显示一致标度。

Conclusion: 指数$5/6$的拉伸指数衰减是AdS$_4$引力动力学中实解析数据的稳健特征，源于几何光学物理而非流体动力学模式。

Abstract: We study the late-time behaviour of nonlinear perturbations of Schwarzschild-AdS$_4$ black branes and show that real-analytic initial data generically enter a regime controlled by the large-$k$ tail of the quasinormal mode spectrum $\{ω_{k\,n}\}$. Using the asymptotic scaling $\mathrm{Im}\,ω_{k\,n} \sim k^{-1/5}$ of the planar AdS$_4$ black brane, we derive a universal prediction that boundary observables decay in a stretched-exponential manner, specifically as $\exp(-c\, t^{5/6})$ up to a mild polynomial prefactor. Fully nonlinear numerical evolutions employing Fourier spectral and discontinuous Galerkin methods confirm this behaviour for small black holes and show consistent scaling - after suppressing long-lived low-$k$ modes - for larger ones. These results indicate that stretched-exponential decay with exponent $5/6$ is a robust feature of AdS$_4$ gravitational dynamics with real-analytic data, arising from geometric-optics physics rather than hydrodynamic modes.

### [144] [Uniqueness of D=8 minimal supergravity with two vector multiplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19002)
*Guillaume Bossard,Bingxin Lao,Ruben Minasian*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于对偶性假设和一致性条件，严格约束了八维最小超引力耦合两个矢量多重态时的受保护耦合，并发现Bianchi恒等式不允许存在引力贡献，最终在BPS扇区中确定了一个唯一的自洽理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知八维中存在四种具有最小超对称性（minimal supersymmetry）的弦理论（string theory），其低能有效描述由最小超引力（minimal supergravity）耦合不同数量的矢量多重态（vector multiplets）给出，但这些理论的耦合形式尚未被唯一确定。本文旨在通过自洽性条件（如反常抵消、高维提升和规范增强点）来严格约束并唯一确定这些受保护耦合（protected couplings）。

Method: 假设理论具有形式为 Γ₀(N)×Γ₀(N) ⊂ SL(2,ℤ)×SL(2,ℤ) 的对偶性对称性（duality symmetry），利用反常抵消（anomaly cancellation）、高维提升（higher-dimensional uplifts）以及规范增强点（gauge enhancement loci）等一致性条件，系统地分析最小超引力耦合两个矢量多重态时的受保护耦合。

Result: 一致性条件强烈限制了允许的耦合，并在BPS扇区（BPS sector）中隔离出一个唯一的自洽理论。特别地，研究发现三形式通量（three-form flux）的Bianchi恒等式（Bianchi identity）不能包含引力贡献（gravitational contributions）。

Conclusion: 通过一致性条件可以唯一确定八维最小超引力耦合两个矢量多重态时的受保护耦合，这为理解仅有的四种八维最小超对称弦理论提供了更精确的低能有效描述。

Abstract: There exist only four known string theories with minimal supersymmetry in eight dimensions, whose low energy effective descriptions are given by minimal supergravity coupled to $l=18$, $10$, or $2$ vector multiplets. It has been argued that these numbers are uniquely fixed by consistency conditions of the effective theory. In this work, we investigate the protected couplings of minimal supergravity coupled to two vector multiplets under the assumption that the theory admits a duality symmetry of the form $Γ_0(N)\times Γ_0(N)\subset {\rm SL}(2,\mathbb{Z}) \times {\rm SL}(2,\mathbb{Z})$ for some positive integer $N$. We show that consistency with anomaly cancellation, higher-dimensional uplifts, and gauge enhancement loci strongly constrains the allowed couplings and isolates a unique consistent theory in the BPS sector. In particular, we find that the Bianchi identity for the three-form flux cannot have gravitational contributions.

Abstract: Our recent result on the construction of perfect fluid equations with N=1,2 Schrödinger supersymmetry [Mod. Phys. Lett. Two cases are considered in detail, which include the N=2 conformal Newton-Hooke superalgebra and N=1 l-conformal Galilei superalgebra with arbitrary half-integer parameter l. Supersymmetric fluid models are built within the Hamiltonian framework by introducing real (for N=1) or complex (for N=2) anticommuting field variables as superpartners for the density and velocity. For both the cases the full set of conserved charges associated with the superalgebras is constructed and the Lagrangian description is given. ### [146] [Microcanonical Energy Sharing and a Page-like Curve for the Capacity of Entanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19725)
*Raul Arias*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究微正则系综（microcanonical ensemble）下可加二分系统的纠缠容量（capacity of entanglement），证明在热力学极限下该容量由能量共享涨落控制，并可通过子系统的标准热响应数据表达。通过将Schwarzian黑洞扇区与二维CFT辐射扇区耦合的简化模型，展示了固定总能量下随辐射扇区增长产生的Page-like单峰曲线，为Page曲线提供了一种热力学微正则机制。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用典型性（typicality）和微正则约化态的块结构（block structure），在热力学极限（thermodynamic regime）下将纠缠容量表示为能量共享涨落的函数，并用子系统的标准热响应数据（standard thermal response data）加以表达。

Result: 推导出纠缠容量在热力学极限下可由能量共享涨落和子系统热响应数据直接计算；在Schwarzian黑洞与二维CFT耦合的玩具模型中，固定总能量下随着辐射扇区增长，共同温度下降，纠缠容量呈现平滑的Page-like单峰曲线。

Conclusion: 本文建立的微正则纠缠容量公式提供了一种产生Page-like容量曲线的热力学微正则机制，为纠缠熵的Page曲线现象补充了不依赖具体动力学过程的统计力学视角。

Abstract: We study the capacity of entanglement in the microcanonical ensemble for an effectively additive bipartite system. Using typicality and the block structure of the microcanonical reduced state, we show that in the thermodynamic regime the capacity is controlled by energy-sharing fluctuations and can be expressed purely in terms of standard thermal response data of the subsystems. As an illustration, we apply the result to a toy model consisting of a Schwarzian ``black-hole'' sector coupled to a two-dimensional CFT radiation sector. At fixed total energy, the growth of the radiation sector forces the common temperature to decrease, producing a smooth Page-like single-hump curve for the capacity. The construction is meant as a thermodynamic microcanonical mechanism for Page-like capacity curves, rather than as a complete dynamical evaporation calculation.

</details>


### [147] [Iterative Solution of the Kerr Black Hole Metric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19948)
*Poul H. Damgaard,Hojin Lee,Kanghoon Lee,Tabasum Rahnuma*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用爱因斯坦方程的递归解，对Kerr黑洞度规进行了双参数（牛顿常数G和Kerr自旋参数a）微扰展开，并在谐和规范下求解至高阶，最终通过引入冗余项将级数重求合为闭式谐和规范度规，同时详细讨论了傅里叶变换的维度正则化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对Kerr黑洞度规进行微扰展开，并构建一个在谐和规范（harmonic gauge）下收敛的闭式度规表达式，同时解决双参数微扰理论中的规范冗余与维度正则化（dimensional regularization）问题。

Method: 采用爱因斯坦方程的递归解（recursive solution）；度规作为牛顿常数G和Kerr自旋参数a的函数，构成双参数微扰展开（double expansion）；在谐和规范下求解递归关系到任意高阶；通过引入冗余项（对应坐标谐和函数的加入）将级数重求合（re-sum）为闭式谐和规范度规；并详细阐述了傅里叶变换的维度正则化处理。

Result: 成功在谐和规范下对Kerr黑洞度规实现了双参数微扰展开到任意高阶，并完成了从级数到闭式谐和规范度规的重求合；同时清晰解释了傅里叶变换维度正则化的相关技术细节。

Conclusion: 双参数微扰展开结合递归解法能够有效处理Kerr黑洞度规的谐和规范构造，但需注意引入冗余项才能完成闭式求和；维度正则化在傅里叶变换处理中起着关键作用。

Abstract: Using a recursive solution of the Einstein equations, we consider the perturbative expansion of the metric corresponding to a Kerr black hole. Because the metric is a function of two parameters, Newton's constant G and the Kerr spin parameter a, the perturbation theory naturally becomes a double expansion. In harmonic gauge the recursion relations can be solved to arbitrarily high orders in these two expansion parameters but to re-sum the series into the closed-form harmonic gauge metric requires the introduction of terms that are redundant and correspond to the addition of harmonic functions to the coordinates. Issues related to dimensional regularization of Fourier transforms are explained in detail.

</details>


### [148] [Kerroll black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15269)
*Florian Ecker,Daniel Grumiller,Lucas Hörl,Mattéo Leturcq--Daligaux,Alfredo Pérez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过两种方法构造了卡罗尔引力（Carroll gravity）中的旋转黑洞：一种是利用卡罗尔相容联络的自由度编码旋转，直接构建了内在卡罗尔性质的旋转解；另一种是从广义相对论在光速奇次幂展开中构建扩展理论，得到了卡罗尔版本的克尔黑洞（Kerroll black hole），并计算了两种理论相应的守恒荷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索卡罗尔引力中旋转黑洞的解是否存在及其构造方式，尤其是寻找其与广义相对论中经典克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）对应的卡罗尔类比。

Method: 第一种方法利用卡罗尔相容联络（Carroll compatible connection）中的自由度来编码旋转，通过为卡罗尔-史瓦西黑洞（Carroll-Schwarzschild black hole）添加旋转荷来构造；第二种方法从广义相对论在光速的奇次幂展开（odd-power expansion in the speed of light）中构建磁卡罗尔引力（magnetic Carroll gravity）的扩展理论。

Result: 第一种方法构造的解是内在卡罗尔性质的，不存在洛伦兹对应物；第二种方法证明扩展理论中存在卡罗尔版本的克尔黑洞（Kerroll black hole），其旋转表现为卡罗尔数据中的奇次幂效应。两种理论的保守荷均被计算。

Conclusion: 卡罗尔引力中存在两种不同构造途径的旋转黑洞解，其中一种是从广义相对论的奇次幂展开自然产生的，为理解超光速极限下的引力现象提供了新视角。

Abstract: We construct rotating black holes in Carroll gravity using two distinct approaches. In one of them, we exploit the freedom in the Carroll compatible connection to encode rotation. In particular, we construct rotating solutions in magnetic Carroll gravity by dressing the Carroll-Schwarzschild black hole with a rotational charge. This solution is intrinsically Carrollian and has no Lorentzian analog. In the other approach, we construct an extension of magnetic Carroll gravity from general relativity in an odd-power expansion in the speed of light. This theory contains magnetic Carroll gravity as a subsector but has in general more physical degrees of freedom. We show that this theory admits a Carroll analog of the Kerr black hole as a solution, which we refer to as the "Kerroll black hole". Its rotation appears as an intrinsically odd-power effect in the Carroll data. We compute the corresponding conserved charges for both theories.

</details>


### [149] [Covariant unification of holographic c-functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18942)
*Niko Jokela,Jani Kastikainen,Carlos Nunez,José Manuel Penín,Helime Ruotsalainen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种协变的全息c-函数（covariant holographic c-function），直接定义在自上而下（top-down）背景中，由余二维切片的外曲率（extrinsic curvature）构造，无需依赖特定坐标系或一致维数约化，并在多种弦论背景中验证了其单调性行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全息c-函数（holographic c-function）基于叶状结构（foliation）定义，依赖特定坐标选择或存在一致维数约化，缺乏推广至复杂背景（如内部空间与全息径向方向混合的流形）的协变形式。本文旨在提出一种不依赖这些限制的协变定义，以统一并推广现有方案。

Method: 定义一种协变全息c-函数，直接利用体几何（bulk geometry）中余二维切片的外曲率构造，不依赖于特殊坐标或一致维数约化。该定义在适当极限下可退化为基于叶状结构的现有全息c-函数。方法在多种自上而下弦论背景中进行了显式计算，包括共形模型、禁闭几何、跨维流以及Klebanov-Murugan几何。

Result: 在共形模型中，c-函数在AdS不动点之间单调插值；在禁闭几何中，c-函数在红外能隙区域单调下降至零；在Klebanov-Murugan几何中，恢复了正确的不动点值并观察到单调性证据。这表明协变定义在复杂背景中仍保持预期的全息c-函数行为。

Conclusion: 本文提出的协变全息c-函数统一了现有定义并拓展至更通用的背景。但仍存在未解决的概念问题，包括：在存在非平凡内部流形时缺乏全息径向方向的普适协变定义；如何从体作用量推导流方程；以及与纠缠熵c-函数（entanglement c-function）的关系。

Abstract: We propose a covariant holographic c-function, defined directly in a top-down background and constructed from the extrinsic curvature of codimension-two slices of the bulk geometry. The definition does not rely on a special choice of coordinates or on the existence of a consistent dimensional reduction. We show that it unifies previous foliation-based holographic c-functions into a single covariant formula, reducing to them in the appropriate limits. We evaluate the covariant expression in a range of top-down string backgrounds, including conformal models, confining geometries, flows across dimensions, and the Klebanov-Murugan geometry, in which the holographic radial direction mixes with internal coordinates and which is not the uplift of a lower-dimensional solution. In all cases, the c-function behaves as expected: it interpolates monotonically between AdS fixed points when they are present and decreases towards zero in gapped infrared regions, while in the Klebanov-Murugan case we recover the correct fixed-point values and find evidence for monotonicity. We highlight open conceptual issues, including: the lack of a universal covariant definition of the holographic radial direction in the presence of a nontrivial internal manifold; the derivation of the flow from a bulk action; and the relation to the entanglement c-function.

</details>


### [150] [Modave lectures on energy conditions in quantum field theory and semi-classical gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18964)
*Jackson R. Fliss*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文综述了经典能量条件及其在引力解（包括奇点定理）中的作用，然后探讨了量子场论中能量条件的违反及相应的非局域约束（如时空平均与能量-量子信息界限），并讨论了这些界限对有效引力理论及量子引力理论的启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典能量条件在爱因斯坦引力中具有核心地位，是推导 Hawking 与 Penrose 奇点定理的基础；然而量子场论（quantum field theory）中即使最简单的模型也会违反局域能量条件，使得经典能量条件在量子引力（quantum gravity）背景下失效，因此需要寻找更一般的约束框架。

Method: 以综述形式回顾经典能量条件及其在广义相对论中的应用，随后转向量子引力领域，讨论通过时空区域平均（averaging over regions of spacetime）以及能量与量子信息（quantum information）之间的界限来约束量子场论中的能量密度。

Result: 量子场论必然违反局部能量条件，但通过非局域平均与信息-能量界限可以恢复有意义的约束；这些界限在有效场论（effective theory）框架内对引力耦合系统具有直接限制作用，并进一步为理解量子引力提供了方向性指导。

Conclusion: 经典能量条件在量子引力中不再成立，但存在基于非局域性和量子信息理论的替代性约束；这些新约束有助于构建量子场论与引力耦合的有效理论，并为探索量子引力提供了概念性工具。

Abstract: We review well known classical energy conditions and their implications for gravitational solutions, including the celebrated Hawking and Penrose singularity theorems. We then consider quantum fields coupled to gravity, where the topic becomes both richer and more subtle, as even the simplest quantum theories violate local energy conditions. We discuss directions for constraining energy densities in quantum field theories, including averaging over regions of spacetime and bounds relating energy and quantum information. We explore implications of these bounds for quantum field theory coupled to gravity as an effective theory and discuss how they guide our understanding of quantum gravity more broadly. These notes are based on a series of lectures given at the XXI Modave Summer School in Mathematical Sciences.

</details>


### [151] [Spin Hall effect and Berry curvature of gravitons from quantum field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19817)
*Ritsuki Ito,Kazuya Mameda,Naoki Yamamoto*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文基于线性化引力的量子场论，为左、右手征引力子（graviton）构建了Wigner函数；通过对爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量导出的引力子能动量张量中的二阶度规扰动（metric perturbation）实施Wigner变换，展示了弯曲时空中引力子的自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect）。该效应源于引力子的贝里曲率（Berry curvature），对左右手征具有相反的符号，并导致与手征相关的引力子能量霍尔电流（energy Hall current）分裂，其分裂幅度恰好为对应光子自旋霍尔电流的两倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索引力子在弯曲时空中的自旋依赖输运行为，特别是引力子是否像光子一样表现出自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect），以及该效应与光子自旋霍尔效应之间的定量关系。

Method: 基于线性化引力的量子场论（quantum field theory of linearized gravity），定义左、右手征引力子的Wigner函数；对从爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量（Einstein-Hilbert action）导出的引力子能动量张量中二阶度规扰动项施加Wigner变换（Wigner transformation）。

Result: 发现引力子在弯曲时空中存在自旋霍尔效应，其根源在于引力子的贝里曲率（Berry curvature）对左右手征具有相反符号；该效应导致手征依赖的引力子能量霍尔电流（energy Hall current）发生分裂，且分裂幅度恰好为对应光子自旋霍尔电流的两倍。

Conclusion: 引力子在弯曲时空中确实表现出自旋霍尔效应，且其手征分裂幅度较光子的对应效应更强，揭示了引力子与光子在自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）行为上的定量差异。

Abstract: Based on quantum field theory of linearized gravity, we formulate the Wigner function for right- and left-handed gravitons. By applying the Wigner transformation to the second-order metric perturbations in the graviton energy-momentum tensor obtained from the Einstein-Hilbert action, we demonstrate the emergence of the spin Hall effect of gravitons in curved spacetime. This effect originates from the Berry curvature of gravitons, which has opposite signs for right- and left-handed helicities, and leads to a helicity-dependent splitting of the graviton energy Hall current. The magnitude of this splitting is found to be exactly twice that of the corresponding spin Hall current for photons.

</details>


### [152] [Approaching the surface of an Exotic Compact Object](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20013)
*Shokoufe Faraji,Samir D. Mathur*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文论证了奇异致密天体（ECO）表面附近的真空爱因斯坦方程会导致混沌度规，其振荡幅度随接近表面而增大。该行为类似于宇宙学中大爆炸附近的BKL“宇宙台球”现象，但其中部分势壁变号成为“悬崖”，引发紧致方向收缩至零的失控行为。在弦论中，这种收缩自然演化为毛球（fuzzball）的内部几何结构，紧致方向坍缩产生磁单极子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力（quantum gravity）的许多方法需要用奇异致密天体（Exotic Compact Object, ECO）替代传统黑洞几何，该天体表面具有大但非无限的红移。研究旨在厘清ECO表面附近度规的真实行为及其物理后果。

Method: 通过分析ECO表面附近的真空爱因斯坦方程（vacuum Einstein equations），揭示度规的混沌特性及振荡行为；将这一行为类比于宇宙学中大爆炸附近的BKL（Belinsky-Khalatnikov-Lifshitz）分析中的“宇宙台球”（cosmic billiards）模型，并指出其中势壁变号形成“悬崖”（cliffs）导致方向收缩的失控行为。

Result: ECO表面附近的度规呈现混沌性，振荡幅度随接近表面而剧烈增大。部分“台球”势壁变号成为“悬崖”，引发某些紧致方向（compact directions）被挤压至零大小的失控行为。

Conclusion: 在弦论（string theory）框架下，这种紧致方向的收缩自然延续为毛球（fuzzball）的内部几何结构，其中紧致方向坍缩产生磁单极子（monopoles），从而为ECO内部几何提供了自洽的弦论解释。

Abstract: Many approaches to quantum gravity require replacing the traditional black hole geometry with an Exotic Compact Object (ECO), which has a large but not infinite redshift at its surface. We argue that near the ECO surface, the vacuum Einstein equations imply a metric that is chaotic, with increasingly large oscillations as we approach the surface. This behavior is analogous to the `cosmic billiards' found in the BKL analysis of cosmology near the big bang. For the ECO, some of the potential walls of this billiards change sign to become `cliffs', resulting in a runaway behavior where some compact directions squeeze to zero size. In string theory such squeezing yields a natural continuation to the interior geometry of fuzzballs, where compact directions collapse to create monopoles.

</details>


### [153] [Stringy T-duality on the lattice and the twisted Villain model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19925)
*Coraline Bacq,Alessio Caddeo,Saskia Demulder,Johanna Erdmenger*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个晶格（lattice）框架，证明弯曲背景下的T-对偶性（T-duality）能够在有限晶格间距下精确实现，而非仅作为红外极限下的涌现现象。通过定义扭曲Villain模型（twisted Villain model），将纤维场与上链耦合，并利用半规范（half-gauging）过程构造拓扑缺陷（topological defect），展示了该对偶性的全局拓扑特征可被晶格模型精确捕获。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续场论中表述的对偶性（duality）是否能够在有限晶格间距下精确实现，而不仅仅是作为红外极限下的近似现象，这是一个尚未解决的问题。本文旨在从晶格正则化（lattice regularization）的角度，验证T-对偶性在弯曲背景下的非平庸拓扑特征能否被精确刻画。

Method: 作者将紧致玻色子（compact boson）的精确晶格T-对偶性推广到具有非平凡圆纤维化（circle fibration）的弯曲背景。为此，定义了扭曲Villain模型，将晶格纤维场与描述丛联络（bundle connection）和B场纤维水平分量的上链（cochains）耦合。通过半规范过程推导了相应的晶格缺陷作用量（lattice defect action），并证明该作用量定义了一个拓扑缺陷。

Result: 在多个纤维化背景的晶格模型中，恢复了T-对偶性特有的丛-通量交换（bundle-flux exchange）特征。半规范导出的晶格缺陷作用量被证明是拓扑缺陷，表明弯曲流形上T-对偶性的独特拓扑特征可在晶格模型中精确实现。

Conclusion: 弯曲背景下的T-对偶性并非依赖于特定连续表示的涌现现象，而是可以在晶格正则化模型中精确存在。这意味着该对偶性在离散晶格层级上即可被完整捕获。

Abstract: We address the question of whether dualities formulated in continuum field theory can be realised exactly at finite lattice spacing, rather than only emerging in the infrared. In this context, we construct a lattice framework for a genuinely stringy form of T-duality. We extend the exact lattice T-duality of the compact boson to curved backgrounds with non-trivial circle fibrations, where the duality is no longer exhausted by the familiar exchange of momentum and winding, but also involves global topological data. To this end, we define the twisted Villain model, which couples the lattice fibre field to cochains encoding the bundle connection and the fibre-horizontal component of the $B$-field. We realise this structure in lattice models for several fibred backgrounds and recover the characteristic bundle-flux exchange of T-duality. Using a half-gauging procedure, we derive the associated lattice defect action and show that it defines a topological defect. This establishes that the distinctive topological features of T-duality on curved manifolds can be captured exactly in a lattice model, implying that this duality is not tied to a particular continuum representation is present in lattice-regularised models.

</details>
